# الحمد للہ رب العلمین
*Source: KASHKOLE, Binder 34 (Quranic Studies), Chapter 164. 11 topics. Language: ur.*

<!-- section 1 (id=5719, raw_sort=1): DRAFT -->

## Section 5719

### Gift - Hadiya

Now lets talk about the word انعمت . The word anamta comes from the word نعمۃ  which means gift. Now what are the two greatest gifts Allah has given all human being from a physical and spiritual sense? It is the heart and the intellect. allah gave these 2 gifts to all human beings. Now what was the purpose of these gifts?

The purpose of these gifts. Was that human beings would use their intellect and their heart to come to the conclusion that there is in fact an Allah. Who is glorious. Who is magnificent. For whom gratitude and praise must be made. He is intensely an extremely loving and caring. And that there has to be a Judgment Day where a balance will be created between life on this earth and the afterlife. So these three realizations would lead human beings to the conclusion that we want to give ourselves up as slaves to Allah. And once we do that we need his guidance. So these are the conclusions that a person is supposed to reach using the two gifts that Allah gave him. The heart and the intellect. This is the conclusion that every human being is supposed to reach all by himself using the two initial gifts that Allah gave him. Because he is supposed to reflect on the creation of this universe using these two gifts as Allah says.

إِنَّ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ وَٱخْتِلَفِ ٱلَّيْلِ وَٱلنَّهَارِ لَآيَتٍۢ لِّأُو۟لِى ٱلْأَلْبَبِ

No doubt about it. Especially when it comes to the creation of the heavens and the earth. And especially when it comes to the fight between night and day. The conflict that takes place between night and day there are signs for the people of intellect.

What are these conflicts that Allah is talking about? Today is a bright and night is dark. As the day progresses the daylight starts winning over the darkness. And then as the day ends. The darkness starts winning over the night. The sun goes from being bright yellow to orange. And the sky goes from being bright blue to dark blue until it becomes completely black. And night finally wins.

‏وَٱلَّيْلِ وَمَا وَسَقَ

I swear by the night and whatever it encompasses

and then that full black night starts losing its battle with the day. And what happens? The sky starts getting brighter and brighter and brighter. Until it's daylight again and all traces of the night has been eliminated. And this battle keeps happening every single day.

Allah says especially when it comes to the creation of the heavens and the earth. And especially when it comes to the battle between the night in the day. In these two things. There are many many miraculous signs. For people who have pure minds.اولو الاباب . people of sound minds.

Let's begin by first understanding what your minds mean. what does uloo albaab mean. Who are these people of pure and sound minds? Because if we are not people of pure and sound minds. Then there are really no miraculous signs for us in the creation of heavens and earth. And there is no miraculous sign for us in the conflict between night and day. Because these things are observed by everyone in the world. But does everyone see the miraculous signs in them? No they don't why's that! ?

Because they do not meet the requirement of this ayah. Because they do not have sound minds.

⟪ar-quote:الُّب عَقلُ صَالحٌ ؛ خالصٌ من الشَّوائب⟫

A clean mind is one that is not polluted by useless things that is the definition of the word Lubb. A person whose thoughts are not polluted by useless things. A person who actually thinks about meaningful things. This mind that Allah gave us is actually a very powerful gift. It is extremely capable. You can actually memorize entire books. You can store incredible amounts of data. There are people. That when they put their minds to something. They become extremely knowledgeable in the area on which they focused. For example if you tune in to ESPN. There are commentators that can tell you sports statistics. From 50 years ago. All off the top of their heads. They know the names of athletes. How long their career lasted. What teams they played for. Which college they went to. What year they were drafted. Who drafted them. How many rings they have. When they suffered injuries. When they were reinstated. My God! That is incredible! These people put their minds to it. And they were able to store incredible amounts of data.

There are young kids. 12/13 years old. They start playing a videogame. And they can memorize every single complicated move for that game. The start playing a first-person shooter and they can tell you all the cheat codes. All the walk-throughs. And they can just tell you all of that from the top of their head. There are people that get obsessed with TV shows. There are people that get obsessed with fashion. There are some people that get obsessed with news. Some people get obsessed with technology. Which chip just came out. Which processor is being developed. For the year  2080. Some people get obsessed with cars. Aren't there people like that? This mind is an incredible thing. When you put your mind to something you can actually do amazing things.

Now this may be good stuff to know from the worldly perspective. You can get a certain kind of a job based on this information. But in line with our ultimate goal. Is this useful knowledge? Is this something that is going to help us in the afterlife? It's not!

Now Allah is telling us in this verse. That there are people in this world that put their mind to all this kind of stuff. But then there are very few people that instead of getting distracted with one thing. Instead of taking this extremely powerful mind and use all of this muscle to put this into some useless thing. Like sports statistics or videogame data. Instead of using their mind on these useless things they focus on things which you and I would not even consider. They stop and think about the skies the earth and how they were actually created. And they start thinking about how there is a natural conflict between night and day.

We have become accustomed to exhausting our minds in useless things. So let's talk about what happens when somebody starts thinking about the heavens and the earth. And starts reflecting on the night and day.

When you think about the heavens. What you notice is this vast expanse of the universe. And how everything is connected with each other so intricately. So delicately. Just think about this. We have the solar system that is so extremely powerful. We have these huge huge planets. But how delicately are they connected with each other. If there is the slightest imbalance. The whole structure crumbles. And how it affects us as human beings. If anything happens to the solar systems who gets eliminated? There is no life form on any of these planets that we know off. But if anything happens to this intricate balance between them. The earth gets destroyed. All life on earth gets destroyed. So the mind starts thinking. There has to be someone who created these enormous structures yet balanced them so delicately. Even if he created science as a tool. What a magnificent creation this tool is. That is keeping everything in its proper place.

Then when he thinks about the skies he thinks about winds. Winds out a means by which clouds travel. Winds are also a means by which dust and pollen travel.  Clouds bring what? Water! Pollen is what germinates the earth and as a result the which we get plants. And these plants need water. And the water comes from the clouds. And the clouds are delivered by the winds. So the breeze that we feel on our face. Is actually a delivery mechanism for this planet. One of the ways in which life on this planet is supported comes directly through winds. Without the breeze we would not actually be able to experience life. Because the plans that need to receive the pollen and wouldn't. Which means plants wouldn't come out. Which means animals would not have something to eat. And even if the earth gets germinated through pollen . The plant would not actually be able to grow without water. You know how we more lawns and water the grass in our backyards. Just look at Allah's backyard. Who's watering all these plants. It's the winds. That's not us. That's just being delivered through this delivery mechanism that Allah created. And then these trees. They inhale carbon dioxide and exhale oxygen. Which you and I are breathing. And all of this is because of the wind. Isn't it incredible how everything is working with everything else.

When we reflect on this. We see that the winds have a very special relationship with the clouds and pollen. In the sky that rains. Has a very cooperative relationship with the earth. They are working together. Constantly. To produce life on this art possible. If you look around and really observe. You see that all creation is actually working in cooperation with each other. Everything is dependent on something else for its own existence. And together they produce a higher purpose.

And then you start thinking about the night and day.  Does the night have purpose? Does Day have purpose? Do we actually need night and day?.  we absolutely do. Do we need sunlight? Yes we do! But then do we also need the absence of sunlight? We do! What would happen if there was only sunlight?   .  The plants would not grow and we would not have any restful sleep. We would have all sorts of physical and biological and psychological problems. Emotional problems. There is no research about places that do not get a lot of sunlight and those places have the highest suicide and depression rates.  Sunlight has to do with our emotional state. So when we really start thinking about the heavens and the earth and the day in the night. We realize that we have a very personal relationship with these things. . We are not independent of these things. We are completely dependent on them.

Now let's think about this a little further. Human beings are the dominant species on this planet. Isn't that true? Every other species. And every other thing on this planet. Is being utilized by human beings in some way or the other.

 the resources of this planet are being utilized by us. We are constantly drilling for stuff. Extracting things from the earth. And as for the other animals on this earth. We are either milking them. Or eating them. Or using their hide. To make clothes. The plants on this earth we are using to draw all kinds of chemicals. And nutrients. Or even barks of trees that we use for our construction. The stones of this earth are being used for our construction purposes. Even the silicon of this earth is being used for our technologies. The medals of this are that providing us with electricity. Copper and all this other stuff. Pretty much everything that exists on this earth. We figured out a way to utilize them and to serve us human beings. But the fact that we learn how to use it to serve ourselves. Makes us wonder. Did I actually invent copper?.  I may have invented copper fiber. But did I actually invent copper. I may have invented a table and a chair. But did I actually invent wood? Whatever things I needed to meet the advancements. That I as a human being needs to make. The raw materials for it. They were already here. weren't they?

You know a kid can take credit for making an amazing Legos thingee. But what can he not take credit for? The Lego pieces. The kid was provided with certain pieces to work with. Who provided those pieces? And how can these pieces fit so well together? When you see the masterpiece of the Legos. The final result of the creation. It's not so much the genius of the kid who put this thing together. It is actually the genius of the designer who design these pieces. That can work so well with each other. Enabling the kit to create this final masterpiece. Isn't it?

When you start thinking like that. Then we start developing a certain kind of appreciation. For our maker. And this kind of thinking makes us realize that everything on this earth is valuable. And has a purpose. And if everything has a purpose. All of these things that are inanimate. All of these have a purpose to serve me. All of these were created with the purpose of serving me.

Now lets see what the word ayah means. It means a lot of things.  It includes the meaning of something valuable.

خرج القوم بآیاتھم . ayah is somethihng valuable. Ayah is something that has purpose and meaning. This is why the word اِی  in Arabic. Literally means. Meaning. Comes from the same origin. the word Aye أَی . in arabic that comes from the same origin. Means to separate something from something else. Or distinguish something from something else. And from this word Aye comes Ayah. Which means that every ayah is distinct. Every ayah has meaning.  and every ayah has value.  

The word ayah also means a sign. A sign is something that points to something else. The wind is a sign that life is being delivered. Life being delivered is a sign. That I am being taken care of. Which is the sign. That I am actually not my own caretaker. Somebody is providing for me. One sign leads to another sign which leads to another sign which leads to another sign. Something is pointing to something. Which is then pointing to something. Which is then pointing to something else. That's part of the meaning of ayah. because one ayah leads to another ayah which leads to another aya.

So Allah  saying. That in the creations of the heaven and earth. And the change of night and day. There is something valuable. There is something meaningful. There is some kind of a lesson. There is some kind of a reminder. There is some kind of an indication. There is some kind of a cluye. For what kind of people? For people of sound minds. For people of pure minds.

But if people's minds are filled with sports statistics. And video games. And junk. And just trivial useless information. If their minds are filled with that. They're not going to see it. They're not going to see the bigger picture. They're not going to see the forest for the trees. They will just stay lost in the little details. They're not going to really appreciate what's truly happening. Someone who is obsessed with the shiny paper of the book. And the beautiful leather cover. And the print of the letters. If that's all he gets obsessed about. He will never actually think about reading the book. He will not worry about gaining the knowledge that comes from reading the book. Why? Because he is focused on the wrong thing. he is obsessed with just the external characteristics of the book instead of the purpose of the book itself. Just with the paper and the cover and the print. But not actually the content of the book itself.

That is the difference between peple who can appreciate an ayah and those who cannot appreciate an ayah. they are both looking at the same ting. but they're focused on the wrong thing.They don't see what it's actually saying. They know so much about it. There's a guy who knows so much about paper. That he can feel the paper of the Koran. And see this paper came from a particular kind of tree. And it's this density. And these are the kinds of factories that make it. That only exist in these countries. I can tell that this is so many years old. They can tell us so much about the paper. All of which is cool knowledge by the way. But does that knowledge actually help him get anything out of this book? Does he actually get any guidance from the book? NO! These are the people who do not have sound minds. They do not have pure minds. It's contaminated with all this other unnecessary facts. They do have amazing minds. It took a lot of knowledge time and effort to absorb all this information. But they put it to the wrong use. They used all that muscle to focus on the wrong thing. But people of pure minds. They are not just smart. They just learn to focus on the right things. On the useful things. That is the key to the whole discussion. To focus on the right thing. You will meet a lot of smart people in your life. College professors. Professionals. People at the top of their game. The problem won't be that they are not smart. The problem will be that they will be focused on the wrong things. And if you hang out with those kinds of people long enough. Guess what happens to you? You get focused on the wrong things to. And you get focused on the wrong thing so much. That when you actually speak with someone who is focused on the right thing. It just feels weird. It feels out of place. Like the friend who's focused on mine craft. Why you thinking about the sky and the earth. You should be thinking about mine craft and food in movies.

**http://www.bayyinah.tv/posts/quran-for-young-adults-day-7--2**

So a very good analogy that is given about people of sound mind. Is that if you eat a lot of junk food and then you throw in an apple once in a while. It does not really make a difference. That would not be necessarily a healthy diet. Neither are you going to see the positive effects of the fruit once a year. Just because your digestion is overwhelmed with foods that are unhealthy. You understand?

So what happens is that if you are constantly taking in useless information. And then once in a while you sucking in a session like this one where you are hopefully learning something positive. Something beneficial. You are not going to necessarily see positive results. It'll feel like in one year and out the other. Why? Because your mind is still focused on what? The wrong kind of information.

Some of you kids are so focused on your cell phones. You are so addicted to them. That you are texting even during the sessions. And you can even help yourselves. Your phone control you. Which is actually a very sad thing.

You see. A lot of dignified human beings with this incredible faculty called the intellect. It is an incredible gift. It is capable of amazing things. And when this incredible gift is used just to play candy crush. That is a tragedy of the human mind. What a waste of this amazing gift. So even if you can give up on entertainment and video games and movies. At least try to cut it down significantly. So you can actually use your mind for what it was created for. Something higher!! Something more!! For something like the quran. You see. One of the greatest dangers that we face in today's world. Is that entertainment has become God. Our entire lives revolve around entertainment. Whether that is movies video games are just having a good time. Now none of this is bad. But what happens is that this need for being constantly entertained. It takes over our lives. And then it controls us.  we are no longer in control of it. Because if you think about it. There is really no end to this. Your life will end. But the number of movies will never end. Your life will end but the video games will keep coming. You will never have played all of them. You will never have all the fun that is possible out there. So then this become sort of a bottomless pit. And we get so addicted to do stuff. That we can never find a break to actually do what we were created to do. So many people waste their entire lives chasing this never-ending high. And their life never actually amounts to anything in the true sense. This is why being from the uloo Albaab. People of sound mind. Is so important!!

Now. Thinking is actually an intellectual thing isn't it? But the people of sound mind are described having two parts. This is the next lesson here that I want you to understand. The Koran is concerned with your mind. And the Quran is concerned with your heart. I'll say that again. The Quran  is concerned with your mind and the Quran is concerned with your heart. What are some things that the mind does? The mind things. It processes information. Reaches conclusions. Analyzes. Tell your body what to do. Store. Remember. Memorize. Recall. Learn new things. So there are a lot of things that the mind does. Right?

According to the Quran what does the heart  do? Not the physical heart. All that does is pump blood. I'm talking about the spiritual heart. The spiritual heart does a few things according to the Quran. According to the Quran . The heart actually remembers. Because remember? One of the meanings of qalb. Is a vessel. And the job of a vessel is to store its contents. The heart also cares. Loves. Hates. Feels emotions. The heart gets excited. It gets motivated. According to the Quran the heart is a place for all the emotions. All emotions are associated with the heart. In a spiritual sense. Not in a neurological sense.

Quran appeals to heart and mind

The Quran's argument is that it wants to appeal to your mind. Now how do you appeal to someone's mind? How do you impress someone's mind? Logic! Evidence. Proof. Tell them something convincing. I can give you a very emotional speech but still be wrong altogether. You know? I can be really fired up. But I might as well put my foot in my mouth. Because I don't know what I'm talking about. So you can have situations where people are being very emotional. They are appealing to people's heart. But what they are saying makes no sense. There is no appeal to the mind. If you want to impress the mind you have to be reasonable. You have to provide good evidence. You have to be sound etc.

how do you appeal to the heart? Emotion! Anger love. Care. When your mom gives you a hug. And says I love you so much. Just be nice to your dad. She is not being rational. She's being what? She's being emotional. She's appealing to your sense of emotion. She's appealing to your heart. And that works!! Meaning human beings are not just intellectual creatures. They are also emotional creatures. We are not only impressed and motivated by reason. We are also motivated by emotion. We are spiritual emotional creatures. But we are also reasonable and intellectual. And we are not just purely one or the other. Were not. Were not robots.

And the example that I can give you to create this distinction between the heart and the mind. Is by giving an example of a young man who likes to smoke. A young man who really likes to smoke but he is also extremely smart. He gets like 100 in biology. And if he gets 100 and biology. You know that he knows. That smoking is pretty bad. Actually he understands that better than most people. Because he has seen pictures of deformed lungs. He knows exactly what smoking does physiologically to you. How many minutes it takes off your life and all this other stuff. And yet. After getting 100 on the same test. On the biology of the lungs. What does he do outside the class? He smokes! And you have to ask this young man. Why do you smoke? And the most common answer that you will get. Is that I don't know. It just feels good. But don't you know that it's so harmful? Yeah I do! But whatever. Is whatever and intellectual response? Is that a reasonable scientific answer? No! What is that? It's emotional. Feels good. My friends do it. Makes me look cool. I think I look extra attractive when I smoke. Because when people pass by me. And they almost puke by the disgusting smell of cigarettes. I think that's a sign of real manhood.

Something is going on in this young man's head. That even though the surgeon generals warning. On the side of the cigarette packet. Which clearly states. That you will get cancer if you smoke this thing. That is still clearly not enough. For this young man to  not smoke. Now the same kid goes home. Goes up to his room closed the door. Lights up a cigarette. And start smoking. And he sees his dad pull up in the driveway. What does he do? But it out. Flush it down the toilet. Air freshener. Mint. HaaaH HaaaH HaaaH. The Surgeon General said you would get cancer. That wasn't enough. But the father pulled up in the driveway and that was enough. The father hasn't even said anything yet. He doesn't even know what you were doing. Nothing! So then what drove him to change his behavior? Fear? Respect? So can I say that he was motivated not by reason but by emotion? You understand? Sometimes you can know that something is wrong. From an intellectual standpoint. But you do it anyway. Only because it feels good. Because the emotion is too strong.

The Koran recognizes that you cannot just change your life through reason. Your heart needs to be won over to. There are two parts of you. You see in the ayah. When a low wanted us to think about the creation of the heavens and the earth. And the conflict between the night and day. That is all intellectual stuff. But the heart needs help to. The heart to needs to be cleansed. So then what these people of sound mind. people who say

ٱلَّذِينَ يَذْكُرُونَ ٱللَّهَ قِيَمًۭا وَقُعُودًۭا وَعَلَىٰ جُنُوبِهِمْ وَيَتَفَكَّرُونَ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا سُبْحَنَكَ فَقِنَا عَذَابَ ٱلنَّارِ

According to the Koran. Zikr. Remembering the law is an act of the heart. So they remember Allah standing sitting in on their sides. In other words they do something that helps make their heart stronger. And they think deeply. And they think a lot. About the creations of the heavens and the earth. Thinking is an action of the mind. So half the verses about the heart and the other half is about the mind. And you need to work on both.

Now this is where we need to analyze this in historical context. Before Islam there were two nations that were supersmart. The Israelites and the Christians. The Jews and the Christians. Jews were supersmart. But Allah said that their hearts became hard. They were extremely intelligent. Very knowledgeable. But their hearts became hard. Because their hearts were void of the remembrance of Allah. On the other hand you have people whose hearts were really soft. They would cry all the time. They were so emotional so loving so caring. But they close the doors to their intellects. Allah says in this ayah. That people of sound minds. Are actually people who remember Allah. And then also reflect on the creation of the heavens and earth. Remembering the law is what again? It is an action of the heart! And reflecting on the creations of the heavens and the earth is what? It is an action of the intellect. Both of these things go hand-in-hand.

So when someone comes and says. Yes I do think about the heavens and the earth. But I do not feel any gratitude in my heart. And I don't find any one worthy of praise for creating this stuff. I don't feel like I owe anybody anything. Well yes! Because you are using your mind. You are using your intellect. But you still have an exercise anything in your heart. Qurna says you are made up of both. You are not purely a rational creature. And you are not purely an emotional creature. You are a perfect combination of both. As a matter of fact. Which one is given a priority in these verse. Which one comes first? The heart!Remembrance of Allah is mentioned first.

And when we started studying the Fateha. What words did we start with? Hamd which means what?  All praise and gratitude belongs to Allah. Is that a matter of the mind or the heart? It's an emotional thing!! To feel appreciated toward someone. To thank someone. Allah says the heart comes first. And that is why a law says in the Quran. That successful people will come before Allah on Judgment Day. Not with a clean mind but with a clean sound heart. Because heart comes first.

And this is really important to understand. Because we need to prioritize what we love and what we hate. Because that's what the heart is all about. What you love and what you hate. What you are afraid of and what you are not afraid of. This is the kind of connection that we need to build with allah. People who believe with the law they recognize his presence all the time. Once they recognize his presence they do not care about anybody else. Or any pressure from anybody else. If somebody is pushing them to do the wrong thing. It really doesn't matter to them. Because to them heart comes first. And now Allah lives in that heart. They constantly recognize Allah's presence. You always feel strengthened when you know that somebody is there for you. You don't feel weak anymore. You don't feel all on your own anymore.

The difference doesn't happen when you only believe in Allah in your head. Even before you came to the session you knew about Allah. You knew you were supposed to love them. You knew you were supposed to be grateful to him. You knew you were supposed to be thankful to him. But all that information does not actually motivate you to stand before him and prayers. But when the love of Allah enters your heart.  And you actually feel his presence in your heart. Nothing in the world can actually stop you from standing before him and prayers. Because in their head. Anybody can say that I believe in a God. But to be emotionally attached in your heart with Allah. His support his love his protection his mercy. To feel it constantly with you. That is something completely different. That is not something that can be explained through words. Words fall short.

So according to this verse. The heart comes first. And when the heart comes first you will automatically put your intellect in the right direction. You will focus on the right things. If your heart has not been conquered yet your mind will work in the wrong direction. That is actually the whole Koranic theory. From what I've understood. Is that the heart actually gives direction to the intellect.

For example. Your heart decides that you want to be a doctor. You want. That is not rational. That is a desire. And because of the intensity of the desire. Now you are going to study what? Medicine. You are now going to exhaust your mind studying medicine but the motivation behind it was what came from the heart. Your heart decided that you wanted to make your dad proud. You wanted to help people. You wanted to make a difference in people's lives. You wanted to make Allah happy by helping his creation. Whatever that motivation was. It came from the heart. So what I'm saying is. You are going to study hard because of what your heart desired. Your mind will be exhausted in what you desire.

There are a people for example. Who hates studying but they love working out. They want to look a certain way. And in order to look a certain way you have to learn something about nutrition. You have to learn something about exercise. You have to learn about good habits etc. So even they who hates studying. Especially biology and physiology. They will study some aspects of physiology. What is the best time to eat what. How much protein how much carbohydrate they need to consume. At what time of the day. Even they will learned that stuff. Why? Because of their desire to look good. Are there desire to get ripped or whatever. They'll do it. In other words your heart will pick a direction. And then your mind will focus on it. That is why the heart is first.This is why Zikr frist. Remembrance first. And then thinking about the heavens and the earth. So remember I told you that people's minds are focused on the wrong sort of things. And they're thinking about entertainment and video games and movies. And stuff like that. But who's going to be thinking about the heavens and the earth? The one whose heart is focused on the remembrance of Allah.

### Conclusion of reflection

now here is the epic part

رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا

so these people are thinking about the heavens and the earth. And after the reflection to reach a conclusion. And the conclusion is.  Rabbana ma khalqta haza batilaa. Oh master. You did not create all of this without purpose. There is no way all of this is useless. There is no way all of this does not have meaning. When something has meaning. What is it called? When something has meaning. And value and purpose. What is it called? It's called an ayah. so this person realizes that everything around him is a sign.  it is an ayah. SubhanAllah

this has to have some meaning. This has to have some purpose. All of this did not just come here for no reason. I am not here for no reason. I am way too intricate. I am way too involved. I have way too many gifts. I am way too advanced a creation to just exist without any purpose. Out of an accident. There has to be something. There is no way that I can accept that I'm here without a purpose. How can all of this around me have purpose to serve me. Yet I can exist without a purpose. That does not make sense to me.   رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا

you did not create any of this without a purpose.

You know there is this really interesting theory about games and sports. I'm actually compelled by this theory. In any game there are certain rules. If you really understand those rules of the game. And you abide by them. You will succeed. Like for example basketball or cricket they have fundamentals. If you get really good at the fundamentals you will definitely succeed. And then you can add your own creativity above and beyond that.

A videogame has certain fundamentals. Once you learn the basic moves you can advance and then learn the more complicated moves. And you can try more creative things and succeed. So if you just simply follow the rules. You can get game points. Trophies. 100% synchronization's. So you know in video games you have these things that you can do. That if you do them properly you can actually synchronize your character up to 100%. And now they can do everything that is possible at the maximum level. So they give you a sense of accomplishment. Why do you think people are obsessed with trophies? Are these trophies worth any money? Especially within video games? Is hundred percent synchronization going to make your couch more comfortable? Is anything valuable actually going to happen? No! Then why is it that we become so obsessed with these things when were playing video games? It's very interesting psychology. And the psychology that is offered behind it. Is that in this life there are no set rules. In other words somebody can work really hard in life and still not when. Does that happen? Absolutely. And somebody does not work hard at all and they win the lottery. That happens to. So it seems like this life is unfair. And even if you play by the rules you will not necessarily get a trophy and you will not necessarily get points. And it doesn't feel good. To work hard and not get something in return. So. We tend to turn towards a mechanism. To a world in which there are six rules. And if you just abide by these rules you will definitely get points. And you will definitely get trophies. That will absolutely happen as long as you follow the rules. Does that work outside of the game? If you just study really hard can you go to school every single day. You will definitely get a good job. You will definitely make it to the college that you always wanted to go in. You will definitely make the money that you dreamed of making. Is anything definite in life? No! So human beings like certainty. In our conscience we love having certainty. We love games. Because games give us what? It gives a certainty. If I do this this and this I will definitely win. I will definitely be ranked higher. I will definitely have more and more and more. We hate the idea that we do not have certainties and guarantees in this life. So we love to immerse ourselves in a world. That does give us some guaranty. Amazing isn't it? And all of this is from a disbelievers perspective!

You know what is even more amazing? That from a believers perspective there are guarantees for this world. Every single thing that you do will be compensated. If you follow the rules that have been laid out. You will get a trophy. You will get points. You will get a higher rank. Nothing that you do in this world is going unpaid. Unrewarded. There is absolutely a point system in place. And you are in this game of life. Incredible that the Koran says that this life is nothing but a game.

وَمَا ٱلْحَيَوٰةُ ٱلدُّنْيَآ إِلَّا لَعِبٌۭ

Worldly life is nothing but a game. And in a game what you have to do? Follow the rules and try to win. Earn points. In some sense that is exactly what we are trying to do. For a disbeliever is there a point system? NO! For us is there a point system? Absolutely! And if we can really understand this. If we are really dedicated towards this point system. This game that Allah has created for us. Then we realized that we really do not have time for the other games. Because we are involved in something that has much higher stakes. Much higher points. SubhanAllah

You did not create this without purpose. There is no way you gave me this life and all my experiences. And that none of them are worth anything. That they are not worth any points. That I have to go somewhere else and try to earn fake points.

رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا

Subhanak you are way above that.  Subhanak. You are too perfect for that.  to create something without purpose.

That leads us to think. How is it possible that I was created without a purpose? Just think about that.

. This is incredible realization. That everything in this universe under the heavens and the earth. In the creation of the heavens and earth. And the conflict of night and day. If all of this has the ultimate purpose of serving me. Then would I not have a purpose? Was I just created to enjoy all of this without an actual ultimate goal? That doesn't make sense! Which means that I do have a goal and purpose! That begs the next question. What is that goal? What is that purpose?

Now let's take the analogy off that video game a little further. If you are playing a game that has no end goal. Imagine that it's a free open world. It's a completely free open world. Do you ever have that when you beat a videogame. When you complete the final stage. They just let you roam around. You have all your powers because you have hundred percent synchronization. But now that you have completed the game. You can just roam around without any more purpose. You can do whatever you want. Is it as enjoyable as it was when you were actually playing the game? When you actually had an end goal in mind? No it's not. You may have some fun for a little while. But you know what you're going to do pretty soon? Pretty soon what are you going to do? You are going to stop playing that game. You will lose interest. Why? There are no points anymore. There is no goal anymore. There are no trophies to win. There is no sense of accomplishment anymore. There is no sense of adventure anymore. All of it is gone. So eventually what you do? You quit.

There are people in this world. That when they start believing that there is no greater purpose to this life. There are no more points. Life has no meaning. Guess what comes next?  They kill themselves. They get married. No I'm kidding. And even if they don't give up on their lives they live a very sad and miserable life of depression. Its a very sad way to live.

So the person reaches the conclusion. you are way to exalted to create anything without a purpose. so now what? فقنا عذاب النار . protect us from the hell fire. In other words. do not let us lose. in this game of life. We cannot afford to lose. So now you realize that this is about points and this is about fulfilling a purpose. So if you do not fulfill that purpose there is going to be a punishment.

What is that purpose of life?

وما خلقت الجن و الانس الا لعبدونِ

رَبَّنَآ إِنَّكَ مَن تُدْخِلِ ٱلنَّارَ فَقَدْ أَخْزَيْتَهُ

Master whoever you enter into the fire has been humiliated. Oh Allah whoever did not use your gifts. Who did not use his heart and his intellect. To reflect on the universe and get closer to you. Who did not play this game of life. And who did not accomplish the purpose of this life. Who did not win points who did not win trophies. And who became the loser in the afterlife. And entered your hell. He's the one who has been truly humiliated.

This is the conclusion that all of us have to reach all by ourselves. Faith is not something that can be given to you by your parents. Faith is not something that can be given to you by your teachers. It has to come from your own heart and your own intellect. You have to believe for yourself.

There is no taqleed in aqeedah. There is no imitation in creed. Rather there is no blind imitation in creed. You cannot actually blindly follow anyone when it comes to being convinced. You will have to reach your own conviction. And that is of the absolute importance. If the only reason you are Muslim is because your parents are Muslims. And you haven't reached this conclusion yourself. For yourself. Then that faith is artificial. And that faith will not provide the right kind of results. I don't know if we can even call it fate. You have to come to this conclusion. The reason were going through these verses. Together. Is because I want all of us to reach this conclusion again. And what is that conclusion?

رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا

Master you did not create all of this in vain. We all have to reach this conclusion for ourselves all over again. You have to think about the skies and the earth for yourself. You have to think about the conflict between the night and day for yourself. Not because I'm telling you. I do this exercise only for myself. But you have to do it for you. You have to sit and ponder. You have to sit and reflect. For your self. And you have to reinforce for yourself what is it that you believe. This is what the call of Quran is. Asking people to reflect. Asking people to think. What a powerful religion this is. This is not a religion that says. Just belief! And if you don't believe you are going to hell. This is a religion that says. Think about the sky think about the earth. Think about the night and day. Come to the realization that there has to be a purpose. And then hear the call of someone calling. That aligns with your belief system that you have come to conclude.

رَّبَّنَآ إِنَّنَا سَمِعْنَا مُنَادِيًۭا يُنَادِى لِلْإِيمَنِ أَنْ آمِنُوا۟ بِرَبِّكُمْ فَـَٔامَنَّا ۚ رَبَّنَا فَٱغْفِرْ لَنَا ذُنُوبَنَا وَكَفِّرْ عَنَّا سَيِّـَٔاتِنَا وَتَوَفَّنَا مَعَ ٱلْأَبْرَارِ

BOOM! Now you have belief. that is what you call faith

<!-- section 2 (id=5749, raw_sort=2): Creation is a sign -->

## Section 5749

Now that we've completed the Istiaaza and the Basmallah. today I want to take a step back and take a look at something a bit different. Something that will get us to the ayah of Hamd. Someone said to me.  that even though we say that Quran is a universal message. it seems from the study of Fateha so far. that the Quran is meant only for the Muslims. So then what about the people who are not born in Muslim families. How do they ever get to the Quran. And that's a very interesting question. Because the Quran does talk about that. and that's what I want to talk about today. I want to talk about this underlying mindset that a certain type of human being develops. regardless of race or religion. that leads him to revelation. In other words. Quran does not begin with the Fateha. It actually begins with a mindset. a thought process that leads to the Fateha. and that's what I want to share with you today.

These are ayaats from Surah Aale Imran. the third chapter. verses 190 - 193. Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ وَٱخْتِلَفِ ٱلَّيْلِ وَٱلنَّهَارِ لَآيَتٍۢ لِّأُو۟لِى ٱلْأَلْبَبِ⟫

No doubt about it. Especially when it comes to the creation of the heavens and the earth. And especially when it comes to the fight between night and day. The conflict that takes place between night and day there are signs for the people of sound essence. The first thing I want you to note. is that it does not say . ⟪ar:لَآيَتٍۢ لمسلمین⟫. There are signs for Muslims. or . ⟪ar:لَآيَتٍۢ لمؤمنین⟫. there are signs for believers. It says. ⟪ar:لَآيَتٍۢ لِّأُو۟لِى ٱلْأَلْبَبِ⟫. So let's first understand the meaning of these two words.

The word ayah means a lot of things. It includes the meaning of something valuable. ⟪ar:خرج القوم بآیاتھم⟫ . The people came out with their valuables. So ayah is something that is valuable. something that has purpose and meaning. Ayah also means to separate something from something else. or make one thing DISTINCT from another. 

Now the Quran is made up of ayats. or verses. And so each verse is valuable. it has a specific purpose. it has a specific meaning. and each ayah is distinct. or searpate. from another ayah. Understand?

The word Ayah also means a sign. And we talked about this earlier. A sign.  is something that POINTS to something else.  The wind is a sign that life is being delivered. Life being delivered is a sign. that I am being taken care of. Which is then a sign. that I am actually not my own caretaker.  Which is then a sign that someone else is providing for me. One sign leads to another sign . which leads to another sign . which leads to another sign.  You understand?

And we see in the Quran. Reciting one ayah. leads to another ayah. which leads to another ayah. And this is how the Quran is formed. right?. Group of ayaats turn into a ruku. Ruku turns into a juz. a group of Juz. they turns into a Surah. Group of surahs turn into Paras. 30 Paras. turn into one single Quran. This is similar to the distinct creations on this earth. each creation of Allah (AZZA WA JAL) is an ayah. Each creation is something valuable. it has a purpose. it has a meaning. it is distinct from every other creation. And then these creations group to form one single planet. within a bunch of planets. to form a solar system. within a galaxy. that exists within billions of galaxies. within one universe. You see the correspondence between the Quran and the universe?. This universe is a physical Quran. just like the Quran is a spiritual universe. I'll say it again. This universe is a physical Quran. just like the Quran is a spiritual universe. So Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ وَٱخْتِلَفِ ٱلَّيْلِ وَٱلنَّهَارِ لَآيَتٍۢ لِّأُو۟لِى ٱلْأَلْبَبِ⟫

No doubt. In the creations of the heaven and earth. and the change of night and day. there is something valuable. There is something meaningful. There are distinct things to observe. and various lessons to learn. There is some kind of a reminder. There is some kind of an indication. There is some kind of a clue. NOT FOR EVERYONE. but for certain types of people. for the ⟪ar:اولی الاباب⟫.

Meaning of Ulil-Albaab

⟪ar:اولی الاباب⟫ is commonly translated as people of sound intellects. But what's more true in meaning. is people of sound essence. Albaab is the plural form. It's singular form. Lubb. is actually a very beautiful word. In Classical Arabic. when you crack open an almond. the kernel that you find inside. that's called lubb. OK?. The kernel . inside a nut. The seed insoide a fruit is called . lubb. why? Because one. it is the essence of the fruit. The seed contains the entire tree within itself in a passive form.  And two. it is protected from all sides by the nut or the fruit. And because it is ALWAYS protected from any and all external influences. it's essence remains pure. So ⟪ar:اولی الاباب⟫. means pure essence. or a clean mind. that is not polluted by useless things. that is the definition of the word Lubb. A person whose thoughts are not polluted by useless things. A person who actually thinks about meaningful things.

This mind that Allah gave us.  is actually a very powerful gift. It is extremely capable. We can actually memorize entire books. We can store incredible amounts of data. There are people. that when they put their minds to something. they become extremely knowledgeable in the area on which they focus. For example there are commentators that can tell you sports statistics. from 50 years ago. All off the top of their heads. They know the names of every athlete. how long their career lasted. what teams they played for. which college they went to. what year they were drafted. who drafted them. How many rings they have. When they suffered injuries. When they were reinstated. My God! That is incredible!. When we human beings put our minds to it. we are capable of storing incredible amounts of data. This intellect. is a REALLY powerful thing.

Some of you kids. 12/13 years old. you start playing a first person shooter videogame. or a fighting game like Street fighter or Mortal Kombat. and you memorize every single move for that game character. SSTTCS-R1-TS. And that's just one combo move. right?. And you know every single move there is for that character. You know all the cheat codes. you know all the walkthroughs. all of the top of your head.

There are people that get obsessed with TV shows. There are people that get obsessed with fashion. There are some people I know that are obsessed with news. Have you met people like that?. When they talk. you're like. WOAH. DUDE! How do you even know that. WHY do you even know that. right? . This mind is an incredibly powerful thing. When we put our minds to something. we can actually do amazing things.

Now all of this may be good stuff to know from the worldly perspective. You can get a certain kind of a job based on this information. Show off to your friends. Appear all K-O-O-L.  But in line with our ultimate goal. is this useful knowledge?.  Is this something that is going to help us in the afterlife? . NO. It's not!

Allah is telling us in this verse. That even though there are SO many people in this world. that will put their minds to all this kind of stuff. there are a few people. special kind of people. people of pure essence. that will focus their minds on things. which you and I would not even consider. They stop and think about the skies the earth and how they were actually created. And they start thinking about how there is a natural conflict between night and day. What are these conflicts that Allah is talking about?. The day is bright and night is dark. As the day progresses the daylight starts gradually winning over the darkness. And then as the day ends. the darkness starts winning over the night. The sun goes from being bright yellow to orange. And the sky goes from being bright blue to dark blue until it becomes completely black. And night finally wins. In another surah Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:‏وَٱلَّيْلِ وَمَا وَسَقَ⟫

I swear by the night and whatever it covers everything. And then . that full black night starts losing its battle with the day. And what happens? The sky starts getting brighter and brighter and brighter. until it's daylight again and all traces of the night are eliminated. And this battle keeps happening every single day.

So Allah is talking about these special people. these people of pure essence. These are the people. who will look at Allah's creation. Allah's AYAATS. and they will actually be able to APPRECIATE the value. the meaning. the purpose. within them. They will be able to SEE . what and who these miraculous signs are pointing to. And those who are not Ulil-Albaab. for them this universe will just be nothing more than a cosmic accident. something that just randomly happened. They will not be able to actually witness Allah's signs. because their mind is focused on the wrong thing.

There are people in this world. that you hand them the Quran. And the first thing they will do is start feeling the paper of the Quran between their fingers. they'll focus on the material of the paper itself. And then he'll tell you how this paper came from a particular kind of tree. and it's this density. and these are the kinds of factories that make it.  that only exist in these countries. you know!. This paper is so many years old. Because this man has spent his entire life studying SO much about paper. Or he'll tell you about the calligraphy of the ayaats. Oh this is the Noorani Nastaleeq script. it was created by this person. in this country. and this is how he perfected it. it has so many variations. and so many different styles in which its written. All of which . BTW. is VERY cool knowledge. It's AWESOME knowledge. It's a very interesting conversation to have over tea. But does that knowledge actually help him get anything out of this Quran?. What was the purpose of the Quran?. Why was the book given to him?. To learn from it. to get guidance from it. But what is he focusing on?. Paper and Calligraphy. So this is what happens when people contaminate their minds with all these other unnecessary facts.  They do have amazing minds.  It took a lot of knowledge time and effort.  to learn. absorb and retain all this information. But that's wasn't the purpose. They used all that intellectual muscle to focus on the wrong thing. They're tying the horse behind the cart.  Now if they did focus on the guidance of Quran first. and in addition to that learn about paper and calligraphy. that would be GREAT!. right?. But instead these are people that peel the banana. toss the fruit aside. and write research papers on the peel of the banana. 

But people of pure minds are different. It's not that they are just smart. they actually just learn to focus on the right things.  on the useful things. That is the key to the whole discussion todeay. to focus on the right thing. You will meet a lot of smart people in your life. College professors. Professionals. People at the top of their game. The problem won't be that they are not smart. The problem will be that they will be focused on the wrong things. And if you hang out with those kinds of people long enough.  guess what happens to you?.  You get focused on the wrong things too. And you get focused on the wrong thing so much. that when you actually speak with someone who is focused on the right thing. it just feels weird. It feels out of place. Why do you want me to focus on the sky and the earth dude?. Let's play minecraft. and build our own sky. That is so much more cool.

Allah says. people of sound intellects. and pure essence. In everything they see around them. they see a distinct sign. And then Allah describes the characteristics of such people. He says.
⟪ar-quote:ٱلَّذِينَ يَذْكُرُونَ ٱللَّهَ قِيَمًۭا وَقُعُودًۭا وَعَلَىٰ جُنُوبِهِمْ وَيَتَفَكَّرُونَ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ⟫

These are people who remember Allah. standing. sitting and on their sides. These are the three possible human states. We are either standing. or we are sitting. or we are lying down. In other words. these are people who are CONSTANTLY reflecting on these signs. on the creations of the sky and the earth.

---

So now let's see this in action.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ وَٱخْتِلَفِ ٱلَّيْلِ وَٱلنَّهَارِ لَآيَتٍۢ لِّأُو۟لِى ٱلْأَلْبَبِ⟫

No doubt. in the creation of the heavens and the earth. and the conflict of night and day. there are clear. distinct. meaningful. purposeful signs for people of clean minds. for people who focus on the right things.

Now when I think about the heavens. the first thing I notice. is the vast expanse of the universe. And how everything is connected with everything else so intricately. so delicately. I see that we have this powerful solar system. we have these huge huge planets. yet they are so delicately connected with each other. If there is the slightest imbalance. the whole structure crumbles. so I see this magnificent design that exists in these creations.

Then I start thinking about the individual creations. and I see that one of the most promient creations. is the sun. So I start thinking about the sun. What are some of the facts that we know about the sun today. The first thing is that it is ENORMOUS. It is GIGANTIC. Today we know that the sun is SO big.  it can fit over a 100 earths in it. We also know that there are nuclear explosions. that are constantly taking place within its core. which is producing energy. And if we wanted to produce the same kind of energy. we would have to detonate . 100 billion tons of dynamite. every second. to match the energy produced by the sun. Then we know. that it is the sun. that is making life possible on this planet. And one of the many reasons for that.  is because the sun is placed at this very specific distance from the earth. which is 92 million miles away from the earth. If the sun was any closer to the earth. it would burn the earth to a crisp. If it was any further away. this earth would freeze.

Then we also know that this huge ball of nuclear energy. is moving at a speed of over 450,000 miles per hour around the Milky way. 450,000 miles per hour. If I drive my car more than 75 miles/hour. there is a good chance I'll lose control of it. That's why we have speed limits right?. The sun is moving at over 450,000 miles/hour. What do you think would happen.  if the sun lost control. even if for a few seconds. What do you think would happen?.

So I start thinking. WOW!. What an AMAZING creation. It's so powerful. Qawee. So magnificent. Azeem. It is SO beautiful. Jameel. Something that is making life possible for me. providing me with sustenance. AlRazzaq. So if this creation is SO incredible. How incredible. how powerful. how magnificent. how glorious and how beautiful must its creator be?. So now am I doing here?. I'm the martian. reflecting on the iPad. to figure out the capabilities of the human being. remember?

Then I see.  that this sun. as powerful. and as magnificent as it is. it is bound. it is bound by forces of gravity. So it makes me wonder. who bound it?. Because the sun is clearly not doing what it feels like doing. It doesn't just show up whenever it feels like it. It only shows up when it is supposed to show up. It sets when it is supposed to set. It does what it is supposed to do. EVERY single DAY.  ALL day long.month upon month. year after year. I see the sun in complete submission to its purpose.

So I think. WOW. THE SUN. despite being so powerful. is in complete submission. And this is just one creation. What about the galaxy itself?. What about this milky way?. Scientists now say that there are atleast 100 billion planets in the Milky way. And this is just one galaxy. And there are 100 billion galaxies in the OBSERVABLE universe. We don't even know how many ACTUALLY exist. 100 billion is just in what has been observed thus far.

So if this is the creation. And we know its a creation because it did not always exist. It has a beginning. a duration and one day it will come to an end. just like me. Just like every other creation. So if this is the creation. what must the creator be like?. And I can't even wrap my head around the enormity of the creation. how am I to understand the powers. and the magnificence and the glory of the creator?. Therefore I reach the conclusion. that the one who created all of this. has to be an Ilah. Someone . whose glory. who's magnificence. whose loftiness. I simply cannot fathom. There's no way I'll EVER be able to understand Him. I see the expanse of this universe. as a sign. pointing to the fact. that there is no way I'll be able to understand its creator. And therefore the one who created this. by definition of the word Ilah. is THE ILAH. ALLAH.

Then I start thinking about the design of the night and day. Does the night have purpose? . Does day have a purpose? . Do I actually need night and day?.  I absolutely do. Do I need sunlight? . Yes I do! . But then do I ALSO need the absence of sunlight? . Absolutely. I need that too. What would happen if there was only sunlight?   .  The plants would not grow. I would not have any restful sleep. I would have all sorts of physical and psychological problems. emotional problems. Today there is research about how places that do not get a lot of sunlight. how they have the highest suicide and depression rates.  Sunlight actually has to do with our emotional state. So when I REALLY start thinking about the heavens and the earth and the day and the night. I realize that I have a very personal relationship with these things. I am not a creation. that is independent of these things. Infact I am completely dependent on them.

Then I think. who is the one benefitting from this creation. Who is the consumer here. If all of this creation is Allah's product. who is the consumer?. Who is the dominant species on this planet. It is us human beings. Isn't that true? Every other species. and every other thing on this planet. is being utilized by human beings in some way or the other. All the  resources of this planet are being utilized by us. We are constantly drilling for stuff. extracting things from the earth. Even the animals of this earth. We are either milking them. or eating them. or using their hydes to make clothes. We are using the plants on this earth. to draw all kinds of chemicals. and nutrients. Even the barks of trees. we use them for our construction. The stones of this earth are being used for our construction purposes. EVEN the silicon of this earth is being used for our technologies. The metals of this earth. they are providing us with electricity. copper and all this other stuff. So pretty much everything that exists on this earth. we human beings have figured out a way to utilize them. and use them to serve ourselves. us human beings. But then it makes me wonder. Did I actually invent copper?.  I may have invented copper fiber. But did I actually invent copper. I may have invented a table and a chair. But did I actually invent wood?.  Whatever things I needed to make these advancements. the raw materials for it. they were already here for me. weren't they?

You know a kid can take credit for making an amazing Legos thingee. But what can he not take credit for?.  The Lego pieces.  The kid was provided with certain pieces to work with. Who provided those pieces?.  And how can these pieces fit so well together that make this construction possible?.  When you see the masterpiece of the Legos. the final result of the creation. that is not so much the genius of the kid who put this thing together. It is actually the genius of the designer who designed these pieces this way. that can work so well with each other. Enabling the kid to create this final masterpiece. Isn't it?

So I'm see these blocks of legos at work all around me. This masterpiece. made up of different blocks. all coming together so perfectly. The sun is providing me with light and heat . making it possible for me to work during the day. The moon is filtering down the light and heat. making the night pleasant so I can rest during the night. winds are carrying clouds. clouds are producing rain. water is being absorbed by the earth. which is then producing vegetation. which is sustaining animals. animals in turn are sustaining human life. I am the one consuming them for food. for clothes. for ornaments. And because this is by design it is consistent. Every creation is doing EXACTLY what it's supposed to be doing. consistently. I never see an apple tree producing mangoes. I never plant a rose garden and then get surprised with tulips instead. Everything is functioning the way it was designed. Everything is fulfilling its purpose. And who is the one taking advantage of all of this.  that this world is offering?. Who is at the center of all of this. reaping all of its benefits. It is me. US human beings. So I now think. WOW!. Allah did all of this for me!!. He designed this entire machienery. put together this solar system. for me. So that I could benefit from it.

Why would he do that?. He must really love me. He must really care for me. He must be genuinely concerned about my well-being. And I think. SubhanAllah! . He is so powerful. yet he is so merciful with me. And not just that. I see he is extremely merciful. and constantly merciful. Because I know that all of this will exist tomorrow as well. I know the sun will rise again. the moon will come out again. the earth will still provide sustenance. OMG. I can completely DEPEND on him. TRUST HIM. Put my weight on him. That is a definition of what word?. ILAH. He is my Ilah.

Then I start thinking about his mercy. and I ask myself. Does he actually need to be merciful?. Does a soverign. POWERFUL king. with ABSOLUTELY no fear of retribution. NO fear of accountability. NO one to answer to. Does He really need to be merciful. Because Allah is not accountable to anyone. He doesn't need anything. Everything and everyone needs him.

⟪ar-quote:يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلنَّاسُ أَنتُمُ ٱلْفُقَرَآءُ إِلَى ٱللَّهِۖ وَٱللَّهُ هُوَ ٱلْغَنِىُّ ٱلْحَمِيدُ⟫

Oh people. you are all in complete need of Allah. And Allah is entirely self-sufficient without you

⟪ar-quote:إِن يَشَأْ يُذْهِبْكُمْ وَيَأْتِ بِخَلْقٍۢ جَدِيدٍۢ ‎⟫

If he so desires. he can remove all of you. and put in your place a new creation

So I ask myself. what if . instead of mercy. what if he had characterized himself with power and justice. Because that would mean. the second I do something wrong. the all powerful should decrees his justice against me. He punishes me right away. Because that's the rule of this world isn't it?. If I am caught stealing. the officer won't say. oh it's ok. I know you really wanted that xbox. it's ok. don't do it next time. NO. My parents won't do that for me. right?. I'll immediately get punished.

So when I miss a prayer. I would expect angels to descends from the sky. and beat me to a pulp. Because prayer. is Allah's right on me. And He has the right to demand that right off me. and punish me if I don't fulfill that right. Can he do that?. Can he FORCE me to fulfill his rights.  whether I want to or not. We all pay taxes ever year. so we know what that feels like. We can't escape a government. do you think we could escape Allah?. What if Allah . being my creator. imposed a property tax on me. I mean he'd be totally justified. He wouldn't be wrong if he did that. After all . he IS my creator. and that makes me his property. So he can do with me . whatever he pleases. Does he do that?. What if my sustenance and my daily ration of food. water. sleep. even oxygen. What if all of this was given to me based on my level of obedience to him. ? Does he has the power to do that?. He sure does.

⟪ar-quote:مَّا مِن دَآبَّةٍ إِلَّا هُوَ آخِذٌۢ بِنَاصِيَتِهَآ⟫

There is not a single moving creature that Allah does not hold by its forelock.

When we start thinking like that. we start developing a very special kind of appreciation for our maker. What an amazing creator!. What a loving creator. What a caring creator. What a merciful creator. His love . his care. his mercy.  is beyond this world. It is SO intense. and it is SO much. that I have not way of measuring it. So now when I realize all of this. what is my natural response?. What is the most natural response. as a decent human being. as a barely decent human being. what should be my response to the one who shows me this kind of extreme love?. I want to love him back. passionately. I constantly start thinking about him. I get obsessed with his love. right?. Cause if I want to be from the UlilAlbaab. that's the characteristic he described.

⟪ar-quote:ٱلَّذِينَ يَذْكُرُونَ ٱللَّهَ قِيَمًۭا وَقُعُودًۭا وَعَلَىٰ جُنُوبِهِمْ وَيَتَفَكَّرُونَ فِى خَلْقِ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ⟫

Those who CONSTANTLY think about Allah and CONSTANTLY reflect on his creation. They are obsessed with Allah. They are passionately in love with Allah. right?. Wait. That's a defintion of what word again?. ILAH.

So now I have feel this sense of obligation. driven by this extreme form of love that is being shown to me. So now I wanna do something for the one who loves me so much. I want to make him happy. Because he is my ilah.

Notice I haven't even heard a single word of the revelation yet. I haven't even heard one single ayah of the Quran yet. I'm reaching these conclusions. just by observing the creation around me. You understand?. the martian is just studying the ipad and thinking about its designer. It hasn't found that manual yet that talks about human beings.

So now I'm thinking. this creator loves me so much. I want to do something back for him. But what can I do?. What need does he have of me?. What could I possibly do in return for the one who has absolutely NO need of me. That's another thing. Why is he doing this for me.  when he doesn't even need anything back in return. Because there's nothing I could possibly offer to Allah. He is AsSamad. Absolutely self sufficient. So then WHY is he being so merciful to me?. It has to be because.

⟪ar-quote:لا یکون من الکریم الا الکرم⟫

The merciful cannot help but show mercy.

So then now what is it that I can do. What can I possible do. for the one who has ABSOLUTELY no need of me?.  The only thing I CAN do. is be grateful to him. That's the ONLY thing I can do in return. for EVERYTHING he has blessed me with. To be grateful to him. Now I think. How do I be grateful to him?. How can I express MY gratitude to him?. The ONLY way I can express my gratitude to him is by fulfill the purpose he created me for. So now what is my purpose?. I mean I must have a purpose. If everything around me . for me. has been created with a particular purpose. to serve me. then I too must have a purpose. right?. Otherwise it just doesn't make sense. How is it possible that all these mangnificent creations around me. have a purpose to serve me. make life possible for me. feed me. clothe me. give me my sustenance. give me modes of transportation. give me riches. How can it be possible. that they all have a purpose. and I don't?. So then what is my purpose?.

So now I start thinking about my own existence. and I begin witnessing the universe within myself. I see that I have a body. with different parts. internal as well as external. And they too are bound. Just like all the other creation outside of me. I can see. but it has limits. I cannot see beyond a certain point. I can hear but it has limits. I can speak but to a certain distance. I can reach out with my hands. but to a certain limit. I can step but ONLY a certain amount. I am restricted. I am confined. I am bound by design. just like every other creation. I can walk. but I can't fly. And then I see that some unseen force is controlling my body. And I could not be my body because if I were. I would not be able to control it. The car doesn't drive itself . it needs a driver. planes don't fly themselves. they need a pilot. the car can't make decisions of where to turn.  and when to accelerate.  and when to brake. it needs the driver to make those decisions for it. So then who is controlling my body. Making decisions for it. What to see. what to hear. what to say. where to go. what to pickup. My body must have an operator. I must have a soul. And then I see . that my body is completely subservient to my soul. It does not refuse a command. If my soul commands the body to jump into the fire. the body will not object to it. It will comply. The body is in COMPLETE submission to my soul. Just as I saw that the universe around me is in complete submission to its purpose. WOW!. That's incredible. Why did the creator. design ALL of his creation this way. It must be to tell me something. I must have a purpose. I must be valuable. There must be some meaning to my edistence. And so what conclusion do I reach?.

⟪ar-quote:رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا⟫

Oh Master. You did not create all of this in vain. You did not create all of this without a purpose. There is no way all of this is useless.

⟪ar-quote:سُبْحَنَكَ⟫

You are WAY above that. to create all of this for nothing. I as a human being. I don't create a simple pen. a paper. a table a chair. for no reason. Even as an insignificant human being. I have a purpose behind every invention that make. There's no way possible. that someone as glorious as yourself. could create all of this for nothing. ⟪ar:سُبْحَنَكَ⟫. You are too exalted for that. There is no way all of this that I see. around me. and inside me. there is no way this does not have meaning. Now what did we say earlier?.  When something has meaning. What is it called?.  When something has meaning. and value and purpose. what is it called? . It's called an ayah. I came to the conclusion. that everything around me. including myself. we are all ayaats. we are all signs of Allah . SubhanAllah. I reach this conclusion. just by having a sound mind. Haven't heard a word of revelation yet. Just by reflecting on the heavens and the earth. I got to that conclusion.

⟪ar-quote:رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَذَا بَطِلًۭا⟫

Master. I see all your ayaats. I see your signs. And I see ALL your signs pointing to one thing. and one thing only. Submission. Islam. I finally understand. You have created me for submission. There is no way I was created created simply to enjoy all of this without an actual goal?. Therefore I too need to submit to my purpose. I need to submit to you. just like every other creation is submitting to its purpose. and submitting to you. I need to do the same.

Now I think. Submit what?. Oh Wait. I just realized there is ONE particular difference between me and ALL of the remaining creation. I HAVE something. they don't. I realize my creator granted me something. that he hasn't granted ANYONE else.  I have FREE WILL. I have the ability to go in both directions. I can DO something. but I can also NOT do something IF I CHOSE not to. I have a CHOICE. I can CHOOSE to do good. I can CHOOSE to do evil. A lion gets angry. if it gets provoked. it'll tear you apart. It's not going to try to reason with you. Oh tell me why did you pull my tail. why did you try to stick your fingers up my nostrills. It's not going to ask you that. I'll rip you apart. But when I get angry. I can choose to reason. I can choose to be patient. I can choose to walk the other way. EVEN when I have the right to react. I HAVE CHOICE. No other creation around me has a choice.  I have the choice. I can choose between two goods. and I can choose between two evils. I can choose the greater good. and I can choose the lesser evil. The sun does not have a choice. the moon does not have a choice. the sky . the earth does not have a choice. The mango tree does not have a choice. it HAS to produce mangoes. The rose garden does not have a choice. It has to produce roses. The car doesn't have a choice. it has to steer in the direction the driver wants.

Animals have free will to some extent.  but they are driven by instinct. not intellect. That's why sheeps need a shepherd. A lion will never eat a vegetable. A goat will never eat meat. Their instinct prevents them from doing that. And that's why human beings make the decisions FOR them. But ONLY human beings. have a fully developed intellect. AND the freedom of CHOICE. to direct that intellect in which ever way they want. So now I realize. I AM THE ONLY ONE. who actually has the freedom of choice. I have free will. OMG. What a GIFT. What an AMAZING GIFT. What an HONOR. What an honor has been given to me by my creator. to be able to CHOOSE. without force. without compulsion.

Then I start thinking about the impact of disobedience. Disobedience to one's purpose. I see that if the sun moves off of its orbit. it will destroy the universe. The car steers in the wrong direction. it'll have an accident. The sky stops its rain. the earth gets destroyed. the earth dies. all life on earth dies. Every disobedience of the creations around me. If they disobey their purpose. if they do anything other than what they have been commanded to do. it has a direct impact. If my body did not obey my soul. I would not even be able to get off my bed. So then that means. my disobedience. to my purpose. must also have an impact. It must also have an impact on my soul. Because I AM my soul. I am NOT my body. I abuse my body. I will see its effect on my body. Which means if I abuse my soul. that must have a negative impact on it too.

So then even though I do have free will. even though I do have freedom of choice. I need to use that freedom to choose what is good for my soul. And I need to choose that good. EVERY single time. If I eat junk food all day long. and then once in a while throw in an apple. it's not going to make any difference in my health. will it?. So if I do things. which I'm not supposed to do. and then once in a while do namaaz. or fast once in a while. it couldn't possibly help my soul.  So now I realize. I need to submit my will. FREELY. WILLINGLY. GRATEFULLY. to the commands of my creator. That is the ONLY way I can express my gratitude. for EVERYTHING that he has done for me. Oh Master! You have done SO much for me. I am SO grateful to you. I wanna show you my gratitude. by now doing what YOU want me to do. And not doing what YOU tell me not to do. Because now I understand. that if I do not fulfill my purpose. If I do not do what you created me to do.  there is going to be hell to pay.

⟪ar-quote:فَقِنَا عَذَابَ ٱلنَّارِ⟫

Protect me from the punishment of fire.

I see that my soul is full of desires of this world. My soul is so engrossed in the fleeting pleasures of this world.  I see that I am such a slave to these sensual pleasures. I see evil elements all around me. distracting me. forcing me to turn away from you.  forcing me to turn away from my true purpose.

⟪ar-quote:فَقِنَا عَذَابَ ٱلنَّارِ⟫

protect me from the enticement. from the shiny temptations of this world. Remember our session on fire vs clay?. Protect me from being among those who get distracted by the entertainment. the lust of this world. the shine. the FIRE of this world. Protect me from that which hinders me from fulfililng the purpose you created me for. I want to submit my will to you. but I need your protection. I need your guidance. It is only YOU who can save me from the fire . from the distractions of this world. YOU created this world. YOU created me. Therefore YOU must know what is BEST for me.

⟪ar-quote:رَبَّنَآ إِنَّكَ مَن تُدْخِلِ ٱلنَّارَ فَقَدْ أَخْزَيْتَهُ⟫
