  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:العالم · علم · العالِم · اللہ · العَلیم⟫
  *Note:* Pedagogical: deriving the divine name al-'Alim by analogy from finite human knowing — the cause/effect/attribute relation lifted to the infinite.

### Linguistic analysis of ALAM, ALIM and ALEEM

Now let's look at the meaning of this word. ⟪ar:العالمین⟫. It's singular form is ⟪ar:عالَم⟫which is ⟪ar:اسم مفعول بہ⟫ . it is an object for the subject which is ⟪ar:عالِم⟫. But forget the grammar part. I just want you to look at these two words. Aalam and Aalim. You can see they both have the EXACT same spelling. The only difference between Aal-a-m and Aal-i-m is the fatha and kasra. Other than that they both have the same spelling. And we've seen this science in Arabic a few time before.  that when two words share a common spelling. they have a deep connection in their meaning. Because they both also share the same root word . which is Ilm. knowlege.
⟪ar:عالِم⟫is the one WHO KNOWS. And the ⟪ar:عالَم⟫is THAT which he comes to know of. 
⟪ar:عالِم⟫. the one who knows. is the CASUSE. And ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. this world.  is that WHICH IS KNOWN. its the EFFECT.

See human beings can know many many things. But even with all the knowledge we have gained. we still cannot know everything. We are knowledgable about certain things.  and at the same time we are ignorant of other things. As opposed to Allah who is ⟪ar:علیم⟫. Who is the one with ABSOLUTE knowledge of everything. But there is NO way for human beings to dirctly know Allah. We cannot know what god is. any more than we can know what god isn't. And the reason for that is. that we are speaking of Allah. we are speaking of the INFINITE creator of the heavens and the earth. And just the fact that we understand that Allah is infinite. Infinite means without limit. Imam Jaffar AsSaadiq AS said. ⟪ar:اللہ اکبر من ان یحد و یحسر⟫. Allah is great in the sense that he does not have a boundary and he cannot be confined to comprehension. In other words. Allah cannot be DEFINED. Yet the ONLY way we human beings are capable of understanding things. is THROUGH definition. Because definition is what DEFINES. or gives FINITE-ness to a concept. It limits it. It puts it in a perspective. That is what Intellect or Aqal means. To set a boundary. to confine. So now we have a problem. How do we. as human beings. as creatures of FINITE-ness and DEFINITION. understand a creator who is INFINITE and cannot be defined.

So the ONLY way possible to do that. is by having an intermediary. Like an interpreter. If all you speak is French. and all I speak is English. Then for me to understand what you're saying. I need someone in the middle who understands both languages. Who can take your message in French and then translate that for me in English. right?. And so we human beings. we needed a third entity. that could act as that interpreter. between Allah and us. Something that is DEFINED. and CONFINED in its existence so that WE could understand it. YET reflect the infiniteness of its creator. And that is the ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. That is this world.

### Universe manfiests existence of Allah

So Allah created this ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. which is this universe. so that the  ⟪ar:عالِم⟫could come to know of the ⟪ar:علیم .⟫

You understand?. The one who knows. which is the ⟪ar:عالِم⟫ . He comes to know of Allah who is ⟪ar:علیم⟫ . THROUGH this universe. the ⟪ar:عالَم.⟫In other words. this universe is the medium through which we Muslims have always understood Allah.  We believe in Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala)  because of the overwhelming proofs being manifested by this universe. And that's why to us. the ultimate proof that Allah exists. is because this universe exists. And the simple fact that every created thing needs a creator. A poet says.

⟪ar-quote:وُجُودُہُ لَہُ دَلِیلُ قَاطِع . حَاجَتُ کُلِّ مُحدَثٍ لِصَانِع⟫

The most convincing that he exists. is that every sculpture requires a sculptor
⟪ar-quote:کُل عالَم.  لِی حَاجَّتاً الی العَالِم⟫

Every world. REQUIRES the existence of a knower. Nothing can exist in a passive  state. And therefore the proof.  of how we know Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) . that He exists. is through the Asaar. through the effects creation. Someone asked a beduin.
⟪ar-quote:بِمَ عَرَفتَ رَبُّك؟⟫. How did you come to know of your master? He said.
⟪ar-quote:إن البِعرَةُ تَدُلُّ علی البَعِیر . والرَّوثَةُ تَدُلُّ علی الحمیر . و آثارُ القدم تَدُلُّ علی المَسِیر⟫

he said. The camel dunk shows me that there was a camel there. The donkey dunk tells me that was a donkey there.  Footsteps in the sand tell me that there were people walking by.
⟪ar-quote:فسمآءُ ذاتُ اَبرَاج. والارض ذاتَ الفِجاج. واَبحَرُ ذَاتَ الامواج⟫

So when I look at the sky.  with its perfect constellations.  and the earth with its perfect valleys and travises. And these oceans with all of its waves.
⟪ar-quote:الا تدل علی لطیف الخبیر؟⟫

Doesn't all of this indicate the presence of the lateef and the khabeer?. SubhanAllah! It was SO simple to him. See. we complicate the heck out of things. But the truth is.  existence of Allah IS the MOST CLEAR and MOST MANIFEST truth there is. The athiest says. I wish there was a proof of the existence of ALlah. and the believer replies. I see nothing BUT the proofs of his existence.

So linguistically speaking. that's the meaning of the word ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. That which is known by the ⟪ar:عالِم⟫. in order for him to recognize the ⟪ar:علیم⟫. And that's why WORLD is not the best translation for Alameen. It limits the scope of meaning. If it meant world. then it would just mean nothing other than the world. And the plural form for that would have been ⟪ar:العوالم⟫.  not ⟪ar:العالمین⟫. The word ⟪ar:العالمین⟫ . encompasses a much broader spectrum than just the physical world. Rabb AlAlameen means. that Allah is not just the master of worlds. he is also the master of all the different species. and all the distinct groups of creation. Every group and category that we can think of is an ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. Because again. that is how we human beings operate. we take a bunch of KNOWN things and group them. we classify them. So ⟪ar:العالمین⟫means. all categories . classifications. and groups that exist. It can be ⟪ar:عالم الروحانی، عالم الجِرمانی، عالم الجسمانی⟫.The spiritual world. the galaxies the solar systems . It can be this physical world.  Then if we just zero in on just this physical world. it includes the various sub-domains and kingdoms. for instance. ⟪ar:عالم المعدنیات⟫. the mineral kingdom. ⟪ar:عالم النبتات⟫. plant kingdom.  ⟪ar:عالم الحیوان⟫. All animal life.  including human beings. ⟪ar:عالم الانسان⟫ . And then if you further drill down within the human category. it means ALL kinds of different races. different nations. These are all called.  ⟪ar:عالمین⟫. For instance says. Allah says in the Quran.
⟪ar-quote:يَبَنِىٓ إِسْرَٓءِيلَ ٱذْكُرُوا۟ نِعْمَتِىَ ٱلَّتِىٓ أَنْعَمْتُ عَلَيْكُمْ وَأَنِّى فَضَّلْتُكُمْ عَلَى ٱلْعَلَمِينَ⟫

I gave you preference over every other nation. and the word used for nations here is Alameen.  It can also means different generations across time.
⟪ar-quote:قُلْ آمَنَّا بِٱللَّهِ وَمَآ أُنزِلَ عَلَيْنَا وَمَآ أُنزِلَ عَلَىٰٓ إِبْرَهِيمَ وَإِسْمَعِيلَ وَإِسْحَقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ وَٱلْأَسْبَاطِ⟫

Say, "We have believed in Allah and what has been revealed to us and what has been revealed to Abraham and Ismaeel and Ishaq and Yaqoob and his Descendants. Now these are all separate and distinct generations. father after son. but collectively they ALL represent ⟪ar:عالمین⟫. So it also includes the meaning of different time periods. And so when Allah calls himself Rabb Alalameen. What he's saying is that no matter what category. what group. what sub-group. you come to know of. You will see my Rububiyyah at work. in ALL of them.

And this is a concept we also find in the English language. So I guess the translation "WORLD" is not completely wrong if you take it in the broader sense. For example. if you talk to a senior gentleman. whose 80 years old.  If you ask him. tell me what life was when you were young. and he will begin by saying. Oh! it was a different world. Ever here that?.  You visit a different country. People who lived all their lives in the US. when they visit third world countries for the first time. they say.  This is a different world.  had no idea people could live like this as well.

I work in NY and so I'm used to a certain type of culture. I visited TX a few years ago and even St. louis. People are actually nice. they're REALLY nice. It's a different world. They actuall say weird things.  like Good morning! and How are you doing today. It's VERY strange. In NY somebody walks up to you and say.  hey good morning. how are you doing?. YOU RUN!. MAN! You run like the wind. Or pull out your pepper spray and go psssss. or whatever. HAHA

In other words. doesn't matter what civilization you belong to. Doesn't matter which culture you belong to.  I am the master of ALL of them. I am Rabb Alalameen. I don't just have ownership and authority over YOU . I don't just nurture YOU. take care of YOU. protect YOU. with love and kindness. I don't just shower blessings and gifts on YOU. I don't just maintain YOUR existence and put YOU to proper use. I do that for ALL of my creation EVERY created thing.

---

Interpreations of Rabb Al-Alameen

Now scholars have given many many beautiful interpretations of this word. Alameen. and why Allah called himself Rabb Alalameen. I'll only share a couple with you otherwise we'll be talking about this for months.

The first is that by saying Rabb Al-Alameen. Allah points out. that because it is He who created different cultures. different creations.  diffferent civilizaitons. people of different languages. Because He alone is the master of all of them. you don't have to be like anyone else.  You can just be who you are.  You don't have to look a certain way. dress a certain way. walk a certain way. talk a certain way.  You can just be yourself. That's fine.  I love you JUST the way you are.  because you are MY slave just as much as the next creation.  I will gave you guidance. and as long as you accept yourself as my slave. and follow my guidance . you can be happy living in whatever culture or civilization or society or country you're in. Because all cultures. all civilizations. all nations are honored by Allah.

The second implication here. and the more important one. when you interact with the people in life. regardless of race or religion. Don't forget that Allah is Rabb AlAlameen. You know why that's important?. Because if you hurt them. if you break their heart with your words. If you torture them with the authority I have temporarily given you over them. You better not forget. I am Rabb AlAlameen. And not just human beings. Even animals. Even plants. Even this earth. Before you're cruel to them. you better remember . I am their Rabb too.

When a slave gets hurt by someone.  who gets insulted ultimately?. The master!.  In the olden days. wars would start because the member of one tribe unjustly hurt or killed the slave of another tribe. His master took that as a personal insult. why? Because he disrespected his property. Slave is his masters responsibility.  Even if the slave was in the wrong. and deserved to be repremanded. Who should the complaint be taken to? His master.

So Allah says. I am Rabb AlAlameen. be careful how you interact with my creation. No matter what group.  what religion.  what cast.  what belief system.  what country they belong to. No matter what your relationship with them is on this earth. Doesn't matter. Before he's your son.  he's MY slave. Before she's your daughter. she's my slave. Before he's your father. before she's your mother. they are MY slaves. Before she's your daughter in law. she's my slave. Before he is your son-in-law. he is my slave. No matter what the relationship. Don't forget.  I am here! and I'm watching. If you treat them unjustly. if you hurt them. if you mentally torture them. insult them. degrade them. If you misuse your authority over them. You will have to answer to ME!!!. Because I am Rabb Alameen. SubhanAllah!

Now here is the most beautiful meaning in my opinion. And this again connects back with the concept of us accepting and submitting to him as his slaves. Scholars say. what this title ⟪ar:رب العلمین⟫ does.  is it bring us all down on the same level in the eyes of Allah.  ALL of us are slaves. No nation. No one group is better than another. And if it is better. it is ONLY by whose standards?. It is in the eyes of who?. In the eyes of the master.

### Humility of Rasul Allah(Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam)

This is something I really want you to take away from today's session. If you forget everything else. I just want you to remember this. Because in todays world we are afflicted with this disease of superiority. and this feeling of having a chip on our shoulders whether we admit to it or not.

Superiority in ranks. can only exist through the eyes of the master. based on the servitude of a slave. NOT through the eyes of the slave. ⟪ar:إِنَّ أَكْرَمَكُمْ عِندَ اللَّهِ أَتْقَاكُمْ⟫. The most honorable in the eyes of Allah. is the one who is the most pious. That's it. Not by anything else. Because even the HIGHST ranking person is Allah's slave. and even the LOWEST ranking person is Allahs save.⟪ar:اشھد ان محمد عبدہ و رسولہ⟫. I testify that Muhammad (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) is his SLAVE and his messenger. AllahuAkbar. The highest ranking person. who has EVER walked this earth. WE testify. in every salaah. that he is the SLAVE of Allah. Then what right do WE have.  to claim superiority OVER each other. or people of other sects and religions? . If we believe that we hold any superiority on the basis of our creed. THAT superiority has to be by the standards of Allah. NOT us!!. We can't make that judgment for other slaves. Allah is the master of a sulemani.  just as much as he is a master of a sunni.  of a shia. of a hindu.  of a christian.  of a jew. even an athiest. Allah is the ultimate master.

And if Allah is the master.  and we are ALL his slaves.  Who is the ONLY one who can judge a slave's rank?. ONLY the master!. right?. Can one slave stand before his master and say to another slave. You are a disgusting person.  You are horrible. You are beneath me.  I am better than you because you drink and I don't. or I pray 5 times a day and you dont. Allah loves me more than you?.  NO. That is not up to the slave.!!! .

But can a slave help another slave?. If one slave has received guidance. he understands it. he has been blessed by his master.  can he help another slave?. Can he try to guide the other slave?. If not . can he at least pray for the other slave. of course he can. But to act all high and mighty.

BTW. Has that ever happened in the past? Does the Quran tell us of such an incident. when one slave tried to judge another slave? .

⟪ar-quote:أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ . خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ⟫

I am BETTER than him. I am created from fire. he is created from clay. Do you remember who said that?.  Iblees! Iblees was an angel. from the ⟪ar:عالَم⟫of angels. Adam was a human being. from the ⟪ar:عالَم⟫of Insaan. They were both slaves of Allah. And Iblees stood before Allah.  He stood before the Rabb Alameen. and said.  ⟪ar:أَنَا۠ خَيْرٌۭ مِّنْهُ خَلَقْتَنِى مِن نَّارٍۢ وَخَلَقْتَهُۥ مِن طِينٍۢ⟫. I am better than him.

And what do we learn in that story. What did his master do?. Did his arrogance bring him closer to Allah. or did it get him removed from his divine presence?.  Do you really think that an act that Iblees was punished for. Allah would let it slide for you and I?. Would that befit his justice?. That he punishes Iblees for his arrogance. remove him from his divine presence. and then bring us closer to him?.

Because you have to understand. When you and I judge each other. When you and I as SLAVES. judge OTHER slaves in terms of superiority. what position do we place ourselves in?. We put ourselves in the position of our Rabb. Now does the Quran ALSO tell us of someone who did that?. Didn't someone say. ⟪ar:انا ربکم الاعلی⟫. I am your GREATEST Rabb. Who said that?. Firon said that. How did he end up?.

And the reality is that Firon KNEW that he was human. He knew he was not a Rabb. Because he was aware of his weakness. and despite that he claimed a station he was not worthy of. You know. He did not like the fact that he needed to go to the toilet. Because that was not befitting a Rabb. So he got all of  his physicians together and he asked them how do I get out of this problem.  and so they told him to eat bananas.  So he ate bananas for 40 days.  and then he had a much bigger problem. 

And so we REALLY have to be CONSTANTLY aware of this. Because this today.  is not just a Fironic problem. This has become a GLOBAL problem. Everyone wants to become Ilah. everyone wants to become Mabood. There are people who WANT to be worshiped. and these are the people that Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala)  addresses and says

⟪ar-quote:وَلَقَدْ خَلَقْنَا ٱلْإِنسَنَ مِن سُلَلَةٍۢ مِّن طِينٍۢ⟫

 you are from some chain of dirt.  of mud and water mixed together.

⟪ar-quote:ثُمَّ جَعَلَ نَسْلَهُۥ مِن سُلَلَةٍۢ مِّن مَّآءٍۢ مَّهِينٍۢ ‎⟫

 we created your progeny from a vial fluid.  who do you think you are?.  Allah tells these people. Get down off your high horse!!!. Be a rajul. Rajul is the one that has ⟪ar:ِرَجَلَ⟫.

⟪ar:ِرَجَلَ عن فَرِسِہ⟫. Rajul is the one who comes down.  off of his high horse…. And gets to the earth….  and puts his feet on the ground. Doesn't see himself raised up above the earth. He comes down to the level that he came from.  from dust. Thats ⟪ar:الرجل⟫.  And all of these other people are just playing games.  trying to be Ilah. and Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala)  says NO!. Be a Rajul. be banee adam. be Adamee.  THAT is TRULY accepting the station of Rabbul Alameen. Humility. NOT arrogance.

But it is the nature of human being. that as soon as he gets a blessing. he becomes arrogant. We immediately jump on our high horses. Oh you know. I run the Sunday Sessions. Who are you to tell me anything. Who are you to give me advise. How dare you?.  This is PURE arrogance. The fact that Allah HONORED me. a slave. to be in this position where I am now being able to benefit others. this VERY honor should ground me in humility. Not arrogance.  Because I am a SLAVE. This Rububiyyah is an HONOR given to me by master. by my Rabb. It's a burden. And the evidence of the fact.  that I truly am viewing this responsibility as a burden. is that you will see it bend my back. When you carry a bruden on your back.  do you bend forward or do you walk upright?. The burden makes you bend. it makes you humble. And this is why HUMILITY is the essence of spiritual progress. Hazrat Ibraheem sahab's words are ringing in my ears right now. The one who is the most humble. will rise the highest. If you want to climb a mountain. how will you climb it?. By bending forward in humility. or by walking upright?. And this is why the HIGEST ranking person in this world. my beloved Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) . of ALL the prophecies that predicted his arrival. THE GREATEST MARK of his prophethood. was his HUMILITY.

⟪ar-quote:یُریدُ أَنَّ یَبعَثُ أُمِیِّ مِنَ الأُمِّیِّن۔⟪ar-quote:وأجعل السكينةَ لباسُهُ ، والبِرَّ شَعارُهُ ، والتقوى ضَميرَهُ ، والحِكمَةَ مَنطِقَهُ ، والصِّدقَ والوفاءَ طَبِيعَتُهُ ، والعَفوَ وَالمَعرُوفَ خُلقُهُ ، والَحقَّ شَريعَتَهُ ، والعَدلَ سيرَتَهُ ، والهَدِىُ إمامُهُ ، والإسلامَ مِلَّتُهُ ، وأحمد أِسمُهُ .  أَهدِي بِهِ بَعدَ الضَّلالَة ، وأعلَمُ بِهِ مِنَ الجَهالة ، وأَرفَعُ به بعد الخَمالَة ، وأعرِفُ به بعد النَّكِرَة ، وأكثَرُ بِهِ بعدَ القِلَّة ، وأغنِي به بعد العَيلَة ، وأَجمِعُ به بعد الفُرقَة .  وأُؤَلِّفُ به بين أممٍ مُتَفَرِّقَة وَقُلُوبٍ مُختَلِفَة ، وأَهواءٌ متشَتَّتَة⟫⟫

Allah revealed all of these incredible signs. that would help nations. identify him. But the GREATEST OF ALL.

⟪ar-quote:لَو یَمشِی عَلی القَصَبِ الیَابِس۔۔۔ لَم یُسمَع مِن تَحتِ قَدَمَیہِ مِن سَکِینَتِہِ⟫

You will see him walk with SUCH humility. that if he walked on dry leaves.  you would not hear the sound of them cracking under his feet. If you want to know why this slave. Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) gained the honor he achieved from his master. It is through ONE thing. HUMILITY!. And that is what identifies a true believer from a hypocrite. HUMILITY. And this is why atheism.  is such a blatant form of arrogance. Because the atheist is rejecting something that is the most obvious.  and the most fundamental aspect of his existence. That he was creatED. Because even he cannot say that he was not created. Now if I say that my father created me and  and his father created him before him. That's what they call Dawr. that's tasalsul.  it just keeps on going back. And then where do you stop.  If it stops at Adam.  then who created him?.  because that's where the buck stops.

⟪ar-quote:وکُلُّکُم مِن آدَم. وَ آدَم مِن تُرَاب⟫

All of you are from Adam.  and Adam is from dust. And arrogance doesn't befit the dirt. because it is constantly trampled upon.

Maulana Ali saw a man acting arrogantly and he said to him. Who do you think you are?. You beginning is a vile dirty fluid. You end is disgusting decaying smelling corpse. And in between those two stages. you walk through life carrying two loathsome thing within your body. your urine and your feces. And your creation is the result of the union of two ugly body parts. What right do you have to act arrogantly before Allah and his creation?. 

And so this is the first thing.  to know our station in this world.  to know who we are. We are Marboob.  We are created.  We will die.  We will be raised up.  THIS understanding.  that we are Marboob.  THIS is the station of the slave.  of knowing that I am NOT Mabood…. I am not the creator….

Wallahi I give you sincere advise. I advise you and I advise my own soul. because this is something we do ALL the time. I have made this mistake so many times in my previous life. when I did not understand these realities. May Allah forgive me for those crimes. And I try to constantly keep myself in check on this matter. even though I still do make mistakes. But I do try to keep returning to this station of humility. And I give you kids the same advise. Because arrogance is the azaan. it is the CALL of our times today. Arrogance is what we are CONSTANTLY being called to in all walks of life. In School. in college. at work. in families. It's ALL about. Life has become all about. I am better than you. And that does not befit an obedient slave.

If we just get this bit. If we really understand the true meaning of Rabb AlAlameen. this world would become such a beautiful place. If we all understood that it is Allah the Rabb Alalmeen who guides everyone. he is the king. he is the owner. he is the one who cares. he is the one who guides. he is the one who gives gifts. then everything about my life is between me and him. He will take care of me. I just need to worry about anything. I don't need to judge another slave. I don't need to hurt another slave. I don't need to show my authority or power over another slave. EVEN if I am hurt. EVEN if I am wronged. ESPECIALLY if I have been wronged. Because my master will take care of me. My master will come for my rescue. he will come to my defense on the day of judgment. And he WILL make that wrong right. He will stand behind me and support me. I don't need to worry about anything. Because wheter we believe it or not. wheter we want to or not. that day is coming. when the Rabb will gather everyone and exact justice.

⟪ar-quote:رَبَّنَآ إِنَّكَ جَامِعُ ٱلنَّاسِ لِيَوْمٍۢ لَّا رَيْبَ فِيهِ ۚ⟫

Oh our master. Indeed you will gather all of us on a day. about which there is ABSOLUTELY NO DOUBT. Because YOU have promised us that.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ لَا يُخْلِفُ ٱلْمِيعَادَ⟫

No doubt. Allah never goes against his promise.

Remind yourself of this EVERY time you recite the Fateha. There's a reason we pray 51 rakaats in one day. and all 51 times we recite Fateha. So that every time we say Rabb Alalameen. we remind ourselves of this hierarchy. Who He is and who we are in this relationship.

⟪ar:وآخر الدعوانا عن الحمد للہ رب العالمین⟫

---

### Man gave Rasul Allah bottle of wine as gift

There was this man who travelled a long distance to meet Rasul Allah (Salawaat). and when he met him. he gave the messenger a bottle of wine. as a gift. He said Ya RasulAllah. I got this special wine as a gift for you. What would we do if someone did that?. If someone. very secularized. shows up at your doorstep with a bottle of wine. as a house warming gift. what how would we react?. La hawla wala quwwata. How dare you. Don't you know I'm a Muslim. Don't you know this is haraam?. Get the hell out of my house. never show me your face again. right?.

And who did this man bring the wine bottle to? . Rasul Allah!!!!. The MOST pious man we can imagine. And you know how he responded?. He smiled. He smiled and said. Brother. Did you not hear Allah's command that alcohol has been prohibited?. He said.  No Rasul Allah. I never heard that!. He immediately gives the bottle to his slave and says something in his ears. Rasul Allah says. what did you just say to him?. The man said. I told him to sell the bottle in the market. Rasul Allah smiled again and said. The one who has prohibitted the consumption of intoxicants has also forbidden its trade. So the man told the slave to dump it out. This is the character of Rasul Allah. This is his humility. This is the Tarbiyyah. his rububiyyah. SubhanAllah! . He didn't say. Don't you know who I am. How dare you bring this filth in my presence. He NEVER did that. Because hearts can NEVER be conquered with harshness. Hearts have always been conquered ONLY with love. and kindness. We should really study. and learn what kind of a Rabb. what kind of a parent. what kind of teacher our prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam)  was. SubhanAllah.

<!-- section 5 (id=5755, raw_sort=5): Gratitude TO Allah -->

## Section 5755

Meaning of wisdom

We're studying the second ayah of the basmallah. ⟪ar:الحمد للہ رب العلمین⟫.  We've looked at the words. Allah, Rabb and Alameen. Today I want to begin discussing the word Hamd. and how it is connected to the words ⟪ar:رب العلمین⟫. Hamd in classical Arabic means two things. It means GRATITUDE and it means PRAISE. Once again. Hamd means gratitude and it also means praise. There is a difference between the two. Gratitude is the quality of being thankful. when something nice is done for you. Praise is admiration for something  amazing or something brilliant. Hamd means both these things at the same time. We'll do a linguistic analysis of the word Hamd in later sessions. Today I just want to talk about gratitude.which in itself is a HUGE HUGE topic. So we'll only be able to cover a portion of this today. In the next session we'll pick up. where we leave off today InshaAllah.

Allah says in the Quran.
⟪ar-quote:وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ . أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ.⟫

And We had certainly given Luqman wisdom. "Be grateful to Allah!". Luqman is the wisest man of his time.
⟪ar-quote:وَمَن يَشْكُرْ فَإِنَّمَا يَشْكُرُ لِنَفْسِهِ⟫

And whoever is grateful. no doubt his gratitude ONLY benefits himself.
⟪ar-quote:وَمَن كَفَرَ فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَنِىٌّ حَمِيدٌۭ⟫

And whoever is ungrateful. denies Allah's favor. then indeed, Allah is Free of all need and is praiseworthy.

Let's look at this first ayah. Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ . أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ⟫

We have certainly granted Luqman wisdom.

Those of you who don't know the story. Hazrat Luqman was a black man from Sudan who lived before the time of Moosa AS. I think around 1100 BC. He was a very perceptive man. One day while he was asleep under a tree, an angel came to him and said. Allah wants to bestow a gift upon you. Either wisdom. or prophethood. And Luqman chose wisdom. When he woke up from his sleep. he realized that his senses were hightened. and his understanding had become sharpened. He suddenly felt in complete harmony with nature. and he could understand the inner meaning of things. beyond their physical reality. When he realized this. he immediately fell into sajda. and thanked and praised Allah for his wonderful gift. He did two things. He thanked Allah for the gify he was given. And he praised Allah for the things he was now becoming aware of by the use of his gift.

He was then later captured by slavers. and sold as a slave. Scholars say this was his first trial. His training in slavery and servitude.He was made a slave so that he could learn how to become the TRUE SLAVE of the divine master. And because of his servitude. his ⟪ar:عبودیۃ⟫. he gained such a status in the eyes of his Rabb. that Allah mentioned him by name in his final message. So Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ⟫

We have certainly granted Luqman. ⟪ar:حکمۃ⟫.  wisdom. Now what is wisdom?. When we think about wisdom what kind of things come to our minds?. Someone very knowledgable. Someone old and with a lot of experience. like Gandof in lord of the ring. Or someone who says EPICLY profound things. that when you hear them. you go. WOAH. I don't even know what you just said. But that was so deep man!!. That sort of thing? . So most people have this fuzzy idea of what wisdom means. right?

One of the most amazing things about the ancient Arab culture. is that they loved to simplifying things . They loved simplicity. And they had this  super simple definition of the word wisdom. that I want to share with you. Their definition of wisdom was this.
You are wise. when you have correct knowledge. and you act upon it. That's it. Two simple parts to wisdom. Part one. Gain beneficial or correct knowledge. And part two. act upon it. When these two things come together. that actually means that you have wisdom. It's not something fuzzy or wooo hooo. It's not an epic quote. It is something practical. To the Arabs wisdom is a practical thing.

Now let's put that to the test to understand what they mean by that. Here's a correct or beneficial knowledge. Fire burns. That is correct knowledge. That is beneficial knowledge. So wisdom would mean. that you did not stick your hand in the fire. Based on your knowledge that fire burns. if you did not stick your hand in the fire. young man.  you have acted wisely. You chose wisely young samurai. Because you acted on the knowledge that you have.

Okay.  let's take it a step further. Smoking can cause all sorts of health issues. Eventually even lung cancer. This too is correct knowledge. As a result of this knowledge what do you decide to do?. You choose not to smoke. If you make that decision. you are acting wisely. Speeding on a highway recklessly can cause a crash. You can kill yourself.  your friends and other innocent people that have nothing to do with your ridiculousness. That's pretty good knowledge. So now if you're not cutting through traffic. not creating your own version of Fast and Furious 8. trying to cut past that bus when it's about to take an exit . That's a pretty wise decision.

Now allah says.⟪ar:وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ⟫. We gave Luqman wisdom. which means Luqman has two things. On the one hand he has beneficial knowledge. and on the other.  whatever knowledge he has.  he puts it to practical use. He acts upon it. His knowledge somehow changes the way he thinks. It changes the way he makes a decision. And this is very important for us all to understand as well. Because at the end of the day what is most demanded by the Quran. especially from the youth. is NOT knowledge. It's WISDOM.  Because at your age studying is easier. memorizing is easier. retaining is easier. taking a test is easier. In fact if I had to go back to school and study the stuff that you guys are studying today. and try to take the same tests that you guys take. I will do horribly in comparison to you guys. why?.  Because I am not in student mode anymore. My mind isn't as sharp as it was when I was a teenager. So gaining knowledge is VERY easy for you guys. But what is hard to do?. Acting upon it. isn't it?. This means that even though knowledge can be acquired at an earlier stage. what takes time to develop. is Wisdom. Because you may learn a lot about the Quran. but you don't really know how to use it yet. Wisdom hasn't completely settled in yet. And so in order for us to develop wisdom. we need to start APPLYING the teachings of Quran in our practical day to day life. We need to start putting it into action. In these sessions we are gaining knowledge. Once the session is over. what do we have to do?. We have to find a way to ACT upon it. Otherwise what's the point?. If we just acquire this knowledge and we do nothing with it.

⟪ar:کمثل حمار یحمل اسفارا⟫

as Allah says in Surah Jumuah. These people are like a donkey carries a huge load of books on its back. But do those books actually benefit the donkey?. No. So the goal of these sessions. or any knowledge for that matter. is not to carry its burden on our backs. but to actually benefit from it. And how do you benefit from it?. By putting it into action. which is the TRUE goal of the Quran. The goal of the Quran is wisdom!

### Gratitude

Now Allah is saying. We gave Luqman  wisdom. And what is the pinnacle. wha is the climax of all of his wisdom?.  Check this out. ⟪ar:أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ⟫ . Be grateful to Allah. Be grateful to Allah. I want you to understand this part. Allah did not say. We gave wisdom to Luqman TO BE grateful to Allah. or. We gave wisdom to Luqman SO THAT he could be grateful to Allah.  Rather. We gave Luqman wisdom. BE grateful to Allah!!. Now what's the difference between the two?. When your mom tells you. DO YOUR HOMEWORK!. Is it a suggestion?. Is it a request?. Or is it a command?. It's a command!. Allah. after granting Luqman wisdom. he's not suggesting to him to be grateful. He is commanding him to be grateful. Which means Luqman understood.  that being grateful is obligatory. It is not something that is just nice to do. it is not something you do once in a while. It's not something you kinda sorta should do. He realized this is something he ABSOLUTELY must do. That is captured grammatically inside  ⟪ar:أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ⟫. In other words. at the end of his life. At the end of all of life's experiences that Luqman had. He realized just one thing. That BEING GRATEFUL. IS THE ULTIMATE WISDOM. Gratitude IS the ultimate wisdom. SubhanAllah!.

You will find people in life. who have a LOT of knowledge about the Quran. But even though they have knowledge. they don't ACT upon it. which means they don't have wisdom. You can be super knowledgable. but still not be wise. And what lies at the heart of wisdom, is gratitude. So the idea is. the more knowledgable we get in this religion. the more wise we're supposed to get by acting upon that knowledge. And the wiser we get. the more Grateful we should become to Allah (Azza Wa Jal). That is the purpose of the Quran.

Then the ayah continues. 

⟪ar-quote:وَمَن يَشْكُرْ فَإِنَّمَا يَشْكُرُ لِنَفْسِهِ⟫

The one who is grateful. is only . actually . truly grateful for himself. For his own benefit. If you are being grateful. who is it that you are benefitting?.  You!. You are becoming a more happier person. You're becoming a more satisfied person. You're making the most of what you have in your life. You're not constantly looking at what you did not get or what you do not have. Or what you could have had. You are actually taking advantage of what you actually DO have. The glass is never half-empty for you. it is always half full for you. In other words. being grateful. in a sense is now the same as being positive. And by being positive you are only helping yourself. you are only improving the quality of your own life.

There are numerous TED talks about the stuff today. That how becoming grateful and satisfied for what you do have. tremendously increases the quality of your life. You will lead a more happier fulfilling life. They are discovering all of this now. and everyone is like this is such an EPIC discovery. and the Quran is stating this 1400 years ago. Listen! if you are going to be grateful it is only going to help you.

This BTW. is one of the first and foremost things about beliving in Allah. Belief in Allah. is not just talking about our belief in his existence. Or a belief in someone with divine powers who does everything. who created the universe. who created us. who is controlling all things. That is not enough. That is just the knowledge surrounding belief. The fruit or the result of belief. is us developing certain kinds of attitudes. And the first attitude that the Quran talks about. is gratitude. We become someone who develop a positive outlook in life. We become appreciative. We always see value in the things around you. even in bad situations.

Hazrat Luqman's master. he was a very rich man. And he respected hazrat Luqman so much. that he treated him as a great friend and a companion. to the point. that he made it a practice. that whenever he had something special to eat, he would first feed Hazrat Luqman from it. and THEN eat the leftover. Is that crazy or what?. But you know what we learn from this?. Wisdom is such an amazing thing. that it can turn a slave into a master. and a master into a slave. Where on earth would you see a master. who would eat from his slaves leftovers?. But this is the kind of love and respect. hazrat Luqman generated in the heart of his master. simply through his wisdom.

Anyway. one day during watermelon season. someone gave his master a watermelon. He calls Luqman (AS). and then he slices the melon. and starts offering hazrat Luqman one slice after another. Luqman starts eating the slices with great pleasure. and as he's eating them he's expressing his gratitude to his master and singing his praises. The more he praised his master. the more his master gave to Luqman. Why is that?. In life. when you are grateful. when you are appreciative of someone. does that increase their affection towards you or reduce it?. It obviously increases it right?. When we are grateful to Allah for his gifts. when we are appreciative of Allah's gifts. will that increase his affection for us or decrease it?. Even though this is the story of a slave. hazrat luqman and his master. it contains a wealth of wisdom for us. about our relationship as slaves with our master.

Anyway. so the master is handing hazrat luqman the slices. and as he's eating them. he's praising his master and expressing his gratitude to him. Which in turn makes the master so happy that he keeps handing Luqman (AS) one slice after another. Finally when there is one slice left. his master thinks. Let me also try one slice of this delicious melon. So he takes a bite from that last slice. That slice was SO horribly bitter. that his master almost choked. Some narrations say that he passed out. When he gained back his senses he asked Luqman. How have you been eating these slices with such a smile on your face. praising me and expressing gratitude all this time?. This thing is more bitter than poison!!.

Hazrat Luqman replies. Oh generous master. from your hands I have received hundreds of beautiful gifts. The burden of your gratitude upon me breaks my back. So I felt ashamed. that the hand that granted me the sweetness of so many favors. if one day. some bitterness should come, how could I turn away from it?. O master!. the pleasure of knowing that it comes from your hands. changed the bitterness of the melon to sweetness!”. SubhanAllah! . You see. THIS. is true gratitude!!!.

At every single moment of our lives. we are surrounded by Allah's blessings. But when one thing doesn't go our way. we turn on our master. So Allah says. We gave Luqman wisdom. It is Allah who gave Luqman wisdom. He did not acquire it himself. Allah gave it to him. And then he commanded him.  ⟪ar:أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ⟫. Be grateful to Allah!.

### Ingratitude

⟪ar-quote:وَمَن يَشْكُرْ فَإِنَّمَا يَشْكُرُ لِنَفْسِهِ⟫

The one who is grateful. is only being grateful for himself. The true ESSENCE of belief. is gratitude. And by the way. guess what the opposite of gratitude is. in Arabic?. In English it is ingratitude.  Do you know what the opposite of Shukr is? . Its very interesting. It's Kufr. What is another meaning for that word Kufr?. Disbelief. So to the arabs. disbelief AND ingratitude. are one and the same thing. There's no difference between the two for them. Someone who is not grateful. he might as well not even be a believer. Why?. Because the first thing that happens as a result of you being a believer. is that you become grateful. you become positive. And this is why the first words of the Quran in Surah AlFateh are what?. Alhamdulillah. If we don't learn this one lesson. we haven't learnt anything from the Quran. We really need to internalize this. And then Allah continues and says.

⟪ar-quote:وَمَن كَفَرَ فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَنِىٌّ حَمِيدٌۭ⟫

And whoever is ungrateful. then certainly Allah is free of all need. and he is praised in and of himself. Now this is a very powerful statement made by Allah. So let's try to understand what he saying here. Allah is saying he does not NEED you to be grateful to him. In fact he does not need you for anything. People asked this silly question. Why does Allah need me to be grateful anyway?. Why does he constantly need my gratitude?. ACTUALLY. he needs ABSOLUTELY nothing from you. because he is ⟪ar:غنی⟫. ⟪ar:غنی⟫mean someone who is completely independent. who has no need of anyone and anything. In fact the only one who does actually have a need. is us!. We dont' thank him for every breadth. but he still provides it . We don't thank him for every single heartbeat. but he still allows it. We dont' thank him for every blood vessel that is filling up with blood. but he's still doing it for us. The fact that we are able see and blink. the fact that we are not overwhelmed with pain in every pore of our skin. ALL of that is from Allah.

And despite the fact that we not necessarily grateful to him. nor do we constatnly express our gratitude to him . but he still provides these things for us . So the fact of the matter is. if there is anyone who deserves gratitude. it's him. And no matter how much we think we pray to him. how much we try to carry out our religious duties. in the grand scheme of things. we CANNOT TRULY EVERY thank him. So we can't think . even for a second . that we have in fact done the job of thanking Allah. because that is not EVER going to be the case. We are NEVER EVER going to be able to thank Allah for what he does for us. Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:وَآتَىٰكُم مِّن كُلِّ مَا سَأَلْتُمُوهُ.  وَإِن تَعُدُّوا۟ نِعْمَتَ ٱللَّهِ. لَا تُحْصُوهَآ⟫

We give you everything that you ask of us. And if you were to try to fully understand. fully appreciate. even a single blessing of Allah. you will not be able to do so . You won't be able to fully grasp it . or fully appreciate it. it's just not humanly possible.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ ٱلْإِنسَنَ لَظَلُومٌۭ كَفَّارٌۭ⟫

No doubt about it. human beings are truly unjust. and extremely ungrateful.

Allah is saying. you can't even thank me properly. or thank me completely. for ONE SINGLE favor I have done for you. The favors that you actually see and experience. You can't even be TRULY grateful for that. So then what about.

⟪ar-quote:وَأَسْبَغَ عَلَيْكُمْ نِعَمَهُۥ ظَهِرَةًۭ وَبَاطِنَةًۭ⟫

Allah has unleashed his favors upon you. the ones that are obvious to you. and also the ones that you don't even see. There are so many unseen ways in which Allah is helping us. that we don't even realize. There are ways in which Allah is protecting us in our sleep. We are walking down the street. and around us are insects. that contain deadly toxins. One bite from them could kill us. They're carring deadly viruses and disease. and they buzz right by us by Allahs command. And they bite someone else and they die. and we dont'. And this was not something that was under OUR control. If that was decreed for us. there is nothing we could have done about it . So we don't even know the ways in which Allah is protecting us. He says in the Quran.

⟪ar-quote:وَيُرْسِلُ عَلَيْكُمْ حَفَظَةً⟫

We sent down guardian angels upon you. He literally put angels. that are on full time duty. just to watch upon you. just to take care of you. You're driving your car. perfectly fine. within the speed limit. within your lane.  and there is a drunk driver right next to you. and he can smash into you at anytime. out of no fault of yours. but Allahs angels are protecting you .  We can't even think of the ways in which Allah is protecting us. He's providing for us. He's doing us these constant favors we don't even know anything about. We create delusions of home security. job security. social security. All of which can crumble in a moment. We have seen it happen. All of this is simply a delusion of security. Allah is the one who is truly keeping us safe. So Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:وَمَن كَفَرَ فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَنِىٌّ حَمِيدٌۭ⟫

He does not need you . because he is ghanee. He is self-sufficient. In fact. YOU are the ones who need him. Then he adds the word Hameed. Hameed is somone who is praised. and who is shown appreciation. ALL on his own. In other words. he does not need YOU to show praise and appreciation to him. If no one in the entire world would praise him and show appreciation to him. he would still be worthy of praise. And he would still be worthy of gratitude. If Allah created absolutely nothing. If there were no human beings. no animals. no plants . If there was NOTHING at all in this world . Allah would still be worthy of praise. He would still be worthy of appreciation. He does not need creation to show him gratitude. The only thing OUR gratitude does. is INCREASE his favors upon us. which is simply a part of his justice. Because that's what justice dictates. Give MORE to the appreciative. Give MORE to the grateful. In school. you show appreciation to your teachers. they will automatically try to teach you more. Because you're showing that you appreciate and value what they're doing for you. It'll make them happy to do more for you. But not because they HAVE to!!. They don't. It's ONLY your gratitude. and your appreciation that is attracting their favors more.

Anjum apa once told me that she was teaching her students about how magnets attract metals. And she said that got her thinking. that Allah's justice must be like that. that if you contain certain qualities. certain metals within you. it will automatically be attracted to the magnet which are his blessings. I thought that was a REALLY beautiful example. Gratitude is that metal within us. that attracts Allah's favors. The more gratitude we have. the more strongly we will attract his blessings. Which means that if I feel I am not seeing his favors in my life. then what's missing?. My gratitude is missing.

Now what is gratitude?. We need to understand what gratitude or shukar is. There are two meanings in the statement. ⟪ar:أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ⟫ . The first is. Be grateful TO Allah. And the second is. Be grateful THROUGH the intermediaries of Allah. I'll say that again. Be grateful TO Allah. And the second is be grateful BECAUSE of Allah. or be grateful FOR THE SAKE of Allah.

### definition of lubb

So let's begin by talking about Gratitude TO Allah. in the context of the ulilAlbaab. people of sound essence. Once again. Lubb. the singular form of Albaab. is the kernel inside a nut. or the seed inside a fruit. And because a seed is always PROTECTED and covered from all sides. it's essence remains pure. It does not get influenced by external factors. In other words it maintains its original pure state. That's why UlilAlbaab. are called people of sound essence. because they have protected their hearts from statanic influences. and so they have been able to preserve their original purity. But that also implies. that they started off with some basic purity.right?.

You guys play video games right?. If you've played any RPG type games. Role playing games. The character always begins with some basic capabilities. He can walk. He can jump. He can kick . punch. but these are not at its maximum level yet. It's at a very basic level. And then as he progresses through the game. he posesses additional powers. new equipments. new weapons.  attack combos etc. So now he can jump higher. run faster.  have a three punch combo etc. And then eventurally you can buy. in-app upgrades. and synch everything up to 100%.  and now your character is like fully awesome. Now it's exactly what you always wanted it to be. right?

But when you started the game. your character is kinda weak. but there are still some basic capabilities your character poseses. in order for you to be able to play the game. you understand?  I'm sorry girls. I haven't played any princess games. so I can't make reference to those.

### Fitrah

So according to Islam. EVERY ONE of us.  ALL human beings are created with some basic pre-programmed spiritual capabilities within the Ruh. the soul!. It's called Fitrah. It's those basic capabilities we're all created with in this game of life. That's why Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) said.
⟪ar-quote:مَا مِنْ مَوْلُودٍ إِلَّا يُولَدُ عَلَى الْفِطْرَةِ .⟫

There is not a single child. that is not born upon this pure state "Fitrah",

⟪ar-quote:فَأَبَوَاهُ يُهَوِّدَانِهِ وَيُنَصِّرَانِهِ وَيُمَجِّسَانِهِ⟫

You-havvi-danihi. wa Yu-nassi-raanihi . wa Yu-majji-saanihi

It is then his parents (i.e. external influences) that make him a Jew, Christian or a Zoroastrian. But the original state of a child is pure. You smile at a child. and it will smile back at you. You look at it in anger. and it will start crying. A child never lies. It'll just look at you in the eyes. smile and say. YOU FAT!. You do something nice for the child. it doesn't even know how to say thank you yet. but it'll hug you. or give you a toothless smile. or lick your face. or do something nice.  Because they're all. WE ARE ALL born with this innate capacity to be a decent person. Decency is not something you are upgraded into. Gratitude is not a power you download later. Kindness is not an inapp purchase you have to make later. These are abilities that every human being is born with. This is the stance that Islam takes with the first creation. See Christianity doesn't believe that. They believe that every human being is born in sin. But we Muslims believe. that the starting point of every human being is good. no matter what family or religion they're born into.

And so one of the fundamental proofs of having a sound essence. is that when something nice is done to you. For example. if I do something nice for you. or if you do something nice for me. At the very least what should I do?. I should be grateful to you. I should have that basic decency in me. to say Thank you. I should not require an upgrade for that!. right?. When someone does something nice for us. is kind to us. feeds us.  does us a favor. gives us gifts. we just naturally become grateful to that person.  and we thank him. So gratitude is from those fundamental emotions we are born with.

Another one is. that when we see something beautiful. when we see something amazing. like a beautiful waterfall. or a breadth taking view. when someone shows us something magnificent. we appreciate it. we praise it.  So gratitude and praise. these are from that basic decency that Allah (Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) created us all with.

This is how we saw. that when these people of sound hearts and sound minds. the ulilAlbaab. when they reflects on the creations of the heavens and earth. they become aware of the existence of their Rabb. And they become aware of his ownership and his authority over them. They witness how their Rabb is nurturing them. maintaining them. putting them to their purpose. And how everything within themselves. and outside of them. are designed as ENORMOUS gifts and blessing. from their master. So they accept him as RABB. and in doing so. they submit themselves to him. as his obedient SLAVES.

### Taking blessings for granted

Now in the previous session I told you. that this act of submission. as slaves. is actually an EXTREMELY difficult task. That's why I said. The greatest challenge. that you and I are constantly going to face in life. every waking moment. is accepting that Allah is Rabb and that WE. ARE HIS SLAVES. It's not easy. Especially not in these times that we live in. and especially not for you kids. Why is that?. Because of the amount of luxury and convenience that we all enjoy today. There's no blame here. It's not a bad thing that you have luxuries and comforts. AlHamdulillah for that. I'm simply acknolwedging the fact.  that YES. It IS really very difficult in this day and age for us to TRULY submit ourselves as SLAVES. And that's because we are all surrounded in comforts. And when a master surrounds his slaves in comforts. It's REALLY easy for us to FORGET what?. That we are still slaves.

We have a lot of what we want. at the tip of our fingers. Literally. We can order things online. We can download things. We have the devices to do so. We have the constant connections to do so. And we have all become used to this kind of convenience. We're all slaves of instant gratifications for MOST things in our lives. When we want something. we want it now. And the problem is. MOST of the time. we even get it right now. And so to not have it is just becomes unthinkable. Look at us and phones. and this necessity to constantly be online.  We're literally enslaved to it. For us to spend one hour without internet. it's devestating. As a matter of fact. If I asked all of you kids to turn your phones off right now. some of you would literally go crazy. What?. Turn my phone off?. Are you nuts Asif mamu?. It's bad enough that my parents make me sit for an hour and listen to you. and now I can't even use my phone?. Oh I hate you so much. right?

And you know why this is a problem?. We have become so used to getting things. whenever we want them. that we start believing that we are actually entitled to them. We believe that we actually DESERVE everything that we have. So in moments when these gifts are given to us. it's feel like no big deal. WHATEVER!!!.  Today we live in a world. where our hearts are afflicted with this disease called. "WHATEVER". Your parents says to you. Look how much I love you and how much I do for you. I take care of you. I feed you. I buy you everything you need. And your response is. WHATEVER!. Your response should have been gratitude. but instead it's. WHATEVER!. Why?. Because you feel. so what if you do all this for me. It's NO big deal. You're supposed to do this for me. therefore. WHATEVER. 

Your friend shows you this amazing project he's been working on. This AMAZINGLY INSANELY INCREDIBLE gizmo he puts together. Hey dude! Check this out. What do you think?. You look at it and say what?. WHATEVER Dude! It's Ayee. Best Buy has a better version of that. Who cares!. The correct response should have been praise. considering the effort and design he put into it. but that would be SO NOT COOL to do. isn't it?. Your COOL FACTOR would take a plunge if GOD FORBID you said. WOW! That's awesome!.

So we are surrounded with SO many comforts. and in most cases we don't even need to lift a finger for it. It is done FOR US. CONSTANTLY. that we start thinking we're entitled to it. I DESERVE It. And we start believing we OWN things. This BELONGS to ME. We have developed this idea of MY STUFF. It's MY stuff. and I'm not going to share it with anyone. Because it is my stuff. Why you touching my stuff. Don't touch my stuff. It's mine. Mine Mine Mine. ma mine ma mine ma mine. You guys literally turn into that bird in  finding Nemo. Mineee Minee Minee. 30:30

This is us today. But the thing about these people of sound essence is. they don't believe that they own ANYTHING. They understand that they do not actually posess anything. WHY?. Because they are SLAVES. and slaves don't OWN anything. An not just that they don't own anything. they themselves ARE OWNED by their master. This realization. is what truly makes them grateful. Because they understand. that everything that they own. is not actually ownership. it is temporary posession. that has been granted to them by their Rabb.

Sure. they worked during the day to earn a living and make money. so they do deserve a paycheck. which then they use to buy things. But would they be able to make that living if they didn't have eyes. or hands. or feet. or an intellect?. They MAY have worked for the paycheck. which bought them the iPad. but did they work to get their sight. their hearing. their heartbeats?. their EXISTENCE?. NO. So that paycheck. that is buying them their toys and gadgets. is based on certain UNDESERVED. UNEARNED gifts. that their Rabb. GRACIOUSLY. GENEROUSLY. blessed them with. So if they don't OWN their existence. and everything that comes along with that existence. then technically.  they don't own their paycheck. and therefore they don't own anything they bought WITH that paycheck. So then who owns all of it?. The one that gave them existence. right?. These people of sound essence realize. that in the TRUE sense. they don't OWN or DESERVE anything. Because they are SLAVES. This is why when they witness the favors and blessings of their master. they feel TRULY and COMPLETELY grateful. And Allah validates this in the Quran by saying.
⟪ar-quote:يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ كُلُوا۟ مِن طَيِّبَتِ مَا رَزَقْنَكُمْ⟫

O you who have believed.  eat from the good things which We have provided for you. and then do what?
⟪ar-quote:وَٱشْكُرُوا۟ لِلَّهِ⟫

and be grateful to Allah.
⟪ar-quote:إِن كُنتُمْ إِيَّاهُ تَعْبُدُونَ⟫

IF you turly consider yourselves his slaves.

When we understand THIS. it completely changes how we see the world. Because now we realize. whatever you and I have. the clothes  that we are wearing. the devices we're using. the possessions that we are so proud of. the cars we are driving in. the homes that we live in. the schools that we go to. None of it is actually something that we deserve. These are all gifts that have been given to us. This morning. all of you woke up and just jumped out of bed. But there are kids that work up in the morning and their parents had to carry them to their wheelchair. because they cannot walk. You woke up and the first thing you did. was grabbed your phone to check your messages. There are so many kids that woke up in complete darkness this morning. That will not be able to see anything for the rest of their lives. This morning some of you ate your breakfast. and you did not like the taste of what you had before you. and you dumped it all in the garbage. just because it didn't taste right. Yet. there are some kids who went through garbage pales this morning. just so that they could find something to eat.

THESE are realizations. These realizations are the soil in which TRUE gratitude cultivates. THIS mental exercise. of submitting ourselves as slaves to Allah. is the key to unlocking the treasures of his gratitude. In other words Gratitude is directly proportional to this realization of being a slave.

---

### Complaint is the litmus test of ingratitude

Now if you want to truly test this concept. of whether you believe you're a slave or not. the litmus test for that. is to catch yourself complaining. Scholars say. COMPLAIN. is the PROOF of ingratitude. It is the physical evidence of ingratitude. I'm not talking about complain when someone is hurting you. or bullying you. or if you have pain in your arm or something. I'm not talking about that. I'm talking about complains we have. related to posessions. or desires. you understand the difference?. If someone his hurting you. and you inform your parents about it. that's not a complaint. That's just you being smart.

The complaints I'm talking about. are related to posessions and desires. That stem from ingratitude. and they're of two types.

The first is the complaint. when you don't get something you want.

and the second is the complaint. when the thing . that you have. that you're complaining about. is not good enough to you. X2

When you complain about something you did not get. you believe that somehow you deserved that thing. you believe you were entitled to it. Like for example. when you study hard and you do really well on the exam and your professor still gives you a C. You complain. Because you believe you deserved an A. But then when your parents are not buying you that THING. that you want. and you complain. you somehow think you're entitled to it. or that your parents somehow OWE you that. which is not actually true. They don't owe you anything. Everything they do for you is out of their love. their care. their concern and their mercy for you. And if they DO actually owe anyone. they OWE Allah. not you!. Because Allah has made them a Rabb over you. But they don't directly owe you anything!. That's the first type of complain.

The second complain is when you get something. you already posess something. and it's not good enough for you. I mean how obnoxious is that!. If someone gives you a gift and you complain about it?.  Lets say.  I buy my daughter a violin for her birthday. because I know she's been wanting it for a while. So I save up my money. and I get the one I can afford for her. Now she takes it in her hand. looks at it. and tells me. Babu. You know.  there is a better version of this in ths store. Is that obnoxious?.  Yes! Its unacceptable. and if she did that. what would I do with that gift?.  If I handed her the violin and she said. you know there is a better version. what would I naturally do?. I'd take it away. And if you know me at all. I'll not only take away the violen. I'll take away ALL the others things I've given to her as well. Because I'm sure there is a better version of all those gifts out there too. And when I do that. she'll be like. NOOO I didn't mean it. Hahaha.

But seriously. we human beings. we don't appreciate the gifts that we have. UNTIL they are taken away. Kids have so many complaints against their parents. sisters have complaints against brothers. brothers complain again sisters. A kid goes to school. someone asks him. Hey! tell me about your mom. . OH MAN!. She's such a pain in my butt. She's ALWAYS on my case. ALWAYS nagging me about homework. about my chores. She's ALWAYS yelling at me. Always bugging me about my prayers. I can't wait to turn 18 and leave this freaking house. I'm SO sick and tired of her. But then. god forbid something happens. and Allah takes away his mother. At that point you ask him the same question. He'll say. I had the PERFECT mom. She loved me so much. She always took care of me. She always made sure I was fed. She never let me go to bed hungry. She would wash my clothes. iron them and folded them for me. She made my bed everyday for me. When I fell sick she would constantly check up on me. She took SUCH amazing care of me. I MISS HER SO MUCH!.

What happened?. What changed?. Just yesterday you couldn't stop complaining about her!. What happened to you today?.

So be grateful to Allah for the parents you have. You don't OWN them. Allah OWNS them. Just like he owns YOU. And one day. the OWNER WILL take back what belongs to him. And on that day you will ONLY be able to remember how good she was to you. If you want to be among the wise. Be grateful NOW.

Same goes for parents. I have never EVER heard a parent complain about their dead child. I have NEVER heard a parent say. My son was iressponsible. he never completed his homework. never did his chores. he always argued with me. NEVER!. They only say one thing. MY SON WAS PERFECT. My brother was perfect. My sister was perfect. APPRECIATE the people you have in your life today. before you lose them.

Because NOTHING lasts forever in this world. THAT is the ESSENCE of wisdom.  Let's summarize what we talked about today. Wisdom means. to have knowledge. and then to act upon it. And the climax of all wisdom is. . ⟪ar:أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ⟫ . Be grateful to Allah!. The ultimate wisdom. is being grateful to Allah. THAT is ULTIMATE wisdom. Because ONLY the wise realizes. that being created. being given existence. is Allah's ULTIMATE gift.

⟪ar-quote:وَٱللَّهُ أَخْرَجَكُم مِّنۢ بُطُونِ أُمَّهَتِكُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ شَيْـًۭٔا⟫

And Allah has extracted you from the wombs of your mothers not knowing a thing. That's our original state. complete ignorance. right? And then what?.

⟪ar-quote:وَجَعَلَ لَكُمُ ٱلسَّمْعَ وَٱلْأَبْصَرَ وَٱلْأَفْـِٔدَةَ ۙ⟫

and He made for you hearing and vision and intellect. These are the three primary gifts. by which we acquire knowledge. By seeing and hearing things. and using our intellects. So that we can study the ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. and become ⟪ar:عالِم⟫. to understand the ⟪ar:علیم⟫?. Without these gifts. could we have a decent life in this world?. Absolutely not!. So Allah created us ignorant. He created us in an UNGRATEFUL state.  and then gave us 3 gifts. hearing.sight. and intellect. to help get us out of our ignornace. to help us move towards wisdom. And why did he do that?.

⟪ar-quote:لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ⟫

that perhaps you would be grateful. And he said .⟪ar:لَعَلَّكُمْ⟫. MAYBE. Why maybe?. Because he knew that human beings are an ungrateful creation. And so we need to move towards gratitude. And gratitude is something that needs to be cultivated. It's a muscle that needs to be developed. And how do we do that?. By realizing that WE are SLAVES. We are slaves that do not deserve ANYTHING. We do not actually OWN anything. Everything and Everyone we have in life. these are all TEMPORARY posessions. They're all as temporary as our lives itself. These are all GIFTS and BLESSINGS. from our gracious and generous Rabb. who will take it back one day. ⟪ar:انا للہ⟫ . No doubt about it. we belong to Allah. We are his posessions. ⟪ar:و انا الیہ راجعون⟫. And no doubt about it. we will one day return to him. One day the owner will take back his posessions. See. ingratitude happens. when we believe things are permanent. But if everything is temporary. the ONLY logical conclusion is to enjoy them while they last. and be grateful to the one who gave them.

An urdu poet says.

سدا نہ باغی بلبل بولے، سدا نہ باغ بہاراں

سدا نہ قائم حسن و جوانی، سدا نہ صحبت یاراں

This nightingale will not sing in this garden forever. nor will the beauty of this garden last forever

Beauty and youth do not last forever. nor does the company of the beloved last forever.

So be grateful to Allah while you have these things.
