## Section 5757

In the previous session we looked at the meaning of the word wisdom. and how the ancient arabs defined it. They looked at is as having beneficial knowledge and acting upon it. And the essence of that wisdom. that was being taught to Hazrat Luqman was. ⟪ar:وَلَقَدْ آتَيْنَا لُقْمَنَ ٱلْحِكْمَةَ⟫ . We granted Luqman wisdom. For that what should you do?.  ⟪ar:أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِلَّهِ⟫.  Be grateful to Allah. Allah is teaching us. that gratitude is the essence. it is the pinnacle of wisdom.

And this gratitude. this ability to praise something good. to appreciate good things. it stems from a basic decency that Allah created us all with. Gratitude is not something we learn in life. It's already there. There are people who lose this basic decency. and are no longer grateful for anything in life. They become completely selfish. They start thinking that all the good things that come to them. are purely because of their own efforts. They deserve the things they have. They are entitled to everything they have. They don't need to thank anyone for anything. They don't owe anyone anything. They are completely independent. To such people. this message will make ABSOLUTELY NO sense. Islam will make NO sense to such people. They are never going to be able to reach the stage of HAMD. Because according to the Quran. for hamd. you have to have 2 things. You need to feel gratitude for the favors that are being done to you. AND.  you also have to have the ability to appreciate the design and the value of things. If someone doesn't have these two things. they're in the wrong place.

Because this is how the Quran begins its conversation.  It begins with the introduction of Allah. ⟪ar:بسم اللہ⟫. and then the very first attribute it mentions is his love. his care. his concern and his mercy. ⟪ar:الرحمن الرحیم⟫. That he is intensely merciful. consistently merciful. Because only the one who LOVES. who cares. who has genuine concern and who has mercy. ONLY someone with these attributes can be Rabb. Because only a Rabb can nurture, nourish, maintain, shower gifts. and elevate the one being nurtured. the marboob. from their present state to a higher state. Only a Rabb can do that. And that is why what immediately follows that introduction. is the idea of being grateful. ⟪ar:الحمد للہ رب العلمین⟫. Praise and gratitude to the Rabb AlAlameen.  It's THAT simple. It's that straight forward.

Then we learnt. that TRUE gratitude is cultivated in the soil of servitiude. In realizing and seeing ourselves. as who we REALLY are. That Allah is our Rabb. and we are his SLAVES. Now slavery. as Razia apa said. it has a very negative connotation attached to it. But the slavery we're talking about is VERY different. In fact. it's COMPLETELY different. And the reason it's COMPLETELY different. is because THIS master that we're dealing with is very different. I'll talk about these differences in detail when we get to. ⟪ar:ایاک نعبد و ایاک نستعین⟫.  But some of the things we can see that are different about this rabb. right off the bat. is that historically. masters are not loving. At best they are kind. or just.or generous. But masters don't LOVE their slaves. They don't shower their slaves with gifts. SO much. that they in fact forget that they are slaves. So that is one of the first things that sets this master apart. Not only did he provide his slaves with what was required. He went way above and beyond in his gifts.

### Islam is not for ungrateful people

If we reflect upon nature. even scientifically speaking. there is no reason. why we should ENJOY food. There is no scientific explanation for taste. Of why we would need taste. Cows eat grass. and they don't put salt or ketchup on it. They don't mix it with tomatoes and apples and make a russian salad out of it. They just eat grass. And they're perfectly fine doing that. Lions eat deer. and they just rip through it. They don't stop and say. hmmm. This could use a little bit of. rabbit topping. Or maybe a turle on the side would be nice. They don't do that. they just eat deer.  You know people feed their cats all this good stuff you can buy in a grocery story. But a cat can eat a cockroach and be happy with it. just like that. It doesn't need to dip the cockroach in chocolate first. It'll just eat it. no problem.

Human beigns however. Allah gave us these strange taste buds didn't he?. So you have certain fruits you like. and then some you don't quite like. Some of us have a sweet tooth. We like sweet things. certain kinds of chocolate you love.  and certain you don't. There are certain restaurants you're obsessed with. there others you can't stand. I don't like that place. Scientifically speaking. did we actually NEED taste. or the enjoyment of taste. when eating food to survive? No!. Its a gift!  I mean you and I could be eating grass and meat and bugs and have no taste. we could just eat to live. We didn't have to fills our stomach and go. OOOOH that was gooood.!  We didn't have to do that.

Similary. human beings didnt need to have color. This earth didn't need to be beautiful for us to live here. It could be completely flat. We could have survived just fine if this world was not beautiful. But are there sceneries in this world that are absolutely stunning?. Are there flowers that are INCREDIBLY beautiful?. Are there waterfalls that are simply breadth taking?. These beautiful creations of Allah. they inspire us to make beautiful designs and decorations. The entire fashion industry is inspired by flowers. they use floral patterns. colors of the sunrise. of the sunset. they are inspired by the colors of the sky. patterns of clouds. Million dollar chandelears are desgined inspired by snow flakes. SubhanAllah!!!. Why did there need to be beauty?. We could have absolutely survived without beauty. But its a GIFT. to his slaves from an amazing master.

Fragrance. Why do we need fragrance?. There are expensive perfumes. inspired by fragrances that exist in the world. Amazing smells. It didn't have to be this way. We didn't need good smell to survive.  There are people who don't have a sense of smell. they survive fine. They live out their entire life. no problems.

So this master. he did not just give us life. he made life beautiful for us. This is something to be appreciated. This is something to be grateful for. Some people though. they are simply not interested in appreciating that. When something bad happens in life. most people. they say. How come this happened to me?. What did I ever do to deserve this?. right?. But when good things happen to them. they never ask the same questions. They never say.  How come this good happened to me?. What did I ever do to deserve this blessing?. But then there are some that do. And it takes gratitude and praise in the heart to be able to do that.

And this is why Islams argument. The Quran's argument is. that IF you're feeling appreciative by what you see around you. please continue reading. If you have no appreciation.  you are completely self indulged. and nothing is good enough for you. all you can do is complain. then that's ok. but don't bother reading anymore. Cause you'll simply waste your time. Good luck to you. See you in hell. PUN intended. Remember the last time I told you. Kafir has 2 meanings. Someone who disbelieves. and someone who is ungrateful. So if you want to be a kafir. go ahead. if you want to be a disbeliever. no problem. Live your life. The Quran is not for you. Allah doesn't need you.  This is the essence of beginning this ayah with AlHamdulillah. Praise and gratitude belongs to Allah. whether you choose to praise him or not. whether you choose to be grateful or not. it's irrelevant.

But a true slave. an obedient slave. a slave of pure essence. he sees his master's favors. his gifts. all around him. and inside of him. and he feels praise and gratitude. even before he hears the revelation. He becomes a witness to the fact that his master LOVES him. This in itself sets this master apart from all other masters of the world. Because no other master will LOVE his slave this way.

### Different kind of slavery

The next thing is. that slavery.  is ALWAYS for the benefit of the master. right?. Historically human beings are enslaved. for whose benefit?. Is it for the masters benefit. or for the slaves benefit?. ALWAYS for the master's benefit. Isn't that true?. But is our slavery for the benefit of Allah?. Does he have a need for us?. Does he actually need our prayers?. Our efforts?. Our gratitude?. NO

⟪ar-quote:وَمَن يَشْكُرْ . فَإِنَّمَا يَشْكُرُ لِنَفْسِهِ⟫

The one who is grateful. is only . truly being grateful for himself. He is ONLY benefitting himself.

⟪ar-quote:وَمَن كَفَرَ . فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ غَنِىٌّ حَمِيدٌۭ⟫

And whoever is ungrateful. then certainly Allah is free of all need. and he is praised in and of himself. This master has ABSOLUTELY NO need of slaves. He does not need our slavery. We accept him as our master. for whose benefit?. For our own benefit. Allah's slavery ONLY and ONLY benefits us. It does not benefit him in any way shape or form. In fact. it is from his mercy. his rehma. that he ACCEPTS us. and ALLOWS us to become his slaves. Just think about the difference between us and him. How pathetic and abject are we before his glory and majesty. Are the BEST of the BEST efforts we've EVER made in life. The BEST salaah we prayed. The BEST fast we ever did. The BEST Zakaat we ever gave. is it on par with his standards?. Is it of the level he deserves?. Of course not. But does he still accept it?. Does he still get pleased with our pathetic efforts?. Does he store an immense reward for us in return?. He does!. This is again unheard of when you think about slavery.

Then every other slavery we know of. is it voluntary or involuntariy?. Historically. Have you ever heard that someone thought of slavery as a profession?. You know. I'm not really sure what I want to become in life. I could go into medicine.  I could become an engineer. or I could try slavery. That sounds like a noble profession. that's something I could explore. Does anyone ever think like that?. NO. People are captured. and forcefully SOLD into slavery. without their choice. Isn't that true?.

But what about Allah?. Does he FORCE us into becoming his slaves?. First of all. COULD he force us?. Does he have the POWER to force us into submission?. Does the one who has forced GALAXIES into submission. does he have the ability to force us into submission?. But does he?.

Also who pays money to buy a slave?. Every slave has a price, right?. Even in the old days. a MASTER would have to go to their local store. Slaves R Us. and PURCHASE a slave. right?. There is always a price involved. But in this case. who is paying the price?. The slave is. We are. We are paying the price to enter Allah's servitude. It's INCREDIBLE. Every other slavery of the world. the master purchases the slave. But this ⟪ar:عبودیۃ⟫to Allah(Azza Wa Jal). we desire it. we work hard for it. we strive for it. WE pay the price to become his slave. He doesn't hold a gun to our head.

⟪ar-quote:لَآ إِكْرَاهَ فِى ٱلدِّينِ ۖ قَد تَّبَيَّنَ ٱلرُّشْدُ مِنَ ٱلْغَىِّ⟫

There is absolutely NO compulsion in religion. True guidance has been clearly separated from falsehood. It's now up to you. FREE WILL. YOU want to become my obedient slave. of your own free will. ⟪ar:فَضَّل⟫.  You're most welcome!. You don't want to become my obedient slave. you want to remain a slave of your nafs. go right ahead. It's really amazing if you reflect on it.

Then. to every other slave.  in the worldly sense. the title of "SLAVE" is an INSULT!. It is a DISHONOR.  To a believer. being Allah's slave is the GREATEST HONOR there is!. What is the title bestowed upon the GREATEST man that every walked the earth. ⟪ar:اشھد ان محمد عبد و رسولہ⟫.  Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) devoted his entire life. JUST to earn this title. "ABD". It is the GREATEST honor that's humanly possible. You tell me. Not even as a muslim. just as an objective individual. Did the slavery of Rasul Allah. honor him in this world?. Or dishonor him?. He is the MOST honored individual in the Islamic world. and respected all around even by non muslims. Why did he receive this honor?. Because he became the slave of Allah. In fact. this slavery of Allah. honored him so much. it elevated him to such of a master himself. such that Maulana Ali said.⟪ar:انا عبدٌ من عبید محمد⟫ .  I am a SLAVE from among the slaves of Muhammad (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Just imagine that!.

Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) is the slave of Allah. for whom Maulana Ali AS PROUDLY says. I am one of the MANY slaves of Muhammad (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Maulana Ali. considers himself HONORED to be called one of his slaves!. Just think what a beautiful slavery it must be!!!. Don't confuse this slavery with the slavery of the world. This is a slavery that people have begged and pleaded for. Maulatina Fizza. She was an actual princess. She was the daughter of a king. true royalty. she gave up her palace. all her riches to become the slave of Maulatina Fatima (salawaatullah Alayha). Maulana Qambar. he gave himself up in the slavery and servitude of Maulana Ali. SO many times Maulana Ali set him free. but he wouldn't leave his side. He wouldn't give up his slavery. because Hazrat Qambar knew. he wasn't the slave of just ANYONE. He knew who his master was. He was the slave of ALI IBN ABI TAALIB. And he took GREAT pride in it.  In fact. there is this one incident. I'm side tracking a bit. but I guess its relevant to what we're talking about.

It is narrated that one day. one of these people in Kufa. who had contempt for Maulana Ali. he saw Hazrat Qambar walking down the street. He knew that Qambar was a slave of Maulana Ali. So he thought. Let me humiliate Qambar publicly today. So he calls maulana Qambar out in the market. in front of everyone. He says. Ya Qambar! انت عبداً؟. Oh Qambar! Aren't you a slave?. Because slavery is considered a dishonor. an insult right?. So he says to Qambar. Aren't you a slave?.

So Maulana Qambar turns to this man. and he replies. Indeed I am a slave. But do you not know whose slave I am?. And then he starts reciting this praise of Maulana Ali. OMG. It's SO incredible. I can't even. Just the beauty of those words. He goes on and on and on.

⟪ar-quote:أنا مُوَلِّى من ضرب بسیفین . و طعن برمحین . وصلى القبلتین . وبایع البیعتین . وهاجر الهجرتین . ولم یکفر بالله طرفة عین. 

أنا ⟪ar-quote:مُوَلِّى⟫صالح المؤمنین . ووارث النبیین . وخیر الوصیین . وأکبر المسلمین . ویعسوب المؤمنین . ونور المجاهدین . ورئیس البکائین . وزَین العابدین.  وسراج الماضین . وضوء القائمین . وأفضل القانتین . ولسانِ رسولُ رَّبِّ العالمین . وأَوَّلُ الوصیین من آل یس . والمؤید بجبرئیل الامین . و المنصور بمیکائیل المتین . المحمود عند أهل السماء أجمعین . والمحامی عن حُرُمِ المسلمین . والمجاهدُ أعدائُہُ النَّاصبین .وأمینِهِ على المخلوقین . وخلیفةُ مَن بعث إلیها أجمعین . سید السابقین . وقاتل الناکثینَ والقاسطین . ومَبیَدِ المشرکین . وسَهمُ مِن مَرامِ اللهِ على المنافقین⟫

And he goes on and on and on. This is only a small portion of what I remember. He literally goes on for like 15 minutes. And every word is so perfect and so amazing.  SubhanAllah!. And then at the end of it all he looks at the crowd and proudly says. Who among you has a master. like the one I have!!!. And everybody is standing there. completely dumbfounded. and awe striken.

This is the honor of ⟪ar:عبدیۃ⟫. the slavery of an amazing master. So my point is. that even though the word for ABD. IS  slavery. and we are indeed becoming SLAVES of Allah. But this is a COMPLETELY different kind of slavery. It is unlike any other slavery we will EVER come to know of. It's an HONOR above and beyond all honors. to become the slave of Allah. And so I thought. to keep this distinction in mind. moving forward. I am going to try to NOT use the word "SLAVE" anymore. I'll try to use the word ⟪ar:عبد⟫. when I talk about this special kind of slavery.  So when you hear this word ⟪ar:عبد⟫. I want you to make this separation. between the derogatory version. versus this complimentary version that I just explained.

---

World operates based on Rububiyyah

Now let's return to Hamd. which means gratitude and praise. I told you there are two types of hamd. There is gratitude to Allah. which we talked about last time. And there is gratitude to the intermediaries of Allah. that I want to talk about today.

If you look at how our physical world operates. you will find EVERY single thing in nature. operating under the blanket of Rububiyyah. If you keep those 6 definitions of the word Rabb in mind. you'll see rububiyyah in action all around you. The heavens have been made a Rabb over the earth. It nurtures it. provides it with rain. It brings the dead earth back to life.

⟪ar-quote:ٱعْلَمُوٓا۟ أَنَّ ٱللَّهَ يُحْىِ ٱلْأَرْضَ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا⟫

Know that Allah gives life to the dead earth.

So the sky or the heavens is a Rabb over the earth. which means the solar system. We know this earth is surviving. because of the rububiyyah of the solar system. Anything goes wrong with their rububiyyah. and game over for us. right?. Then the earth is a Rabb for all living things. It provides them with food and water. it provides nourishment for the survival of all species. Then in our day to day lives. you'll find rububiyyah. in every organized system there is.  Take your schooling for instance. There is a board of education. that is a Rabb over these various levels of Primary education, middle school, high school, college. right?. Then each one of these act as a rabb. individually over the teachers. Teachers are Rabb over students. Parents are rabb over kids. Doctors are rabb over patients. Governments are rabb over the country. CEO and board members are Rabb over their corporations. right?. So we see that this world operates under the blanket of rububiyyah. That's the first thing. The next thing to understand is. that rububiyyah. works through intermediaries. which are the cause and effects. required to get the job done. OK?. So two things to understand. First. Rububiyyah is a process. designed to provide a systematic. and progressive benefit to the marboob.  And the second is. that the process of rububiyyah is executed THROUGH various intermediaries. to get the job done.

Gratitude to intermediaries

Let's look at the example of a farmer. to understand this better. A farmer in classical Arabic. is a perfect example of a Rabb. Because he is responsible for cultivating his land. and growing crops. So he holds ownership of that land.  has authority over it. he nurtures the plants. maintains them. waters them. He protects them from bugs and animals. He does everything implied by the definitions of the word Rabb. So the farmer is the Rabb of his crops. But does he actually GROW the plant?. Does he make the plant tear out of the seed?. Does he actually pull out its roots. and spread it in the ground?. Does he shove his hand in the dirt. grab the plant by its neck. and then stretch it into a tree. NO!. He does none of those things.

The way he executes his rububiyyah. is by delegating these responsibilities. to certain intermediaries. which are the elements of nature. The soil, the water, the sunlight, the darkness. He controls them. and they in turn. fulfill their jobs of raising the plant. Does that make sense?. The farmer makes sure the soil has the right temprature. He makes sure water is provided in the right amounts. and at the right time. He makes sure enough sunlight is  provided. but not so much that it burns and kills the plant. He makes sure he uses the right fertilizer for the right kind of plant.  you understand?. So the farmer. as the ULTIMATE Rabb. is executing his rububiyyah. not directly. but THROUGH these intermediaries. He doesn't interact with the plant at all. Who does he interact with?. Who does he influence?. Who does he work on?. the intermediaries. which are the soil. the water. the sunlight. the minerals. They are the ones doing all the work. under his guidance. But intentionally speaking. who is it that the farmer want to benefit?. The plant, right?. His goal is the development of the plant. He is working on EVERYTHING else. so that the plan could receive the benefit.

Now the question is. these plants. these crops. Who should they be grateful to?. Should they be grateful to the farmer?. or should they be grateful to the intermediaries?. Let's think about it.  Granted that these intermediaries. soil. sunlight. water. minerals. fertitilizer. no doubt they have the potential. and the ability to make the plant grow. But was that potential enough without the farmers design and control?. Let's say the farmer.  just dumped the seeds in the ground. stamped on it a few times. and walked away. Now the soil is still there. the water is still there. sunlight is still available. But would all these things. make the plant grow?. NO. Of course not. Even though they all have the potential. the capabilities to make plants grow. but without the design and the control of the farmer. none of these intermediaries would be able to benefit the plant. Correct?. OK. Fair enough. The plant owes gratitude to the farmer for its growth and survival. But then would that growth have been possible. if the intermediaries did not do all the hard work that they did FOR the plant?. Had they not slaved for the plant day in and day out. week after week. month after month. would the plant be able to grow?. ABSOLUTELY NOT. Hmmm. the plot thickens. Who does the plant be grateful to now?.

What we're learning here is. that even though the plant owes its gratitude. its hamd. ultimately to the farmer. justice dictates. that it's not possible to be grateful to the farmer. without FIRST being grateful to the intermediaries. the asbaab. the wasaayel. that the farmer put in place for the plant. Because the PLANT is dealing with these intermediaries. NOT. the farmer directly. So it needs to FIRST be grateful to the intermediaries. And what does that mean?. What would be the gratitude of the plant?. To accept and submit TO the intermediaries. SO THAT they could benefit it. There is a relationship there right?. The intermediaries are now the master. and a master needs an ABD. to complete the relationship. So the plant needs to complete the relationship by submitting to these intermediaries. ALLOWING them to benefit it. That would be the plants gratitude to the intermediaries. and THAT would be the plants gratitude to the farmer.

Listen to this carefully. For this plant metahphore. The plant can ONLY be grateful to the farmer. by begin grateful to the intermediaries. The plants gratitude to the intermediaries. The plant submitting TO the intermediaries. allowing the farmer to do what he intendes to do. IS its gratitude to the farmer.

BE GRATEFUL TO THE INTERMEDIARIES. IN ORDER TO BE GRATEFUL TO THE RABB.

---

### Chain of gratitude

Now let's look at an example closer to hom. For us human beings. when it comes to Rububiyyah. the closest thing we have. in the seen realm. right in front of us. is our parents. So now as decent human beings. we realize that our parents. ESPECIALY our mothers have done an enormous amount of good for us. So basic human decency dictates. that we be grateful to our moms. Not as a muslim. just as a basic decent human being. Why?. Because she almost died giving you birth. She almost killed herself. so that you and I could be alive. That's a pretty big deal. You and I wouldn't be breathing right now. if our mother's didn't bleed for us. That's just a fact. So basic decency dictates that we be grateful to our parents especially our mothers.

Now when I say. I REALLY want to thank my mom. I TRULY want to be grateful to my mom. I realize. that my mom wasn't opening up her stomach and putting spoons of food in my mouth.  Some automatic thing was happening inside my mom that when she ate food. I was getting fed. It was all automatically getting taken care of. for me inside her. There was a predictable. systematic design of cause and effect that was taking place within my mothers womb. which was feeding me. developing me and allowing me to grow. And all of that was through the noursihment coming to me from my mom. Which means that if my mom didn't eat. I would not have been fed. right?

This means that in order to TRULY be grateful. I have to now also be grateful to the one who was feeding her. so that I could be fed. Mabye she didnt have the means to earn money at that time. Maybe it was my dad who was making the money. that bought the groceries. which fed her. which in turn fed me. So maybe I should thank my dad who was providing the food for us both. So now I don't just want to thank my mom. but also my dad for making that living. But then I think about my dad and mom. and I realize that my dad wouldn't earn this living. if he hadn't received a good eductation. which probably my grand parents got him. Because it is that education. that led him to earn a living. so that my mom could eat. so that I could get food. You see what I'm doing here?. So now I realize that I need to be grateful to my grandparents as well. on both sides. for the food I'm getting in my mothers womb. you understand?.  But then I realize that my grand parents only exist. because their parents existed and raised them. who then raised my parents . etc.  So now maybe I should not only thank my parents. but also my grand parents and their parents . and their parents. and so on. Because IF all of that didn't happen. I wouldn't be having this meal in my mothers tummy. you understand?

When you really start thinking about THANKING someone. and I mean TRULY feeling grateful for someone. does it end with the person you are about to thank?.  Cause they could not have done what they did for you. if someone else didn't do something for them. And if you go further back. someone who did something for them. someone ELSE must have done something for them. and you keep going back. And if you are TRULY TRUYLY grateful. then you realize. This all had to start somewhere. It all had to start somewhere. and that's how you reach who?.  You reach Allah!!.  I am grateful for being born of my parents. who are grateful for being born of their parents. who are then grateful of being born of their parents. And it keeps going back till you get to the first parent. which is adam and hawwa (Alayhim AlSalaam). who were grateful for being created. by. Allah.  So it all goes back to Allah.

When I was inside the fetus. which was my ENTIRE world. my ENTIRE universe. Inside that world. I was being taken care by a process of rububiyyah. executing through cause and effects. which was designed by Allah. Now that I'm outside the fetus. in the real world. I am still being taken care of. by the same design. by the same process of rububiyyah. executing through cause and effects. So when you think about TRUE gratitude. it's not just gratitude to the person right in front of you. it's also for all the cause and effects put into place. so that this benefit could reach you. And when you truly reflect and traverse that chain back. the one you find. HOLDING this rope. is Allah (Azza Wa Jal) . This is in the physical sense. The physical rububiyyah.

Now let's talk about spiritual rububiyyah. I am grateful to my teacher.  my spiritual Rabb. Javeed bhai. who taught me everything I know today. I am truly grateful to him. Because I owe my spritual existence to him. But I cannot be truly grateful to him. until I am grateful to his teachers who taught him. why?.  Because had they not taught him. I would have remained ignorant. So in a sense. Allah put him through all of his training. so that he could train me. So now if I want to be TRULY grateful to him. I must also be grateful to his teachers and their teachers and their teachers and so on. And if I go back all the way. where will I eventually reach?. I am grateful to my teacher. Javeed bhai. who learnt from and is greatful to manaseeb. who learnt from and are grateful to Duaat. who learnt from and are grateful to Aimma. who learnt from and are grateful to Maulana Ali AS. the source of all true knowledge. And when I get there. who do I find Maulan Ali grateful to?. ⟪ar:انا عبدٌ من عبید محمد⟫. He is grateful to Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). who is grateful to. Jibraeel AS. is then grateful to. Allah(Azza Wa Jal). Once again. even at the spiritual level. the buck stops with Allah. You understand?. This is why Allah says in the Quran.

⟪ar-quote:أُو۟لَٓئِكَ ٱلَّذِينَ يَدْعُونَ. يَبْتَغُونَ إِلَىٰ رَبِّهِمُ ٱلْوَسِيلَةَ⟫

Those whom they call upon. they too seek MEANS. Intermediaries. to access their Rabb

⟪ar-quote:أَيُّهُمْ أَقْرَبُ⟫

Each one of them closer to their master. Closer in what?.

⟪ar-quote:وَيَرْجُونَ رَحْمَتَهُۥ وَيَخَافُونَ عَذَابَهُ⟫

In their hope for His mercy.  and they fear of His punishment.

This is why in every dua that we recite. we mention the names of Rasul Allah. Maulana Ali. Aimma Tahireen. BEFORE we begin our conversation with Allah. Why is that?. Why can't we just directly pray to Allah. Why do we have to place these individuals in between us and Allah?.We have to do that. because Allah HIMSELF placed these intermediaries in between. We came to know of Allah. THROUGH their rububiyyah. And so now justice dictates. that we have to be grateful to them first. we have to honor them first. We have to do what they ask us to do FIRST. And then we have to use them. as waseela. as means. to approach Allah.

⟪ar-quote:يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ ٱتَّقُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ وَٱبْتَغُوٓا۟ إِلَيْهِ ٱلْوَسِيلَةَ⟫

O you who have believed. fear Allah and seek the INTERMEDIARIES to approach Him. Don't just directly come to Allah. come to Allah THROUGH his means. through his intermediaries. What does this mean?. If its gratitude. BE grateful to them FIRST in order to be grateful to Allah. Obey them FIRST. in order to Obey Allah. LOVE them FIRST. in order to love Allah. Acknowledge them. honor them. APPRECIATE them first. in order to acknowledge and glorify Allah.  ⟪ar:وَٱبْتَغُوٓا۟ إِلَيْهِ ٱلْوَسِيلَةَ⟫. These intermediaries are the milestones for us on the path to Allah. This is where the training of gratitude begins. And the VERY FIRST milestone for us. are parents.

This is why. the Quran's argument is not that you just have to find a creator.  No No No. That comes much much later. The Quran's argument is. Don't you want to be grateful?.  Aren't you a decent person?. Isn't gratitude something I built inside of you. And if you ARE a decent person. and you DO want to be grateful. Be grateful to the Rabb right in front of you. the one who exists in the seen realm. Because if you're not going to be grateful to your parents. your immediate Rabb. How are you going to be grateful to me?. If you can't see your parents as Rabb. How will you EVER be able to see me as Rabb????. Because Rububiyyah. just like anything and everything else in the world. is a progression. It's a training. You want to be TRULY grateful?. Be grateful to you parents. Be gratefuly to your grand parents. Be grateful to your teachers. Be grateful to your teachers teachers. Be grateful to the Imams. Be grateful to Maulana Ali. Be greateful to Rasul Allah. Because being grateful to ALL OF THEM. will be your gratitude to your ultimate Rabb. 

### Interpreation of drinking water

See. I'll tell you something. What are the ettiquettes of drinking water?. We muslims. following the teachings of Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) . when we drink water. we hold the glass in our right hand. and then we sit and drink the water. right?. Now why is that?. It is to honor. to show gratitude. to the greatest blessing there is for human life. which is water. It is the ULTIMATE blessing for all living things. We would DIE without water. An arrogant person doesn't even think about this. But a true ABD. an obedient ABD. he remembers and appreciates this fact. every single time he has a drink. The fact that had his master not provided him with water. and made it SO accessible for him. he would not be able to survive. So how does he show gratitude to his master for that blessing?. He makes himself humble before Allah FOR that blessing. And he displays that humility IN ACTION. by lowering himself before it. By sitting down and drinking it.

But then this slave ALSO realizes that he would not be able to drink the water. unless it was not confined in a glass. Of course.  he could dunk his face in the sink and drink like an animal. But to be able to drink in a civilized.  honorable way. he needs to use a glass or a cup. Now is WATER the real blessing of Allah. or is the glass the real blessing of Allah?. Obviously it's the WATER!. The glass is just a means. an intermediary. to a goal. which is to drink the water.

But look. Our prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) in his vast wisdom. he made it compulsory to pay respect to the glass as well. And this is why we hold it in our RIGHT hand and not our left hand. to honor it. to express our gratitude to it. Because we Muslims. we use our right hand ONLY for honorable things. and we use our left hand for foul things. So  Rasul Allah made it obligatory. that when you drink water. hold the glass in your RIGHT hand. to show gratitude to the glass. to honor it!!!. Now notice which honor comes first?. Do you hold the glass first?. or do you drink the water first?. You hold the glass first. So you have to honor. and show gratitude to the means. to the INTERMEDIARY. BEFORE you can show gratitude to the blessing. Isn't that interesting?. Even though the real blessing is the water. you have to honor the glass first. And then you have to lower youself before the glass. and elevate it. in order to drink from it. I want you all to think about this action of drinking water. You've already lowered yourself. humbled yourself before Allah's blessing. You've honored the glass by holding it in your right hand. But that's not enough. As you're drinking the water. you are continuously ELEVATING the glass. Because you HAVE to elevate the glass to drink more water. isn't that the case?. Its not possible to drink more. if you don't keep lifting the glass up. The MORE blessings you want. the MORE you MUST elevate and honor the glass. the intermediary. SubhanAllah! . This entire structure of gratitude is placed as a reminder. for every single time we drink a glass of water.  AllahuAkbar. There is NOT a single thing in our religion. not a single hadees. not a single action. commanded by our beloved prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) that is not filled with immensely beautiful.  and profound meanings. SubhanAllah!

### Parents are immediate intermediaries

So what I want you to understand. is that your parents are the glass.  through which you are enjoying the blessings of Allah. You have to honor them first. you have to be grateful to them continuoulsy. IN ORDER to be grateful to Allah. Because parents are the FIRST of all the intermediaries. between us and Allah.  He says in the same surah Luqman.

⟪ar-quote:وَوَصَّيْنَا ٱلْإِنسَنَ بِوَلِدَيْهِ⟫

And We have made it obligatory upon man to care for his parents.

⟪ar-quote:حَمَلَتْهُ أُمُّهُۥ وَهْنًا عَلَىٰ وَهْنٍۢ وَفِصَلُهُۥ فِى عَامَيْنِ⟫

His mother carried him. which increased her in weakness upon weakness, and his weaning is in two years.

⟪ar-quote:أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ إِلَىَّ ٱلْمَصِيرُ⟫

Be grateful to Me and to your parents. To Me is your final destination.

أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ. Be grateful to Me and your parents. This is SO beautiful. If you notice. Allah joined the twe extreme ends together. He says be grateful to ME. Allah is the furthest link. ALL the way at the other end. And he joins it with . وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ . and to your parents. who are the closest link to me. Notice when he talks about gratitude he mentions himself. but he doesn't use the word shukar again for parents. He doesn't say.

⟪ar-quote:أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَ اشکر وَلِدَيْكَ⟫

Be grateful to me and be grateful to your parents. No he only uses the word shukr ONCE. with himself. ⟪ar:. أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ⟫. Be grateful to me AND your parents?. Why?. Because being grateful TO your parents.  is a PART of your gratitude to me. You can't be grateful to me if you're not grateful to your parents.

We were brought into this world by Allah. But in the seen world.  in the seen sense. we were brought into this world by our parents.  Allah provides all of our food and sustenance. but in the physical sense. who did Allah make the means to provide us with food? Our parents. Allah protects us. but who has he given that responsibility to in the physical sense? To our parents. You know today. when you are older and you get scared. you say.⟪ar:اعوذ بالله⟫. but when you were a child. and you got scared.  when a two year old get scared. what does he say?.  mama.  mama. They do that or not?. Because everything that Allah is to us in the grand scheme of things. when we are a child. we don't see Allah. we don't even understand the concept of Allah.  the only thing we understand is what?.  mama. parents. SubnhanAllah. Allah clothes us. but in the physical sense our parents  clothe us.  Allah teaches us. ⟪ar:علم الانسان مالم يعلم⟫. He taught the human being what he did not know. ⟪ar:علمہ البیان⟫. He taught the human being how to speak. but technically who teaches us how to speak?  our parents.

In other words. ALL of what Allah did for us.  he did it for us. through our parents. The most important entity for a child is its parents. Their refuge is the parents. Their source of love is parents. Protection is parents. Provision is parents . EVERYTHING that you can think of later on with Allah.  in the beginning of your life.  as a child. its your parents. Parents are GREATEST GIFTS and BLESSINGS of Allah. Because they are doing the WORK of Allah. that he wants done for us. Parents are actually the ambassador of Allah in raising you.  They are Allah's ambassadors. They represent him. They represent his work. And do you know what Allah's goal is for you and me?. You know what he's using parents for?. To make us RABB. That's what a parent is doing. They're nurturing you to elevate you from the status of Murabbee. and turn you into a Rabb. How?. So that your SOUL now becomes the Rabb of your body. They elevate you from the pathetic. helpless state of a child. to an elevated intellectual state. of a Rabb. Look at a child. the parent needs to make all the decision FOR it. From that state. your parents got you to the state. where you are now able to handle your own Rububiyyah. If you honestly reflect on it. that's no small task. that's not a small favor. That's an INCREDIBLE favor. And if you are a decent person. if you haven't lost that decency that Allah created you with. you will feel immense gratitude for your parents.

Because if you don't feel gratitude for them. you'll never get to the next stage. You won't be able to be grateful to the spiritual parents. who are going to now raise you. from this pathetic. and helpless state of mortal physicality. to the glorious and immortal state of spirituality. If you can't be grateful to your parents. you'll never be grateful to your teachers. and you'll never be grateful to Rasul Allah. and you'll never be grateful to Allah. Becuase it's all a chain of command. This is why he says.

⟪ar-quote:وَٱعْتَصِمُوا۟ بِحَبْلِ ٱللَّهِ⟫

Hold strongly to the rope of Allah. ⟪ar:وعتصمو⟫. comes from. ⟪ar:عصم⟫. which means. You know that sport of bull riding?. When you're on the bull and you're holding that rope. and the bull is trying to throw you off. How would you hold that rope?. What kind of a grip would you have to maintain?. A REALLY strong one right?. That kind of a hold is called ⟪ar:عصم⟫. Allah says.  ⟪ar:وَٱعْتَصِمُوا۟ بِحَبْلِ ٱللَّهِ⟫. Hold tightly to the rope of Allah. What is this rope of Allah?. It is these intermediaries between us and Allah. Imagine this. Imagine a rope is hanging down from the heaven. and its coming all the way down to you. Now you have to climb this rope all the way to heaven. How will you do it?. You'll grab what's closest to you with one hand, right?. And then where will your other hand go?. Directly to Allah?. No. You'll grab the rope right above your other hand. Isn't that how you climb a rope?. So what does this mean?. You'll grab the first intermediary. which is your physical parents. and that intermediary will nurture you. life you. help elevate you. from your current rank. to the next higher rank of knowledge. which are your spiritual parents. And then your spiritual parent. will lift you to the next parent. until you reach the final parents. There is a hadees of Rasul ALlah.

⟪ar-quote:انا و انت یا علی. ابوین المومنین.⟫

Oh Ali. You and I are the parents of all believers. But if you can't love your physical parents. you'll never be able to love your spiritual parents. It's just a natural fact. If your relationship is not good with your parents. then I guarantee you that your relationship is not good with Allah. You can see this for yourself. And so the ONLY way to rectify your relationship with Allah. is to rectify your relationship with your parents.

### Definition of Hamd

OK. so we're talking gratitude. Hamd. which means two things. It means gratitude and it means praise. Let's start by defining these two things. and understanding how they are related?. Gratitude and priase are emotions. that are generated in the heart. when one realizes that an undeserved gift. or an unearned benefit has been provided by a benefactor. In other words. when someone does something nice for you. you feel this emotion of love in your heart. for two things. Love for the person providing the benefit. and love for the gift itself. You understand?. Love for the person who gave you the gift. and love for the gift itself. The love for the gift is experienced as praise. And the love for the giver is experienced as gratitude. I'll give you an example.

Your dad buys you. your brand new dream car.  and hes dangling the keys before you. What do you feel?. For you dad. Oh Thank you thank you thank you. you're the BEST dad ever. I love you so much. I can't believe you did this for me. Thank you dad. Thank you. So for your dad. you feel gratitude. And when you look at the car. checking out the leather interior. the shiny rims. you go. WOW!. This thing is DOPE. This thing is freaking AWESOME. So for the car. for the gift. you feel praise. You understand?. So gratitude towards your dad. and priase for the car.

Now does your dad just hand you the keys to your new car?. NO. Obviously not. You know there is a lecture that comes with that. You know it. Dads going to say. Listen. you need to stop at stop signs. You need to stay under the speed limit.  You have to not be out after 9pm.  you need to. you need to. you need to. Hes not gong to give you a 1000 things. He'll most likely give you 10. He'll say here are the 5 things I don't want you do.  And here are the 5 things I DO want' you to do. Keep it clean. Make sure you change the oil. etc. etc. He'll say. Listen. You din't buy this car. I did. and I'm giving it to you. Its hard earned money that I worked for. that I am using . to buy this car for you. You absolutely have no share in this. You do not deserve this car. You did not earn this car. I am not asking you to pay me for it. The only reason Im giving it to you. is because I love you. But in return. all I expect from you. all I ask of you. are these 10 things. please don't do them. And BTW. these 10 things I'm telling you. are for your own safety. Obeying me doesn't benefit me. it benefits you. Please don't speed. you'll get a ticket. Please don't crash into a tree. you'll get hurt. I don't care about the car. I care about you. For the car I have insurance. Please don't let your friend drive the car. right?. So he sets these few rules for you. Is that fair?. With undeserved gifts. comes responsibilities. Because the gifts are being given to you for a reason. And you can fulfill that reason. or you can ignore them. You understand?

Allah has given us numerous UNDESERVED gifts. Allah says I'll give you 5 fingers on each hand. use them wisely!.  I'll give you 2 nosrills. I'll give you functioning lungs. Ill give you a heart that beats. I'll give you 2 legs. all the toes on every leg. I'll give you a stomach that works. I'll give you a chest. I'll give you bones. bones that don't break upon contact. You know there are people who have very brittle bones by the way. they could break very easily. Just a regular hand shake can break the bones in their hand. Allah gave us eyes. ears. hands. feet. But with these gifts came responsibilities.

So hamd. in the truest sense. is appreciating the value of the gift. when you appreciate the value of a gift and the benefit it provides. what generates in the heart is PRAISE for the gift. and that praise moves out of the heart. and comes onto the tongue and it is articulated. in the form of . AlHamdulillah. and SubhanAllah. That is the hamd of the heart and the tongue. And there is the hamd of the jawarih. of the body parts. In other words the gratitude and praise does not just remain confined to the heart and the tongue. it then moves to the limbs. and they get busy in the execution of the purpose they were given for. In other words. it is not simply lip service. it's not just on the tongue. it actually becomes manifest in the actions of the human being. and this is why. ⟪ar:شکر نعمت العین….  خِفضُ البَصَر⟫. The eye itself is a blessing. and the gratitude for the eye.  the way we thank Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) for the blessing of the eye. is to lower it from the forbidden. We do not look at the things that Allah has prohibited to see. The gratitude for the blessing of hearing is to not listen to the forbidden. the gheebah. gossip. backbiting. Because of the Day of Judgment the hands and the eyes will bear  witness.  against the human being. 
⟪ar-quote:بَلِ ٱلْإِنسَنُ عَلَىٰ نَفْسِهِۦ بَصِيرَةٌۭ . . وَلَوْ أَلْقَىٰ مَعَاذِيرَهُۥ ‎⟫

The human being knows what he's up to.  even if he starts giving excuses.  This is why the arabs say. 
⟪ar:العُزرُ اَقبَح مِنَ الذَّنب⟫

The excuse is uglier than the wrong action. Because we all have excuses. Life is just filled with excuses. And so HAMD. is the manifestation of the praise and the gratitude. within action. and this is why the Prophet said. 
⟪ar-quote:لا الہ الا اللہ المفتاح الجنۃ……. وَلِکُلِّ مِفتَاح اثنان.⟫

La Ilaha Illa Allah is the key to jannah….  but then he said. Every key has teeth.  you have to have the locksmith fill in the teeth so that it can fit the lock. And the teeth of La Ilaha Illa Allah  is acting according to it.  it is entering into the circle of the people of La Ilaha Illa Allah. Because it is a circle…. And when you bind yourself within a circle…. You are leaving everything that is outside the circle…. So entereing the circle of La Ilaha Illa Allah …. Means leaving all bad stuff outside…. This is TRUE gratitude.

This is why we find every creation that Allah created in a state of constant gratitude. What does that mean?. Does that mean they're saying Thank you all the time?. NO. It means they're DOING what they were created for. They are fulfilling their responsibilities.
⟪ar-quote:أَلَمْ تَرَ أَنَّ ٱللَّهَ يُسَبِّحُ لَهُۥ مَن فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ⟫

Do you not see that Allah is praised by whomever is within the heavens and the earth. This is true praise. doing what you were created to do. The sun is in a state of hamd. the moon. the solar systems. the galaxies. animals. birds. plants. minerals. EVERYTHING is in a state of hamd. Everything is doing what it is supposed to do. This is the ESSENCE of Hamd. Isn't this also the meaning of wisdom?. To gain knowledge and then act upon it?. This is why Allah said. We gave Luqman wisdom. Be grateful to Allah. Because they're both connected in meaning.

[00:12:25]

and us being grateful to my parents is indirectly as being grateful to Allah.  Allah provides us from the unseen.  Allah protect us from the unseen.  physically I got the check in the mail or deposit in the bank.  but we know as part of our faith.  who is actually paying you?.   Allah is.  but that is in the unseen you cannot physically see it.  and you cannot trace the deposit at bank transfer directly back to Allah.  but what the parents did for you is that in the unseen or is that something that you can see and experience.  that you physically carry you in her stomach. did she physically deliver you  . . did she physically feed you. did your father physically raise you. they did. that is not some matter of faith. that you have to believe it even though you haven't seen it. you've experienced it for yourself. if you can't even be grateful for what you experience in the seen world. how can you be expected to be grateful to Allah who does everything for you from the unseen world. that doesn't make any sense. that is why Allah mentioned the parents first.

now we learn that luqman  was given wisdom.   and the first bit of wisdom that you shared with his son his do not commit shirk with Allah.  in other words the opposite of being grateful.  is being a person of shirk. and then we talked about the slavery and the elements of slavery and we discuss that you can be doing shirk in any of those categories.

Now the relationship I had with Allah. was that I was supposed to praise him and thank him. As Allah's property that was my original function. thats what I am supposed to do.
