## Section 5760

This is a continuation of the previous session. I broke down the concept of Hamd. as it relates to us in two parts.  We covered the first part last time. in which I explained what hamd means. types of hamd. there is hamd for Allah. and hamd for the sake of Allah. which is the hamd of his intermediaries. We talked about the fact that even though Allah does not NEED us. he still DOES love us. He does not NEED our praise and gratitude. but he DOES love and appreciate it. We also talked about how HAMD is a mechanism. designed by the Rabb for the progression of his ABD. It facilitate his physical and spiritual growth. and brings him closer to his Rabb. And this ability to appreciate and be grateful. has been placed within the core essence. the LUBB. of all human beings. Every child is created with this ability of Hamd.

In fact it is narrated in a hadees of Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) in which he tells us. that when Allah fashioned his first creation. Adam AS. And he blew his ROOH into him.
⟪ar-quote:ثُمَّ سَوَّىٰهُ وَنَفَخَ فِيهِ مِن رُّوحِهِ⟫

This ROOH was blown into Adam from the head down. And the hadees says. when the rooh reached his nose. it tickled him. and when something tickles your nose. what happens?. You sneeze!. So Adam AS sneezed. And appreciating the fact that he has been giving the blessing of life. that he is now alive. he instinctively appreciated the gift of life and became grateful for it. And so his immediate response to that sneeze. WITHOUT anybody teaching him anything. The first words that came out of the mouth of the the first human being. was AlHamdulillah!. Allah did not teach him that. And this is very interesting. because when it came to proving himself before the angels. ⟪ar:وَعَلَّمَ آدَمَ ٱلْأَسْمَآءَ كُلَّهَا⟫. Allah TAUGHT Adam all the divine names. When Adam and Hawwa made the mistake of reaching for the forbidden tree. they were punished. But they wanted to seek forgiveness. ⟪ar:فَتَلَقَّىٰٓ آدَمُ مِن رَّبِّهِۦ كَلِمَتٍۢ فَتَابَ عَلَيْهِ⟫. Their master taught them certain words through which they presented their repentence. So on every stage we find that Adam needed training. But not when he sneezed. Not when he recognized. appreciated. and was grateful for the blessing of life. He instinctively said.  AlHamdulillah. Because HAMD is something that Allah had ingrained it within him. within his inner nature. within his Lubb.

When Allah heard these words. he was so happy. that his slave appreciated his blessing. and he expressed his gratitude to him.that he responed back saying. Yarhamakul Allah Ya Adam. Your Allah will ALWAYS have mercy on you Oh Adam. Think about this for a second. This is the very first conversation that is taking place between the very first ABD. and his RABB. And what is this conversation?. An exchange of Hamd and Rehma. This is the first rule that is being set between the Rabb and the ABD. You come to me with HAMD. I will respond back to you with love, care, concern and mercy. Rehma!.

This is why today when we sneeze. we say AlHamdulillah. and the one who hears us sneeze says. ⟪ar:یَرحَمَکُ اللہ⟫. May Allah have mercy on you. It's a reminder of this relationship that we have as ABD. with our Rabb. And this is why even in Surah AlFateha. immediately after ⟪ar:الحمد للہ رب العلمین⟫. what comes next?. ⟪ar:الرحمن الرحیم⟫. And notice there is no other word attached with it. It's now part of a sentence. It stands all on its own. Just pure REHMA. The more Hamd the ABD does. the more mercy. the more love. the more blessings. the RABB responds with. SubhanAllah!. What a beautiful relationship this!

---

Linguistic meaning of Kausar

Then I explained why hamd has to be both elements. It has to be praise AND gratitude. We talked about why it cannot be one or the other. And then finally we talked about the relationship between Hamd and Salaah. which is a physical manifestation of Hamd. We find in Surah AlKausar. Allah says to his beloved messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam).
⟪ar-quote:إِنَّآ أَعْطَيْنَكَ ٱلْكَوْثَرَ ‎⟫

No doubt about it. we have granted you Kausar. Most translations will explain Kausar. as abundant. No doubt we have given you abundantly. But that word doesn't even come close to capturing the meaning of Kausar. The word Kausar. it belongs to an Arabic pattern. ⟪ar:فَوعَل⟫.  and this is one of the patterns of hyperbole in Arabic.  it's called ⟪ar:صیغۃ المبالغۃ⟫. AlKausar comes from kasra. or kaseer. WHICH actually means to have in abundance. to have plenty. to have lots. But AlKausar is then a hyperbole of Kasheer. It means INCREDIBLE amounts of something. When you have lots and lots and lots and lots. then you don't call it kaseer.  you call it ⟪ar:کَوثَر⟫. Allahs  says I have given you lots and lots and lots and lots. and I can keep repeating the lots as much as I want. because it is ⟪ar:کَوثَر⟫.

Then ⟪ar:کَوثَر⟫is not just about huge quantities. It also implies something extremely valuable. For example. If someone owns a huge quantity of hay. or TONS and TONS of grass or straw. they would not use the word ⟪ar:کَوثَر⟫. That would still have to use the word kaseer. For ⟪ar:کَوثَر⟫. it not only has to be huge in quantity. it also had to be enormous in its value. That's another implication in the word Kausar. No doubt we gave you huge quantities of blessings. and each and every blessing that we gave you.  is extremely valuable.

Now when you  say a LOT of something and a LOT in value. it is possible that it could be all good. or it could be all bad. or it’s a mix of both. For example. having a lot of drugs. lot of ammunition. centuries old wine cellars.  These can be in huge quantities. and they can be very expensive. but they're not good. So it is possible to have huge quantities of expensive stuff that is bad. Or some is good and some is bad. In all those cases. you would still have to use the word Kaseer. Because the word kaseer. can be used for both good and bad things. but the word ⟪ar:کَوثَر⟫.  can ONLY be used for good things. it is ⟪ar:مُتخَصَّص⟫.  It can only be used in the context of THAT which is good.

Then there are several other meanings which I'll skip. For our discussion today. in this ayah Allah is saying to his messenger.  ⟪ar:انا اعطیناک الکوثر⟫. We have given you enormous amounts of invaluable blessings. and each and every one of them. are incredibly good. Now let's quickly look at some of these incredible gifts that Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) is referring to.

### EXAMPLES

Allah says to his messenger in the Quran.
⟪ar-quote:مَا وَدَّعَكَ رَبُّكَ وَمَا قَلَىٰ⟫

We did not leave you. nor are we displeased with you…  ⟪ar:تَودِع⟫.  in Arabic is when you say goodbye. That's where you get the word. ⟪ar:الوداع⟫. And you say ⟪ar:الوداع⟫. when you are leaving someone.  So Allah is saying to his messenger. Your Rabb is not saying goodbye to you. nor is he displeased. There is a special gift in this verse.  because the expected sentence should have been. ⟪ar:ما ⟪ar:ودَّعک⟫ربک و ما قلاک⟫. There should have been a "KA" at the end of Qalaa. the English translation of that would have been. Your master did not say goodbye to YOU. and he is not displeased with YOU. but with goodbye. with ⟪ar:ودَّعک⟫.  the messenger is mentioned. but with displeasure. the messenger is not mentioned. and that is a gift of Allah to his beloved messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Cause it shows Allah's extreme love for his messenger. The word goodbye does not have any negative connotation associated with it. But the word displeasure clearly does. and so Allah does not mention his beloved messenger next to that negative word. This is how careful Allah is when addressing his messenger. And of course the lesson of the ayah is. the Allah is never going to EVER be the one to abandon his beloved messenger. 

Then he says to his messenger .⟪ar:ولا الاخرۃ خیر لک من الاولی.⟫No doubt about it. what is coming at the end. is better for you. than what is at the beginning. What an amazing gift to the messenger (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Allah is saying to him. You're being honored right now. only a few people are becoming Muslims right now. But in times to come. Islam will spread like wild fire. and your name will be honored more and more as time passes by. So what's coming later in terms of your honor. is way more than what you're seeing right now.

Then on top of that.⟪ar:ولسوف یعطیک ربک فترضی.⟫I will give you so much that you will be pleased. You know when you tell someone. I'm going to give you a gift. The verbal or non-verbal response to that is always. What are you going to give me?. how much? . What's it going to be worth?. How valuable is it going to be for me?. I bet it's the new iPad Pro because he knows I want that. And then when you unrwrap it. its a nailcutter. LOL. (True Story).

But the real question is. how WOULD would you place a VALUE on a gift?. Look at the value that Allah put on his gifts for His Messenger. he says. ⟪ar:فترضی⟫. The quantity. the value. and the goodness of the gift has been described in such a way. that I will give you SO much. I will KEEP giving you SO much. and I won't stop. until YOU yourself say it's enough. Until you say. Ya Allah I am pleased. You can stop now!. And look at the love of this amazing messenger for us (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). ⟪ar:فدا امی و ابی⟫.  He said I will not be pleased until every single person from my Ummah is saved from the hell fire. This is the value HE. (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) placed . OUR freedom. Our salvation. This is the kind of love he had for us.

And even when it comes to the rewards that Allah is going to give to his messenger.
⟪ar-quote:وَإِنَّ لَكَ لَأَجْرًا غَيْرَ مَمْنُونٍۢ⟫

My beloved messenger. You have a reward that can't even be quantified. It cannot have any brakes on it. it cannot have any limits on it. Think about it. When it came to giving the messenger blessings in this world.  the limit on it was set at what?. Until the messenger HIMSELF says enough.  and when it came to giving the rewards for his work to his beloved messenger in the after life.  Allah says. ⟪ar:وَإِنَّ لَكَ لَأَجْرًا غَيْرَ مَمْنُونٍۢ⟫. No doubt about it. I will give you SO MUCH reward that there is no number that can possibly define it. and my reward will never end. it will only keep increasing for all eternity. AllahuAkbar.

Then another gift from AlKausar. is that Allah elevated Rasul Allah beyond the seventh heaven. and spoke to him directly on the night of Meraaj. This was a gift that was not given to any prophet. any messenger before or after him. Then during their conversation. Allah bestowed another gift on his messenger. ⟪ar:ان لا ذُکرتُ الاَّ ذُکرتَ معی⟫. Allah said. My name shall not be called upon without the mention of your name along with it…… We say. ⟪ar:اشھد ان لا الہ الا اللہ⟫. And immediately what comes next?. ⟪ar:اشھد ان محمد رسول اللہ⟫. This is an incrediby valuable gift given by Allah to his beloved messenger. Name one other human being on the planet. who is being mentioned in this way constantly. Constantly.  And instead of the mention going down over time.  what happens?.  it keep going UP over time. It keeps on increasing. SubhanAllah! . And then on the same pattern Rasul Allah said the same thing for Maulana Ali. That I will not accept my name called upon until your name is mentioned along with it. And that's why immediate after the mention of the prophet. we have. ⟪ar:اشھد ان مولانا علی ولی اللہ⟫.

Another gift is that Allah made it obligatory on Muslims to remember and send praises upon the Prophet (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). So a believer is constantly looking for opportunities to do so. But not just that. Allah himself sent his praises and blessings on his beloved Prophet.
⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ وَمَلَٓئِكَتَهُۥ يُصَلُّونَ عَلَى ٱلنَّبِىِّ⟫

No doubt even Allah and his angels. CONSTANTLY send praises upon His messengers. 
⟪ar-quote:يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟ صَلُّوا۟ عَلَيْهِ وَسَلِّمُوا۟ تَسْلِيمًا⟫

So those of you who believed. you need to realize this and you need to send praise and blessings on my beloved messenger as well. And there is something really very interesting about this ayah. There are so so many ayaats in the Quran in which Allah begins with . ⟪ar:يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟⟫. But in this verse he did not beging that way. Allah did not begin by saying Oh you who believed. He began by first talking about himself and his angels. then he said. ⟪ar:يَٓأَيُّهَا ٱلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا۟⟫.  Why?. Because he's saying. I want you to realize that what I'm telling you to do.  is something I do myself.  and my angels do it too.  How  can the mention of this amazing messenger not be elevated?. And this is why we never say his name. Muhammad. without saying (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Because Allah curses the one who says the name of his beloved without praising him.

Then Allah swears by the city he lives.⟪ar:لا اقسم بھذا البلد⟫.  he swears by the city in which the messenger is born. He honors the city of Mecca. Why?. ⟪ar:وأنت حلٌّ بھذا البلد⟫.  only because YOU. my beloved messenger. because you are living in it.

Then another gift from AlKausar. Allays says.⟪ar:الم نشرح لک صدرک.⟫. Did we not open your chest for you?. And what a magnificent opening that the entire Quran can fit into it. The same Quran which would shatter and exploded mountains if it was revealed on them. 
⟪ar-quote:لَوْ أَنزَلْنَا هَذَا ٱلْقُرْآنَ عَلَىٰ جَبَلٍۢ لَّرَأَيْتَهُۥ خَشِعًۭا مُّتَصَدِّعًۭا مِّنْ خَشْيَةِ ٱللَّهِ⟫

But this same Quran  fits into the heart of the messenger. 

Another amazing gift to Rasul Allah. is an obedient ABD like Maulana Ali. When Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) had to migrate to Madina. he needed a decoy. He needed someone to sleep in his bed while he escaped to Medina. And only Maulana Ali agreed to do that. And this was the night when the kuffar were planning to assassinate Rasul Allah. And Maulana Ali knew this and he chose to sleep on his bed that night. And much later he confessed. He said. I swear! I never slept SO peacefully in my ENTIRE life.  as I slept on that night of Hijra on Rasul Allah's bed. Imagine that. People are coming to assassinate him. and he says. I never slept MORE peacefully than that night. That night was the BEST sleep I ever had in my entire life. What a gift to have an ABD like Maulana Ali. My nana. Mulla Shafaqaut Hussain. in one of his poems he referes to this incident. he says.

شب حجرت شجاعت کی، علی کی دیکھئے منظر

نڈر ہو کر باطمینان سوئے تان کر چادر

گواہی دے رہا تھا یہ رسول اللہ کا بستر

علی حیدر، علی صفدر، علی داور، علی یاور

علی ایماں ، علی قرآں، علی سلطاں ، علی آقا

Then another gift is the never ending chain of Imamat that will be from the progeny of Maulana Ali and Maulatina Fatima. And Rasul Allah compared these Imams to the arc of Nooh AS.
⟪ar-quote:مثل اهل بيتى فيكم . كمثل سفينه نوح⟫

The example of my progeny among you. is like the ark of Noah.
⟪ar-quote:من ركبها نجا . ومن تخلف عنها . غرق وهوى⟫

Whoever climbs aboard it will be saved. and whoever refuses to get onboard. will drown in this ocean of ignorance and be destroyed. And the door to that ark is AHAD Shareef. Through Ahad shareef we climb aboard this ship of Imamt. Imamat is the guarantee of salvation for his Ummah. Another incredible gift.

And there are thousands upon thousands of such gifts mentioned in the Quran and hadees. Innumerable. Invaluable gifts that Allah bestowed upon his beloved messenger. Without even him asking in most cases.

You know Ibraheem AS  made so many prayers for the Qibla. He prayed day an night to Allah. to make Bait Almaqdis the qibla for believers. To turn the hearts of the people towards it.  make this a place that is full of virtue.  and a place of peace. 
⟪ar-quote:وَإِذْ قَالَ إِبْرَهِۦمُ رَبِّ ٱجْعَلْ هَذَا بَلَدًا آمِنًۭا وَٱرْزُقْ أَهْلَهُۥ مِنَ ٱلثَّمَرَتِ مَنْ آمَنَ مِنْهُم بِٱللَّهِ وَٱلْيَوْمِ ٱلْآخِرِ⟫

He made SO many prayers. and then after all those requests. Allah made Masjid AlAQSA the qibla for Ibraheem AS and his followers.

But when Allah changed the direction of the Qibla. from AlAqsa to Masjid Haraam.  Do you know why he did it?. He explained his reason in the Quran. And that reason was. Listen to this.
⟪ar-quote:قَدْ نَرَىٰ تَقَلُّبَ وَجْهِكَ فِى ٱلسَّمَآءِ⟫

My beloved messenger. We saw your face turn towards the sky. 
⟪ar-quote:فَلَنُوَلِّيَنَّكَ قِبْلَةًۭ . تَرْضَىٰهَا⟫

and so we. are changing the Qibla  for you.  No doubt about it. ⟪ar:فَلَنُوَلِّيَنَّكَ⟫. then we swear that we are for sure. changing the qibla for you. Why?. Because you simply looked at me with that desire in your heart. SubhanAllah! . He didn't ask Allah. He did not pray to Allah. He did not make dua. He just had a sad look in his eyes. and he looked at the sky. and that very instant. the ayah comes down. Look we're changing the Qibla. ⟪ar:تَرْضَهَا⟫. To make YOU happy!.⟪ar:تَرْضَهَا⟫. so that you would be pleased. SubhanAllah!

This one action. that Rasul Allah looked at the sky with a desire for the qibla to change to Bait AlHaraam. it changed the entire world's history. Billions of people today are praying in a different direction. for one reason alone.  ⟪ar:تَرْضَهَا⟫. So that the messenger could have a smile on his face. (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) . This is an incredible thing to appreciate. The love that the creator has for his beloved messenger.

### Prayer is expression of gratitude

So now when Allah grants such gifts. on his beloved messenger. How you do you think Rasul Allah must have felt?. What did we say is the natural response for any decent human being. for any blessing no matter how small it is?. Praise and Gratitude. Right?. So then what would you imagine. would be the response of someone like Rasul Allah's.  for something like AlKausar?. Immense Praise. Immense gratitude?. right?

But how should he express that gratitude?. How does a humble. incapable. ABD. a slave. How can he express his gratitude to such a benevolent. such a merciful. such a self-sufficent. SUCH a loving Rabb?. Because the gratitude needs to be acceptable to the benefactor right?. When someone does something incredible for you. What is your reaction towards that person?. Tell me what can I do for you in return!. YOU tell me what will make you happy?. cause there is absolutely no way I can think of repaying you for this. Please tell me if there is ABSOLUTELY aything in the world that I can do for you. Does that happen?.

In history we study that people when they received an audience with the king. they would take these expensive gifts. jewels and precious stones. or something of great historic value. to gain his pleasure. Why is that?. It was to show appreciation and gratitude for that audience. The chance to stand before the king. And obviously the gift or the gratitude has to reflect the level. the status. the position of the king!.

So how do we. as ABD. as slaves. express our gratitude to the king of all kings. To the Rabb of All Rabbs?. right?.  And so now Rasul Allah has to show gratitude for not just any gift. he has to show gratitude for AL-KAUSAR. For uncountable, invaluable, blessings each one better than the next. So who can possibly dictate the terms of that gratitude?. Who is going to tell him what level of gratitude will be acceptable to him?. Obviously Allah has to set those terms. Ya Allah. with everything that you've done for me. what can I do now. to express my gratitude to you?. A praise and a gratitude that would be acceptable in your eyes?. And Allah answers that question in the very next verse as the surah continues.
⟪ar-quote:فصل لربک ونحر⟫

We have given you ALKAUSAR. We have given you gifts that are more valuable than the entire treasures and sovereignty of this world combined. with all of its assets and its wealth. So now what do you do to express your gratitude?. You establish Salaah for your master. Present your appreciation and your gratitude to your Rabb. How?. ⟪ar:فصل لربک ونحر⟫. Establish salaah for your Rabb and sacrifice. Sacrifice being a reference to Hajj. when we HAVE to sacrifice an animal. Again. Allah joins two ends together. Remember I explained to you previously he said. ⟪ar-quote:اشکر لی ولوالدیک⟫

Be grateful to me and your parents?. He combined two ends together. Allah is on the furthest end for us. parents on the closest end for us. So he mentiones the two intermediaries. but the implication is. and all the intermediaries in between. This is a typical style of classical Arabic. Here also he says.⟪ar:فصل لربک ونحر⟫ . Prayer. which is obligator EVERY single day. 5 times a day. and Hajj which is obligatory only ONCE in a lifetime. You want to be praise me and be grateful to me?. Then establish Salaah which is every single day. and Hajj which is once in a lifetime. and everything in between. So the ⟪ar:7 دعائم⟫. is the format that Rasul Allah set for us to express our gratitude to Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala). and it begins with Salaah. 

FA is a connective particle in arabic. It is used to show response.  I did this for you. SO. you do this for me.
⟪ar:إِنَّآ أَعْطَيْنَكَ ٱلْكَوْثَرَ⟫.  We gave you AlKausar. ⟪ar:ف⟫. SO. ⟪ar:صل لربک ونحر⟫. Pray to your master and sacrifice.

And we know that anything that Rasul Allah is taught in the Quran. that teaching automatically applies to us. Because he is the intermediary through which Allah speaks to us. He not only gave Rasul Allah ALKausar. He also gave US ALKausar. What greater blessing to us than Rasul Allah himself (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). Through this man we got the Quran. we got the means of our salvation. the recognition of our master. his love. his mercy. protection from hellfire. promise of heavens. And then the gift of Maulana Ali. and the panjatan. and the Imams and the duaat. and the manaseeb. teachers. parents. And so weven when we look at our lives. we have uncountable. invaluable gifts within us. And so Allah mentioned the rule in Surah AlKausar. You feeling grateful?. Salaah and Hajj and everything in between.

Heart, tongue, limbs

[diagram: Teaching diagram about Praise (al-Hamd). Three icons across the top: a red heart labelled 'HEART — Intention' containing 'الله'; an open Quran with a tongue icon labelled 'TONGUE — Claim'; a galaxy with a human silhouette labelled 'LIMBS — Evidence'. A blue arrow at the bottom defines Praise (Appreciation + Articulation + Action) and Gratitude (Gratitude + Claim + Fulfilling Purpose).]
  (see ../images/003.png)
  *Arabic labels in image:* ⟪ar:اللہ⟫
  *Note:* Pedagogical breakdown of 'al-hamdulillah': praise requires three coordinated levels — heart's intention, tongue's claim, and limbs' embodied evidence.

With that understanding. I now want to take a more granular look at Hamd. and explain its various forms of manifestation in us human beings. All of human activity. is divided into 3 parts or 3 components.  First is the heart. which is where intention (⟪ar:نیت⟫), will (⟪ar:ارادہ⟫), and belief (⟪ar:ایمان⟫) resides…… Then we have the tongue. which is called ⟪ar:ترجمان القلب⟫. The interpreter for the heart. Because it articulates what the heart feels. In other words the tongue. puts forth a claim BASED on an intention. And then finally we have the limbs. which are tools for ACTION. Action for what?. To PROVE the CLAIM. that the tongue made. BASED on the intention of the heart. I'll say that again. ACTION of the limbs. is the physical PROOF. for the CLAIM that the tongue makes. about the INTENTION of the heart.

Intention is unseen. it is invisible. It is spiritual in nature. If I am feeling thirsty and I want to drink water. that feeling is something that is in my heart. There is no way for you to know that. Because there is no hard core evidence for that intention. But then that unseen intention. is given life. THROUGH a claim. which is speech. So I articulate that feelings to you. by saying the words. I AM THIRSTY. Now. THROUGH my claim. you came to know of my intention. But the thing with claim is. it can be true. or it can also be false. And that is why the claim. then needs to be followed by an ACTION. which serves as a SOLID. substantial proof. of what the speech CLAIMED. about the INTENTION of the heart. So now if I am thirsty. and I claim that I am thirsty. And then I back that up by drinking a glass of water. My ACT of drinking water. becomes a proof. that my claim was true. and that I really was feeling thirsty. Not only do YOU become a witness to my act. I myself become a witness to it.

This is why. one of the attributes of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala).  is ⟪ar:الشھید⟫. And Shahada means two things. It means witness. and it also means testimony. Now you can't testify. until you've actually witnessed something. right?. So when it comes to this entire universe. it is divided into two parts. ⟪ar:عالم الغیب و الشھادۃ⟫. The world that is unseen (⟪ar:الغیب⟫). And the world that is seen (⟪ar:الشھادۃ⟫). Allah exists in a realm that is beyond the spiritual and physical worlds. because he is the creator of both worlds. From that unseen realm. he puts forth certain claims ABOUT himself. about his essence and his attributes. How?. Through the Quran. Through this reveleation. Why is it called revelation?. Because it is revealing to us what is hidden from us. And so Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) is making claims about himself. I am Rehman. I am Raheem. I am Azeem. I am Ghafoor. There is a reward for good deeds. There is punishment for bad deeds. I will reward you. I will punish you. right?. He is revealing himself and his intentions to us through this Quran. which is serving the purpose of a tongue. Because that's what the Quran is. It is speech. It is a ⟪ar:لسان⟫. Language.

⟪ar-quote:وَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ لَهُوَ ٱلْعَزِيزُ ٱلرَّحِيمُ ‎⟫

⟪ar-quote:وَإِنَّهُۥ لَتَنزِيلُ رَبِّ ٱلْعَلَمِينَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:نَزَلَ بِهِ ٱلرُّوحُ ٱلْأَمِينُ⟫

⟪ar-quote:عَلَىٰ قَلْبِكَ لِتَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلْمُنذِرِينَ⟫

⟪ar-quote:بِلِسَانٍ عَرَبِىٍّۢ مُّبِينٍۢ⟫

So Allah is making all these claims. revealing all these things about the unseen world!. Where is the proof?. What is the evidence for all these claims?. This physical world. The Rabb AlAlameen created this ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. as a witness. and a testimony. for his attributes and existence. And this is what we learnt in the session on Alameen. He created the ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. so that the ⟪ar:عالِم⟫ could witness the attributes of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) manifesting through his creation. and TESTIFY that whatever Allah is saying through the Quran. is in fact true. And that truly. there is no ILAH except Allah. ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫. Allah himself gave us PHYSICAL evidence for ALL his claims. to set an example for us. that ULTIMATELY it is ACTION. and not words or intentions. that hold value. And this is why if you look at the famous hadees of Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) on intentions. what does it say?
⟪ar-quote:انما الاعمال بالنیات⟫

No doubt Actions are based on intentions. There are several meanings of this hadees given by Imam Jaffar AsSaadiq AS. I'll explain ONLY one meaning today which is line with the context of our conversation today. ⟪ar:انما الاعمال بالنیات⟫. No doubt. if you TRULY intended something. your ACTIONS will prove it. And what's really interesting. is the sequence of words in this hadees. Which word is first?. Amal. or Niyyah?. ⟪ar:انما الاعمال بالنیات⟫. Amal is first. But we know that intention happens first. then why is it being said this way?. He could have said. ⟪ar:انما النیت محرک العمل⟫. No doubt intentions drive action. NO. He brought action FIRST. Because this physical world. is a world of Action. It is ⟪ar:دار العمل⟫. The house of ACTIONS. Akhira is ⟪ar:دار النیۃ⟫. the house of intentions. So anything that will be proven in this world. will be proven THROUGH action. Therefore no doubt ACTION is based on intention. If there is NO action. then you have NO evidence for your intention. and your claims of your intention are false.  In fact notice. claim is not even mentioned in the hadees. There is only action and intention. Because those are the two things that really matter. Claim is just the middle man. connecting the two things. right?

Now of course there are cases when we intend to do something. are then are not able to do ACT upon it because of certain circumstances. But those are exceptions. But the general rule is. if you truly intend something. you WILL prove it through your ACTION.

So these are the three components of an ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. Any ⟪ar:عالَم⟫. The heart (⟪ar:قلب⟫). The tongue or the claim (⟪ar:لسان⟫). and finally the limbs(⟪ar:جوارح⟫). And in the final analysis. it is the physical ACT which becomes the CLEAR EVIDENCE . for a claim. that was based on an intention. Just like this physical world manifests and testifies for the realities and the truths of a spiritual universe. Physical actions testify FOR the realities and truths of the soul.

Distribution of Hamd on 3 components

So now lets look at Hamd. and how it applies to these three parts of human activity. Hamd begins with the appreciation of a blessing. ⟪ar:إِنَّآ أَعْطَيْنَكَ ٱلْكَوْثَرَ ‎⟫. We have granted you innumerable. invaluable blessings. ALL of which are good. The ABD recognizing these blessings from his Rabb. he develops an appreciation FOR them. Where?. In his heart. He then articulates that appreciation through his tongue. he says subhanAllah! What an amazing gift. And then his limbs come into ACTION. in order to RECEIVE the benefit of that blessing…… This is the process of praise. that occurs through these three components. the heart. the tongue. and the limbs.

So this is how praise takes place. BEFORE the benefit is received. which motivates us TOWARDS the benefit.

Now once the benefit is received. what gets generated in the HEART. is gratitude for the benefactor. That feeling of gratitude. is then articulated by the tongue with words of gratitude. And then the limbs come into ACTION. to take advantage of that blessing. to put that blessing to its proper use. This is VERY important to understand. Gratitude of the heart is the recognition of a blessing. that somone did something nice for us. Gratitude of the tongue is verbalizing that feeling by saying "THANK YOU". But the gratitude of the limbs. is actually USING the benefit FOR its intended purpose.

Let's say your parents buy you a phone. which YOU don't pay for. THEY pay for it. But they buy it FOR you.  so that they can always make sure you're safe…… So that they can reach you when they need to. So that you can contact them in case you're running late. or in case of an emergency. That is why parents buy their children a phone. Now its OK. if you use that phone to talk to your friends. play games. text them. chat with them. use it as an alarm. All of that is fine. 

But if you do all those other things. but you never call your parents when you're supposed to. to let them know you're safe. If you don't answer their call when they are trying to reach you. If you don't call them when you have an emergency. then you are NOT being grateful for that phone…… You may be feeling gratitude in your heart for you. you may be saying thank you. But PHYSICALLY. PRACTICALLY. you are not showing gratitude for that phone. You understand?. Why?. Because TRUE gratitude manifests in ACTION. when you fulfill the purpose of that blessing. And this is why

⟪ar-quote:الشُّکرُ نِعمتُ العَین. خِفضُ البَصَر⟫

The eye is a blessing. The ability to see itself is a blessing. and the gratitude for the eye. the way we thank Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) for the blessing of the eye. is to lower it from the forbidden. We do not look at the things that Allah has prohibited to see. The gratitude for the blessing of hearing. is to not listen to the forbidden. the gheebah, the nameemah, the bohtaan. all this type of things. The gratitude of the tongue. is to speak the truth. and not engage it in lies. in gossip. in back-biting. Because every single part of the body is a blessing that has a specific purpose. Understanding that purpose. and fulfilling it. IS the true HAMD for that blessing.

This is what Allah means when he says.

⟪ar-quote:تُسَبِّحُ لَهُ ٱلسَّمَوَتُ ٱلسَّبْعُ وَٱلْأَرْضُ وَمَن فِيهِنَّ.  وَإِن مِّن شَىْءٍ إِلَّا يُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِهِ.⟫

The seven heavens and the earth and whatever is in them exalt Him.  And there is not a single thing that does not exalt his Hamd.

⟪ar-quote:وَلَكِن لَّا تَفْقَهُونَ تَسْبِيحَهُمْ.  إِنَّهُۥ كَانَ حَلِيمًا غَفُورًۭا⟫

But you do not understand their ways of exaltation. No doubt he is Forbearing and Forgiving.

What does it mean everything in the world is doing his hamd?. Have you seen the sun saying Thank you Allah!. Have you seen the moon. the starts. the sky. the earth. praising Allah?. How are these things showing their gratitude to him?. They are praising him. and they are showing gratitude to him. BY FULFILLING THEIR PURPOSE. That is what SHUKUR means. To fulfill its purpose. And we find the evidence of this in EVERY SINGLE creation in this universe. in nature. Every organ . ever cell within our body. knows what its supposed to do. which is praise. and then it is DOING exactly what it is supposed to do. which is gratitude.

⟪ar-quote:وَإِن مِّن شَىْءٍ إِلَّا يُسَبِّحُ بِحَمْدِهِ⟫

There is not a single thing that is not doing his Hamd. If there is a creation that is in fact NOT doing Hamd. it is us human beings. The ONLY creation for which this entire universe was created in the first place!

### False Praise

A praise that BEGINS in the heart and ENDS on the tongue. And does not translate into the ACT of benefitting from the blessing. is false praise…… It's hypocrisy…… Because you're saying one thing. but then you're doing something contrary to what you're saying. You believe Allah is your Rabb. You admit that Allah is your Rabb. But then you don't want to do what he asks you to do. That's false praise. Similarly a gratitude. that begins in the heart and ends on the tongue.  is a false gratitude. It is a delusion of gratitude. It is gratitude that has no physical. no tangible evidence. Not for you, not for anyone else…… You're just kidding yourself that you're grateful.

See. I can believe I love Allah. I can claim that I love Allah. But if I am not obeying Allah. then I am deluded about my love for Allah. Because true love is doing what the beloved asks. Even in the worldly sense.

⟪ar-quote:َزعَمتُ حُبُّ الاِلٰھِی وَ تُعصِیہُ⟫

You claim that you love Allah and then you disobey Him. 

⟪ar-quote:ان کان حُبُّکَ صَادِق .  لَطاَعَتُہُ⟫

If your love was real. you would obey him

⟪ar-quote:لأِنَّ المُحِبَّ لمِنَ یُحِبُّ.  مُطِیعُ⟫

Because the one.  who loves somebody is always obedient to them. Otherwise its just lip service. which means nothing. And this is why in Surah Yaseen Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:ٱلْيَوْمَ نَخْتِمُ عَلَىٰٓ أَفْوَهِهِمْ وَتُكَلِّمُنَآ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَتَشْهَدُ أَرْجُلُهُم بِمَا كَانُوا۟ يَكْسِبُونَ⟫

On the day of judgment. we will seal their mouths. And their hands will speak to us and their feet will testify. about what they have earned. Why?. Isn't the tongue the organ of speech?. Why is Allah sealing my mouth?. and making my limbs speak?. Because on that day. ACTION is all that is going to matter. ACTIONS will litreally speak louder than words on that day. And look in this ayah. the word used is ⟪ar:کسب⟫. earned. Why earned?. What is an earning?. It is something you GET. in return for labor or services. Earning is not something you get on good intentions. Earning is not something you get on verbal claims. Earning is ONLY based on action. right?. Blessings are always earned through the ACTION of hamd.

This is the most natural phenomenon that exists in this world. Right from birth. When a child is born in this world. its mothers milk is the first blessing it tastes. Not even milk. what the baby gets is colostrum. which is not even sweet. But even to get that. Does the baby just get it. or does it have to work for it?. The baby literally has to suck it out?. But then that's how it grows. right?. The muscles get engaged. they get stronger. And when its shows gratitude for it. which is to demonstrate that it can digest it. Because that's gratitude. To demonstrate that it is able to use the benefit for the intended purpose. What happens next?. Allah gives it the blessing of milk which is better and sweeter than colostrum…… When it can digest that. that is. show gratitude for it. they start eating semi solid foods. then solids. and then a world of different tastes open up for the child. So the benefits keep increasing. as the child demonstrates that it is grateful for the previous blessing…… and EARNS the next one. In other words. it is the HAMD of the child. that advances it through the various level of his feeding.

Salaah is Hamd in action

OK. Let's recap. What did we talk about so far?. HAMD is a response to a blessing. That response has been divided between three components. The heart, the tongue and the limbs. ACTION of the limbs. is the proof for the claim made by the tongue. about the intention of the heart.

Which means. proof of sincere praise. is that it generates in the heart. it is articulated by the tongue. and it is ACTED upon by the limbs in receiving the benefit. And proof of sincere gratitude. is that it generates in the heart. articulated by the tongue. and then the limbs start USING that gift. for the purpose it was given for.

⟪ar-quote:انا اعطیناک الکوثر⟫

We gave you ALKAUSAR. So now what do you do?. Appreciate all those blessings. and be grateful for them. And how do you express that HAMD. physically?.

⟪ar-quote:فصل لربک والنحر⟫

The first step is. Pray to your master. Now if you look at Salaah in this context of Hamd. It is a perfect manifestation of Hamd. through the heart, tongue and limbs. The ABD when he hears the AZAAN. already having recognized the glory and the blessings of his Rabb in his life. he drops whatever he is doing. to answer the call of his Rabb. The hamd is already in his heart. which physically gets him on the Musalla (Janemaaz) in order to receive the rewards of salaah. That was praise right?. the desire to receive the benefit?. And then once he begins his salaah. it is all an expression of his gratitude. And so salaah demonstrates this perfect harmony between action speech and belief. The body is doing what the tongue is articulating. and the tongue is saying what the heart believes. There is absolutely no contention. no contradiction between any of them.

Another thing which I find incredibly beautiful about Salaah. is that it is composed of two states. rest and motion. All the duas that are recited in the state of rest. are either praise of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) or it is listening to revelation. Notice our state when we are reciting the Fateha or a surah. Physically we are supposed to be completely at rest. There should be no movement in the body. why?. Because our master. our Rabb is speaking to us through the Quran. So we stand there attentively listening to his speech. And then as soon as revelation ends. we get into motion. in obedience to what the Rabb commanded us to do. And in every movement after that. we do not recite Quran. we recite a tasbeeh. And what is tasbeeh?. It is affirmation of the Rububiyyah of Allah(Azza Wa Jal). And what you believe in your heart and affirm with your speech. you HAVE to back it up with action. So we bow down before him in rukoo. with the affirmation of.

⟪ar:سبحان ربی العظیم و بحمدہ⟫

We say. my Rabb is great and is truly deserving of my Hamd. and then in order to prove that bgelief and claim. we bow down before him in Rukoo. physically expressing our humility. our servitude. while at the same time expressing our beliefs.

⟪ar:سبحان ربی العظیم و بحمدہ.⟫

Then ⟪ar:سمع اللہ لمن حمدہ⟫. Allah listens to the HAMD of those who praise him and show their gratitude to him. and as we're saying that we lift our hands to our ears. because we have the ability to listen as well. And we have heard his message. that's how we know that he listens to our hamd. Once again you can see this perfect harmony between heart tongue and limbs. And now that we believe and affirm. that Allah does listen to our Hamd. therefore what comes next?. ⟪ar:ربنا لک الحمد⟫. Our Rabb. we praise you. and we are grateful to you. and with that affirmation. we fall into sajda. which is a GREATER form of humility. It is complete physical submission. And then in that state of submission we express why we are submitting.

⟪ar:سبحان ربی الاعلی و تعالی⟫. because my Rabb is lofty and almighty. And what do you do before someone who you believe is lofty and almighty?. You submit your essence. your intellect to them. which is the act of placing your forehead on the ground. because the head contains the essence of all 5 senses. If you remember the word Sajda. it means when a camel lowers itself before its master. submitting and relinquishing control of its movements to its master.

And then if you notice. sajda. is the MOST vulnerable state from a physical stand point. Because our head is on the ground. we can no longer see who is around us. who is behind us. If somebody attacks us. we have no way of knowing. If someone is talking to us. or about us. we cannot know. because our face is on the ground with both hands on the side. Why is that?. Because ⟪ar:سبحان ربی الاعلی و تعالی⟫.  My Rabb is lofty and all might. He is lofty. so I don't care about anyone talking to me. or about me. I am not going to be distracted by the enticement of this world anymore. He is almighty. so he will protect me from my enemies. my troubles. my sorrows. my anxieties. I don't have to worry about it. My Rabb will take care of me. Its complete physical submission. So Salaah is the perfect expression of hamd. unifying belief of the heart. speech of the tongue. and actions of the limbs.  Its incredible.

Now if you take this same analogy and apply it to life. take it to the next level. the entire salaah is a state of rest. and the time BETWEEN the two prayers. is the time of motion. Salaah is like a charger for the soul. When you charge your phones. ideally you're not using it while its charging. right?. But why are you charging it?. So that you can USE it when its off the cradle. Isn't that true?. So Salaah is charging the soul. It is reminding our soul of our Hamd at all three levels. At the level of belief. at the level of speech. and at the level of action. But when salaah is over. its now time to put all of that energy to use. in our daily activities. During salaah I say.

⟪ar:سبحان ربی العظیم و بحمدہ. سبحان ربی الاعلی وتعالی. اللہ اکر. ربنا لک الحمد⟫

These are all claims aren't they?. I'm making all these claims standing before Allah in Salaah!. But where am I going to prove. that I really believe what I'm claiming to believe?. In the world. in school. in my house. at my job. in my dealings with people. with my parents. with my teachers. in my dealings with my own self. That's where I'm going to prove it.

But then when I'm in the world proving my beliefs. I am incurring MORE blessings of Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) . Not just that . because this world is an extremely challenging place for a believer. to ACT out our beliefs. because of all these distractions around us. So despite our best efforts. we make mistakes. and our soul becomes weak by the constant challenges. our battery gets drained. And so what did Allah give us after a few hours?. Another salaah. Time to recharge again. Time to be grateful again. Remind ourselves of our purpose again. Revitalize our beliefs. make those same claims again. And then when that salaah is over. get back into the world. and start proving those claims true again. And it goes on an on.  It's really amazing.

And this is why a true momin. is ALWAYS in the state of salaah. When he's not before Allah. affirming his beliefs and making claims. he's in the world proving those claims to be true. And when he is not ACTION. he is reminding himself of HAMD through Salaah. This Salaah is an amazing gift to us. this is why Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) says.

⟪ar-quote:إِنَّ ٱلْإِنسَنَ خُلِقَ هَلُوعًا⟫

No doubt about it. Human being has been created in a state of anxiety. He's always anxious. His heart is never at rest. He is easily disturbed.

⟪ar-quote:‏إِذَا مَسَّهُ ٱلشَّرُّ جَزُوعًۭا⟫

The moment a hardship touches him. he screams

⟪ar-quote:‏وَإِذَا مَسَّهُ ٱلْخَيْرُ مَنُوعًا ‎⟫

And when something good happens to him. he becomes miserly

⟪ar-quote:‏إِلَّا ٱلْمُصَلِّينَ⟫

Except the ones who pray.

⟪ar-quote:‏ٱلَّذِينَ هُمْ عَلَىٰ صَلَاتِهِمْ دَآئِمُونَ⟫

Except the ones who are CONSTANTLY in the state of prayer. They are in the state of salaah during prayer. they are in the state of salaah when they're out in the world.

<!-- section 9 (id=5761, raw_sort=9): Knowledge -->

## Section 5761

In the last session. we took a granular look at HAMD. I explained how appreciating a blessing. praise. makes us desire the benefit. And then when we benefit from the blessing. we feel the need to be grateful to the benefactor. And TRUE gratitude for a blessing. is to use it for its intended purpose. Then I explained how HAMD is split between the 3 parts of human activity. the heart. the tongue and the limbs. In today's session. I want to take a step back. and talk about how we get to actually get to appreciation. Because if we are unable to appreciate something. we cannot praise it. which mean we will be unable to benefit from it. and therefore never be grateful for it.

Scholars say that the recognition of a blessing begins with knowledge.⟪ar:العلم⟫. And knowledge is defined as. Understanding the true reality of something. ⟪ar:معرفتُ الحقیقۃ⟫. Being aware of the true reality of something is knowledge. Now appreciation begins with the knowledge of 2 things. Knowledge of a NEED. and knowledge of THAT. which fulfills the need. When these two pieces come together. we develop what is called. a TRUE appreciation for that thing. Scholars then make a further distinction between superficial appreciation. and TRUE appreciation. For example. We KNOW. that HUNGER indicates a NEED for the body. And we also know. that FOOD will satiate that hunger. That is why we appreciate food as a blessing. But then despite that knowledge. why do we waste food?. Because we're certain that there will be more food tomorrow. So what? if I throw away half the stuff on my plate today. I know I can buy more tomorrow. But if you go to one of these starving countries. I guarantee you they don't think that way. Why?. Because even though they have the same NEED as I do. they have VERY limited resources. If *I* skip meals. its because I'm dieting. When they skip meals. its because they're starving. So to them. HUNGER is VERY REAL. and that's why FOOD. is a TRUE blessing to them. But for me. Hunger is NOT that big a deal. Therefore FOOD is not such a big deal. So you can see how NEED. drives appreciation. And you can apply this to all aspects of your life. It holds true for anything in life. You go to school to learn. If that NEED to learn is REAL. If you have that THIRST for knowledge. you'll naturally appreciate your teachers. you'll appreciate the education. because they are instruments that can fulfill your need. Same applies to work. friends. to parents. and it certainly holds true for Allah and his religion. 

And so this reality has been placed in this verse we're studying ⟪ar:الحمد للہ رب العالمین⟫. Who is the Hamd for?. It is for Allah. Why?. because he is Rabb. Rabb of what?. ⟪ar:العالمین⟫. Because a Marboob NEEDS his RABB. Remember our conversation about relationships?. Children NEED parents. for parenting to take place. Students NEED teachers for learning to take place. Slave NEEDS a master for direction. Every effect NEEDS its cause. So in this verse. Alameen is the effect. that necessitates the existence of a RABB. a cause. And this why the the ALEEM created the AALAM. to manifest and reflect his attributes so that WE could become aware of the reality that HE is our Rabb. And this is why if you look at these three words. ALAM. ALIM. and ALEEM. they all share the same root word. ⟪ar:علم⟫.

Now just like all human activity is divided in 3 components. the heart. the tongue and the limbs. Knowledge also has 3 levels. The first is the knowledge of operation or function. How does a THING operate?. How does it function?. Then the second level. is knowledge of structure. What are the different components involved in the function of this entity. and how do they all come together. in a very particular order. to accomplish its function. And then finally there is knowledge of INTENT. WHY?. WHY are all these components designed this way?. What were the factors that led to the creation of this entity?. Why this material?. Why this shape?. These are all questions related to essential knowledge. INTENT.

From an Islamic theology stance. these 3 levels are called. Islam. Iman and Ehsaan. But I don't want to get technical. I want to keep keep things really simple. We'll call them. Functional Knowledge (which is Islam). Structural Knowledge (which is Eman). and Essential Knolwedge (which is Ehsaan).

Lets look at a very simple example to understand this. Let's use my usual example of a phone. It all has to begin with a NEED. So I realize this NEED. to communicate with my friends and family. I walk into Best Buy and I explain my need to the salesman. I tell him. You know. I don't know what it is. But I have this strong urge to talk to my friends across the world. And this need is keeping me up at nights. I don't know what to do. Please help me. And so he takes me to the phone section. hands me this rectangular device and says. THIS is what you need. it's called a PHONE. And I'm like huh?. Really?. This THING is what'll help me communicate with my friends?. How do I use it?.

Now when I say. How do I use it?. What level of knowledge am I seeking?. That's operational knolwedge. right?

So he turns the phone on. and he starts demonstrating how this device works. Now when he's teaching me how to use this phone. if we simplify things. what are the broad categories his teachings fall under?. The Requisites. The How To's. and Dos and Don'ts. That's it. right?

What are the Requisites?. You are absolutely required to charge your phone before you can use it. In order to do that you have to have a power outlet that uses a specific type of socket. that outputs a certain amount of voltage. You HAVE to have that to use this phone.

Second. This is how you use it. This is how you turns it on. This is how you turn it off. This is how you dial a number. This is how you download an app.

Finally. These are the things you do and these are the things you don't do. Keep the phone dry. don't take it swimming with you. It's delicate so don't use it as a door stopper. don't try to hammer a nail into the wall with it. Keep the phone clean. don't use it as a dinner plate. especially if it is PLUS size. If it gets dirty. wipe it with a clean cloth. You don't have to put it in the washing machine and then the dryer. twice. So that's dos and don'ts.

That's it. Those are the 3 categories of operational knowledge. The Requisites. How to use it. and the Dos and Donts. If you do these things. this instrument will satisfy your need. to communicate with your friends and family.

Now we know. that internally. every phone is made up of certain components that are structurally placed a certain way. There is a battery. a circuit board. a camera. microphone. memory. CPU. Now these are all completely different. completely independent components. Yet they are arranged in a VERY specific manner. to accomplish one single goal. Allow me to use the phone. If I change anything in that structure. the phone will no longer work. right?. So this is all structural knowledge. or component level knowledge. 

Now do I need to know any of this to operate the phone?. NO. I just need the operational knowledge. right?. How to turn it on. how to dial a number. and talk. I don't need to know the techincal details of how things are working under the hood.

Who needs to know those kinds of details?. The phone repair guy. a technician needs to know that. right?. So that when it stops working. he can fix it. Because that is the level of NEED. he operates at. He NEEDS to have the knowledge of structure. what goes where!. how each individual component works. But you and I don't. Because we're operating at the consumer level. The repairman on the other hand. is operating at a higher level of knowledge. But when he makes calls. despite his additional knowledge. does he use the phone EXACTLY the same way as me?. ABSOLUTELY. But at the same time. does he have a much greater appreciation for how the phone works?. Of course. Hes has a much greater awareness. and a much greater appreciation for it.

Where I'll say things like. look how beautiful the icons look on this phone. He'll say things like. Actually. these are 24bit pixels being illuminated from this light source in the back. and each pixel is capable of showing 10 million colors. right?. Completely different levels of appreciation. My point is. EVEN though he and I will use the phone in EXACTLY the same way. because of his knowledge of structure and components. he can appreciate things about this same phone which I cannot.

And then there is the designer. The guy who actually designed each and every component of this phone. This is the guy who designed the circuit board. the camera. the microphone. the screen. and then puts all these things together in this particular order. Now this guy is operating a COMPLETLEY different level. He has an appreciation of the phone. which you and I can't even imagine right?.

If I say. look how beautiful the icons look on this phone. and the technician says. these are 24bit pixels being illuminated. THIS guy says. let me tell you WHY I designed it this way. Why I used 24 bit colors and not 32 bit colors. Let me tell you why I used copper here. and a plastic there. Let me show you all the things I put into place just to get this one component working. Let me tell you how this technology evolved from here. and what I'm planning to do 10 years from now.

This is the level of INTENT. Where the designer is actually letting you enter his head. And when we understand his thought process. now we have an appreciation like never before. And who do we actually appreciate THROUGH the appreciation of the phone?. The designer himself right?. DUDE! You're a genuis. This is such PERFECT design. It's AMAZING.

But now when it comes to using this phone. Does the DESIGNER also use the phone. EXACTLY the same way as the technician does. and as we do?. ABSOLUTELY.

So you see. at the operational level. at the level of Islam. functionally. we are all the same. We all do the EXACT same things. From  Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) to Maulana Ali. to Imams. to Duaat. to Manaseeb. we ALL perform salaah EXACTLY the same way. We're all the same on the level of function.

But when it comes to the inner realms of knowledge. at the structure and design level. what we get are ranks. or MARAATIB. one technician will know more than the other. But no matter WHO knows HOW much. all levels of knowledge exist to serve one. and one purpose alone. OPERATION of the instrument.

Think about it. What was the INTENT of the designer when he was designing the phone?. Was it just the design of the phone. or was it its USE?. It was usage right?. If he put this AMAZING. MIND BLOWING. design together. Used the BEST possible material for the components. Arranged it in the BEST possible way. But nobody used it. Would any of it matter?. NO. So INTENT and STRUCTURE. are all geared towards one single purpose. its USE. Because it is ONLY the actual USE of the device. that will bring about the benefit. Only by USING the phone. will I satisfy my NEED. to communicate with friends and family. You understand?. So if I have ALL the knowledge that exists about the phone. But I don't actually USE the phone. I will not benefit from it. And on the other hand if I ONLY have the operational knowledge of phone. and I know nothing more than that. I will still benefit from it. IF i put it it to use. So in the end what it boils down to. is ACTION.

Isn't that what we said about our existence?. There is the heart that holds the intent. the highest level of knowledge. Then there is the tongue. which provides structure to the intent. How?. See a thought. a desire. or an intention. These are all just mental images. They don't have any particular structure. But when we speak. we give that intent. the structure of words. Isn't that what speech is?. It is structured words. in a particular sequence based on grammatical rules. You break that structure. and you can no longer deliver the intent. And then finally. there are the limbs. which are tools of operation. They are the dos and donts of the intent. they are the prerequisites to EXECUTE the intent. They physically execute the intent. And in the final analysis. it is ACTION. and not words or intent that is considered EVIDENCE. It is ACTION. and not words or intent that provides BENEFIT. right?. It is the ablity to communicate with the phone. and not its structure or its design that matters.

AND YET. intent and speech. contribute to the strength and the quality of my action. The stronger my intention. the stronger my belief. the more eloquent. the more powerful my speech will be. And that will translate into a LOT MORE effort in the quality of my action. So you see. even though these are 3 different things. in essence they are the same thing. When all three things combine. When the heart believes. And the tongue articulates what the heart believes. And the limbs ACT upon what the tongue claimed about the heart's belief. THAT's when you get PERFECTION in action. This is why a true believer.  is defined as the one who comprises all three things.

⟪ar-quote:تصدیقٌ بالجنان. قولٌ بالسان. و عملٌ بالارکان⟫

A PERFECT believer is the one who believes in his heart. articulates that belief with his tongue. and ACTS upon that belief with his limbs. In other words there is absolutely NO contradiction. NO conflict between his belief. his speech and his actions. They're all the same.

---

Now understanding these levels of knowledge. if we look at the ALAM. the whole idea becomes to REVERSE ENGINEER it. Because when we study the ALAM. what we see. is how it works. how it functions. So we study how it operates. to understand its structure. so that we can understand the INTENT of the creator. Because every. THING. ⟪ar:شئی⟫. has within it. the ⟪ar:مشیئا⟫. and the ⟪ar:منشاء⟫. the WILL. and the INTENT of its creator.

If you think about our phones. We are all using them. in this particular way. BECAUSE that was the ⟪ar:مشیئا⟫. and the ⟪ar:منشاء⟫. the WILL. and the INTENT of its designer. If we reverse engineer the phone. we connect its operation. to the structure of the components. we can determine the will of its designer. The reason everything is structured this way. is BECAUSE. this is how the designer INTENDED for me to use it. And then the user manual confirms that.

So the idea is. study the operations. and the structure of this ALAM. through the manual of the Quran. to understand the INTENT of the RABB. Now when we look at this universe. just like a phone or any other devise. this AALAM is comprised on many different components. But desipite these complete disparate components. it is acting as a single entity. with one UNIFIED purpose. To serve human beings. And if PRAISE is understanding the purpose. and gratitude is ACTING FOR that intended purpose. then EVERYTHING in nature is in a state of HAMD. Because everything understands its purpose. and it does EXACTLY what its supposed to do. which is to serve me. make life possible for me. This is what I learn from my study of how this world is operating.

Which then forces me to think. I TOO am a creation. just like them. Therefore I must ALSO have a purpose. I must also have a HAMD. What is my HAMD?. What is MY praise?. What is MY gratitude?. Because I am a fully functioning. fully operational unit. comprised of all these independent components. I have not only been given the gift of sight through my eyes. I have ALSO been given the gifts of scenery. All the things around me that I can see. I have ALSO been given light. the medium which enables me to SEE things. Again 3 things. The ability to see. the objects that CAN be seen. and the medium through which I can see them. Similarly I have not only been given the gift of hearing. I have also been given the gift of sounds in this world. and the medium of AIR. which enables me to hear these sounds.

I know I did not work for any of these things. Therefore by definition. these are all gifts. And I realize that all these GIFTS. they have a very specific structure to them. My eyes exist in the top part of my face. What if it was in my belly?. Would I be able to see the world the same way as I do today. What if I had one eye on my forehead. would that limit my vision?. Because of how they are placed. my eyes provide me with a linear line of sight. with some peripheral vision. but my ears gives me access to sounds in a complete circular fashion. 360 degrees. because they're placed on the side of my head. What if they were placed on my feet?. or anywhere else except where they are right now?. How would that have worked out for me?. And then why is everything been placed in such a perfect balance?. EVERYTHING that exists on the sides. inside and outside my body. they exist in pairs. And EVERYTHING that exists in the center. stands alone. We have one brain. one nose. one mouth. one neck. one heart. one belly button. one genetal. because they're all in the center. And everything on the side exists in pairs. whether internal or external. eyes. lungs. kidneys. arms. feet. Anything that's on the side. if one side fails. I can still survive using the other. Anything in the center fails. that's it for me. This is INCREDIBLE structure. My eyes can see all the way to the horizon?.  Why can't my ears hear sounds. as far as my eyes can see things. Why can't my nose smell things as far as my ears can hear sounds?. Why can't me tongue taste as far as my nose can smell?. Why do I have this gradual degradation within my senses?. Are these capabilities placed within me to benefit me or harm me?. There is a book in which Imam Jaffar AsSaadiq explains human design to his Dai Hazrat Mufaddal. All his arguments prove one thing. Every creation on this planet has been given EXACTLY what they needed. Not less and not more. Because any less and it would have hurt them. and ANY more and it would have hurt them. There is SO MUCH wisdom in this design. I see everything has been put into place. very systematically. PERFECTLY. to benefit me.

So now that I realize I have been given SO MANY gifts. that are uncountable. invaluable. and ALL good. ⟪ar:انا اعطیناک الکوثر⟫. No doubt about it. we have given you Kausar. Why are these Kausar for me?. Because I now have the KNOWLEDGE of how much I NEED these gifts. And what a disaster it would be. if I even LOST one of these gifts. Forget losing. How much would I suffer if any of these gifts even deteriorated. Therefore. ALLAHUAKBAR. It is clearly BEYOND my ability to praise Allah for these amazing gifts. He is BEYOND my ability to be grateful to him for these incredible gifts. So what do I do now?. ⟪ar:فصل لربک والنحر⟫. Establish Salaah for your Rabb. and sacrifice.

For the one who REALIZES. the NEED. to praise Allah. For the one who realizes. that he has a NEED to be grateful to Allah. for such a person. these forms of worship. are a TRUE blessing. Because they help him satiate that NEED. that HUNGER. to be grateful to Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala). But for the one who is ungrateful. For someone who is stuck in the filth of this DUNIYA. who is stuck at the level of the physics chemistry and biology of THINGS. and cannot see anything else beyond that. All he knows is to use these gifts to pursue vain pleasures. chase empty desires.

For the one completely obsessed with himself. his money. his youth. his beauty. his cars. his business. his children. Who believes HE is the creator of his destiny. who believes HE is his own ILAAH. For such a person. worship means ABSOLUTELY nothing. Salaah means NOTHING to such a person. It is as valuable to him. as a phone is valuable to a monkey. Because he has no knowledge. He has no knowledge of his NEED. and so he is not even going to bother looking for THAT instrument. that can satisfy his need.

I was talking to one of the kids the other day. and she told me she's studying how nerve endings work in school. and how these signals are transmitted to the brain when we touch something. And she said. I turned to my friends and said. How can this be without design?. How can this be evolution?. And I felt SO happy. I immediately remembered this hadees of Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam). that a DISBELIEVER is bewildered by creation. but a BELIEVER is bewildered by his creator. 

⟪ar-quote:الکافر حائرٌ فی المخلوق. والمؤمن حائرٌ فی الخالق⟫

Another kid in her class. same intellect. same maturity. receiving the exact same knowledge of design. she would stop at the level of creation. but she saw Allah behind it. SubhanAllah!. Because this is what the RABB AlALAMEEN wants. For us to study and decode this physical ALAM. to SEE the RABB working behind it. So in essence what Yasu said in her own way. is. ⟪ar:لا الہ الا اللہ⟫. How can this be from anyone other than Allah?.

You know. it is so INCREDIBLE. that how these Arabs. in their eloquence. they did not call human beings. ⟪ar:الحیوان العاقل⟫. The intellectual beings. Instead they called them. ⟪ar:الحیوان الناطق⟫. The articulating animal. Or the animal of reason. Because ⟪ar:نطق⟫is also the root word for ⟪ar:منطق⟫. which means reason or logic. and we need language in order to reason. We can't think without language. If you ever catch yourself thinking. you'll notice you're using your native language to think in. So they called human beings ⟪ar:الحیوان الناطق⟫. because of their ability to articulate. Why?. Because Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) granted this ability to speak ONLY to human beings. as a sign. Because if you look at speech. What is speech?. It is encoding and decoding. I am encoding my intent. I'm taking a MEANING. which is spiritual or meta-physical in nature. and I am encoding that into a structure of physical words. You are then listening to those physical words. decoding it. and extracting the meaning from it. SubhanAllah!. And this langugae. this ability to encode and decode. is what we have as the MOST basic level. Why?. Because THAT is the very nature of this AALAM. It is the WORD of Allah. It is encoded in the physical. so that we can decode it. to extract the MEANING. the meta-physical from it. which is purpose of its creation. Talk about clear signs.

So now if we look at salaah. or any other form of worship for that matter. It is also a physical THING. It is ⟪ar:شئی⟫. It belongs to the world of worship. Its from ⟪ar:عالم العبادۃ⟫. It's an instrument. and instrument satisfy needs. What is that need that it was built for?. HAMD. Salaah is the food. for the hunger and thirst of HAMD. Our internal NEED for HAMD is what drives us towards Salaah. I cannot emphasize this enough. People ask. why do I need to pray?. It's VERY simple. Are you grateful to your Rabb?. Do you feel the NEED to express your gratitude to him. in a way THAT would make HIM happy?. Then salaah is your answer. It's really that simple.

This is how a believer judges his own gratitude. If you want to know whether you're grateful or not. measure yourself against salaah. Look!. whether I want to talk to you or not. is determined by whether I use my phone or not. correct?. If I really want to talk to you. I'll pick up the phone and I'll call you. If I'm hungry. I'll eat. If I'm thirsty. I'll drink. That's how I know I was thirsty. because I ENJOYED the drink. I know I was REALLY hungry. because I ENJOYED the food. I know I really wanted to talk to you. because I ENJOYED the conversation. If you want to know whether you're grateful to Allah for KAUSAR or not. see if you enjoy SALAAH.

I personally feel this is such a blessing from Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala) that he gave us these tools to measure ourselves against. Because we are delusional creatures. We THINK we love. We THINK we're just. We THINK we believe. How do we know for sure?. These are the standards that Allah set for us. These are like symptoms for us. How does a doctor diagnose a physical problem?. through symptoms. right?. If I have a fever. along with a sore throat and runny nose. I clearly have diabetes. LOL. Good thing I didn't go into medicine. 

Knowledge of symptoms. are such an enormous blessing from Allah. Because if we didn't have these symptoms. how would we ever fix the problem? right?. So if I'm feeling this repulsion from Salaah. something is wrong with my HAMD. That's what I need to work on. This is where people go wrong. When someone is not motivated for prayers. they start forcing them with ⟪ar:وعید⟫. threats of hellfire. punishment. force. beating. But does that really work?. It doesn't. Because you're not addressing the root cause. HAMD. The question to ask is. why is this person not in NEED of HAMD. What is he missing?. Because HAMD is the MOST natural thing for a human being. You just have to get them there. Once that thirst develops. salaah is just a natural response to it.

---

Now let's look at the 3 levels of knowledge in the context of religion. The first is ⟪ar:شریعۃ⟫. which is the knowledge of operation and function. And this is all about Huqooq (Rights). It begins with Huqooq Allah. The Rights of Allah. These are all the forms of worship. and matters that are related to dealings between the ABD and his Rabb.

Then you have Huqooq AlNafs. Rights of the soul. These cover topics like personal hygine. and day to day etiquettes. how to eat. how to sleep. how to talk. what to say what not to say. how to use the bathroom. what to see. what not to see. What to heart. what not to hear. Basically all rules related to the body and soul.

Then you have Huqooq AlIbaad. Human Rights. These are all related to dealings and interactions with others. These cover laws of marriage. inheritance. politics. contracts. trade. economics. judicial matters. etc.

It's interesting that this word Shareeah. comes from ⟪ar:شارع⟫. which means road. But ⟪ar:شریعۃ⟫is not just any road. It is a specific road that leads to water. Imagine the Arab desert. scorching heat. blazing sun. extremely dry weather. What could possible be the GREATEST of all blessings for an Arab in the desert?. Water right?. So to them this life. this world was like a hot scorching desert. which in their case. it literally was. And Aakhira or jannah was like a body of cool water.

Now when you're driving on any road. there are laws to be obeyed. for example speed limits. right of way. And these laws are set by a governing body.which are all covered by Huqooq Allah. Then YOU are the one actually taking the journey. so you need to apply certain rules for yourself. like for example. seat belts. check your side mirrors. rearview mirrors. Make sure your car is clean. It is well serviced. well maintained. You've filled it up with gas. These are all covered by Huqooq AlNafs. And then there are all these people travelling besides you on the road. There are rules of interacting with them. right of way. slow lane. fast lane. signal when you're turning. These are all covered by Huqooq AlIbaad (Human rights). So to the Arabs. if they followed the Shareeah. if they abided by these three rights. Rights of Allah. Rights of Self. and Rights of others. it would guarantee. that they would ALL. successfully reach water.

Now everything dictated by shareeah. they're all physical actions. no matter what category of Huqooq you take. They are all physical actions. instruments. Which means they all have prerequisites. they all have dos and don'ts. and they all have How Tos. So if you take salaah as an example. its operational knowledge would be. understanding its pre-requisites. Taharah. That's the first pre-requisite. THEN complete wudu. These are ABSOLUTELY required things. You want to charge the phone battery. you gotta plug the charger in the wall. You may not understand HOW or WHY the charger is charging the phone. but you know it WILL definitely charge. Wudu literally creates that connection. It plugs you into the spiritual socket.

Now Wudu is its own THING. Which means it has its own set of pre-requisites. How Tos and Dos and Dont's.

Then there are the do's and donts of salaah. You can do certain things. and you can't do certain things. You have to recite Surah Fateha. but then you have a choice to recite which ever surah you like after that. You have to do ruku with the tasbeeh. but then you can extend the ruku with other tasbeeh as much as you want. You can't look away from the sajda. you can't speak with anyone. you can't read anything. These are all the How To's of salaah. This is how this instrument works. Makes sense?. Why do I have to do Salaah?. To express my Hamd. How do I operate this instrument called Salaah?. Meet the pre-requisites. follow the dos and don'ts. Keep your hands inside the janemaaz at all times. Simple.

Now once you've gained an understanding of the Shareeah. Once you've gained the knowledge of the NEED to HAMD. and you've gained the knowledge of THAT which will fulfill your need. which is Shareeah.  You're on the road that will lead you to water. You have a direction. you know what you need for you YOURSELF. and how to interact with others. Once you've perfected the outward form. the next level of knowledge is. ⟪ar:علم التاویل⟫. The knowledge of Taveel. This is the knowledge of the components. and what they represent. The Misaal and the Mamsool. The symbol and the one it symbolizes. So for example in wudu. why are there certain parts I must wash. and then others that I only have to do masah on?. What does washing symbolize?. What does Masah symbolize?. When I wash my face. why should I put water in my eyes?. In salaah. what does Rukoo symbolize. what does Sajda symbolize. what does Qayaam symbolize. And how are they all connected together. Why Qayam comes first. then rukoo. then sajda. Why is there one rukoo and two sajda. Why is it that I spread my fingers on my knee when I'm in Rukoo. but I bring them together when I'm in sajda. All of this falls under the knowledge of Taveel.

The word taweel means. ⟪ar:رجع الی الاول⟫. returning to the beginning. How it all started. And how do you do that?. How do you get to the beginning?. But tracing back the symbols to the ones they symbolize. By decoding the external physical form. to understand what they represent in their counterpart. their interal spiritual form. The external forms are all signs. ayaats. Misaal. They point to the Mamsoolaat. And you trace one sign after the other. and that's how you get to where it all started. The awwal. It is listerally a bridge that connects the Shareeah. to its purpose.

⟪ar-quote:التاویل جَسَرَ الحقائق⟫

Taweel. is the bridge that leads to realities. But if you have not practiced. and mastered the external form. how are you going to understand the internal represenations?. If you don't know the symbols. how are you going to get to the symbolized?. You can't do calculus without learning algebra right?. Can't run until you learn how to walk. you'll fall.

So Taveel connects you to this third level of knowledge. which is the knowledge of the ESSENCE. or the INTENT. It is the knowledge of how it all began. and how it will all end. The knowledge of pre-existence. and eternity. What happened before this physical universe came into existence. What were the factors that led to the creation of this physicality. Why did all of this come into existence. where did it come from. where is it going. how will it all end. WHEN will it all end. What are the realities of these oceans. these trees. the celestial bodies.  That's all covered by the knowledge of the origin. and the return. Mabdaa and Maad.

Shareeah gave us knowledge of the form. Taveel helped us return to the beginning. by tracing the components to their design. Mabda Maad. is how and why these components originated. why they were made this way. why they have this form. this shape. and how will this all return back to where it came from. And then just as in the study of matter today. we can study things at a molecular level. at an atomic level. at a sub-atomic level. There are also realms of knowledge that explain each composition at an extremely minute level. So then you have haqaiq. After that you have Daqaiq. After that you have Haqaiq Alyia. After that you have Daqaiqul Daqaia. After that you have Ifaadaat. So you can see there is no end to knowledge.

And BTW how do you verify all these 3 levels of knowledge?. How do you prove to yourself that these concepts are not made up fictitious stuff?. Because you can't use the physical universe to prove them. Mabda Maad is a realm of knowledge BEFORE physicality even existed. So how to you know for sure that all of this is true?. The Quran. EVERY single thing can be proven from the Quran. Hazrat Zia Ali Sahab used to say. The ignorant thinks the Quran is just a book of stories. But the AALIM knows that its a book of Haqaiq and Daqaiq.

I hope. I've given you SOME clarity on how all of this is organized. and the importance of a systematic. progressive study. I know a lot of people. who've studied a little bit of this. a little bit of that. and a ultimately a whole lot of nothing. This is because they just study randomly. little bit from here. little bit from there. So that's what they end up with. Random knowledge. confusions. So you have to study systematically. but that takes a lot of patience.

And BTW. where do these sessions fit into this?. All I'm hoping to do in these sessions. is show you the way to get you from the scorching sands of the desert. to this road that will lead you to water. I hope and pray. I'm getting you to the ⟪ar:شارع⟫. But there is a LONG LONG road ahead of you. You HAVE to learn Shareeah. before you learn TAVEEL. before you learn Mabda Maad. It's a LONG journey. But I can tell you from personal experience. WALLHI.It's an AMAZING journey. But I can only get you to the road. You're the one who has to walk on it. We all have our own walking to do. And walking. is a PHYSICAL act. It is not a verbal claim. and it is not a good intention. It is physical work.
