---

For those of you who have time. I want to share 4 things. that have really helped me improve my salaah. And I hope that InshaAllah it does the same for you.

The first and foremost is. REMEMBER why you are praying. remember the purpose of this instrument. We appreciate Allah's blessings. and we NEED to express our gratitude to him. and the tool given to us. to statisfy that NEED of HAMD. is salaah. That is the ONLY reason to pray.

But then while we're perfecting our prayers. through daily practice. we also need to make an effort to study taveel and mabda maad. because what these uloom do is. they increase our CONVICTION of HAMD. They raise the intensity of Hamd in our hearts. They make us more appreciative. more grateful for Allah's blessings. Look. from Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) to Maulana Ali. to Imams. to Duaat. to manaseeb. to us. we're all doing the EXACT same salaah. But the quality of conviction is different at each level. And what gives strength to that conviction. is these higher realms of knowledge. The MORE you know. the more THIRSTY you will be HAMD. and the more you will want to drink from this fountain of salaah. So that's my first recommendation. Study. Make that effort. I promise you it will be a rewarding one. Begin by studying the Shareeah. and perfecting the outward.

**Shareeah. even though the most precious thing we have. it is the most undervalued entity in our lives

It teaches us discipline. love. patience. courage. ettiquettes. hiearrchy. ADAB. It teaches us all the divine attributes.

Designed and formulated by Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) . He witnessed the spiritual world. and designed Shareeah on the same pattern for us.**

Then the next thing is. Understand what you say in salaah. You don't have to be a master of Arabic for that. All translations are available. I have translated pretty much all the duas for you. Make an effort to understand them sentence by sentence. And to begin. Begin with your rukoo and and sujood. Slow them down. Some of you guys pray so fast. I'm sure it starts a hurricane somewhere. No wonder texas gets so many hurricanes. Its because of your rukoo and sujood. When you go into rukoo. the person standing next to you gets hit with a wind. SWOOSH. LOL. Slow down. At least slow down your rukoo and your sujood. Start there. Visualize your HAMD when you're in RUKU. Subhana Rabi alazeem wabihamdih. My Rabb is SO perfect and amazing. and he is worthy of all praise and gratitude. Subhana Rabbiyal Aala wataala. My Rabb is so lofty and so mighty. Reflect on these words. Do this JUST for your FARZ. forget the rest. Just FRAZ.  That's not much to do right?. But reflect on these words. These are EXTREMELY powerful words. SubhanAllah and AlHamdulillah. They are the MOST beloved words to Allah(Subhanhu Wa Ta'ala). Rasul Allah (Salallahu alayhi wa aalihee wa sallam) said in a hadees.

⟪ar-quote:کلِمَتَینْ. خَفِیفَتَینِ عَلی الِّسَانْ. ثَقِیلَتَینِ فِی المِیزَانْ. حَبِیبَتَینِ اِلَی الرَّحمٰنْ⟫

Two words. ⟪ar:کلِمَتَینْ⟫. SubhanAllah and AlHamdulillah.⟪ar:خَفِیفَتَینِ عَلی الِّسَانْ⟫. Extremely Light on the tongue.

⟪ar:ثَقِیلَتَینِ فِی المِیزَانْ⟫. Extremely Heavy on the scales on the day of judgment.

⟪ar:حَبِیبَتَینِ اِلَی الرَّحمٰنْ⟫. Extremely beloved to the Rehman.

And we're constantly repeating these words in our tasbeehaat. So start there. and slowly make an effort to expand that out. Understand the surahs. then the tashahhud. and then expand. It will help a LOT with your focus. This is the reason why we lose focus. Because we don't know what we're saying. If I started doing these sessions in Urdu right now. how long will it take. before those of you who don't understand Urdu. how long before you pass out?. Few minutes right?. That's what happens in salaah. we begin with this enthusiasm. and then we zonk out. because we don't know what we're saying. So that's my second suggestion.

The next thing is make salaah an EVENT in your life. Salaah and ALL forms of worship are NOT meant to be an activity. they are meant to be an experience. We have to learn to experience our salaah. Prepare for it. think about it in advance. When you wake up in the morning to go to school. Do you just roll out of bed and head out to school?. Actually I know some of you do. LOL. But hopefully there are some. who actually prepare for school. Parents. when you get ready to go to work. you don't just get up and walk out right?. You shower. you dress up. and then you head out. Because work is a really important thing. isn't it?.

Well guess what?. Salaah is a MUCH MORE important thing. Allah. our RABB. is a very important entity. Orepare for him. Dress up for him. A person who is praying in his Tshirts and Pajamas. CLEARLY does not understand what he's doing. If you're doing that. especially for Fajr. you have ABSOLUTELY NO idea who you're standing before and what you're doing. Cause I guarantee you. you would not show up to work and stand before your boss in that outfit. The outfit that you're standing in. before ALLAH.

Some say. oh its not haraam. Its pure 100% cotton. so techincally I can pray in it. Well techincally it's not illegal for you. to show up to work in your bathrobe and slippers. is it?. If technicality is all that matters. then show up like that to work. You won't get arrested. Why don't you?. Because you know your boss will not like that. it is disrespectful to him. Well Salaah. is not meeting your boss. it is not meeting your teacher. it is meeting your creator. your Rabb. Be mindful of that. It'll completely change your experience of salaah. Start thinking about salaah. and start preparing for it in advance. Before you begin your day. check the timings for all prayers. and plan your day accordingly. Make it a priority in your life. It's like anything else in life. If you make it important. it WILL become important. It's all up to you.

And try not to pray late. Pray in the earlier portion of the time. Understand that it's our RABB that is calling us. What'll happen if I show up to work 45 minutes late everyday. and tell my boss. Oh you know.  the second I wanna leave.  my son wraps himself around my leg and starts crying. that's why I come in late everyday. It's SO cute I'll show you a video next time. I don't think my boss will find that cute. If it makes sense to not keep my boss waiting. then how can it make sense to keep my master. my Rabb waiting?. so try your best to pray at the earliest time possible. I promise you it'll change your experience of salaah. I understand it's not always easy to do that with our work and life styles. But atleast try to do the best you can.

I always remind myself of this fact. that a dog. chewing on a bone. What's the MOST pleasurable delight in the world to a dog. a bone. But when its master calls. it drops the bone and comes running to its master. So how is it then. that my glorious master. RABB AlALAMEEN. He calls me. ⟪ar:حی علی الصلوۃ. حی علی الفلاح⟫. and I just keep doing what I'm doing. ignoring him completely?. May Allah protect me from falling to a level. which would make a dog look better than me.

And finally. measure your salaah by the time you spend when you're NOT in salaah. This is the HARDEST PART. for ALL of us. Make an effort to be obedient to Allah. And this is where you will see the effects of your salaah. Every instrument in the world. has a definitive result. right?. How do I know your knife is working properly. because it cuts. A microwave is working properly. if the food is coming out hot. My phone is working properly. if I'm able to communicate with people. EVERY instrument has a definitive result. What is the result of salaah?. How do you know your salaah is working?. Is it some special tingly feeling in your chest while you're in prayer?. No. that's heart burn.

Where do the effects of salaah show up?. When you're not in salaah. TAQWAA. Consciousness of the presence of Allah in your life. If you are thinking more and more about your Rabb. while you're in school. while you're at work. If your sins. your evil actions are constantly eating at you. they disgust you. if your good actions for the sake of Allah are beginning to please you. KNOW that your salaah is working. But even after praying 5 times a day. all you're doing is lying. cheating. gossiping. back biting. hurting peoples feelings. using foul language. watching filth on the internet. then you're not really praying. EVEN if you're going through the motions. Something is VERY  wrong there. If the power outlet in the wall is working. and the charger is working fine. but the phone is still not charging. Where's the problem?. The phone battery. right?. The battery is dead. You can't show up to salaah with a dead heart and expect salaah to charge it for you. Evil acts. Sins. they KILL the heart. Allah says.

⟪ar-quote:وَأَقِمِ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ ۖ إِنَّ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ تَنْهَىٰ عَنِ ٱلْفَحْشَآءِ وَٱلْمُنكَرِ⟫

Establish prayer. No doubt about it. salaah prevents you from evil and ludeness. And the word INNA is used there. which means DEFINITELY. ABSOLUTELY. NO DOUBT IT. Salaah prevents you from evils and shamelessness. So if someone is praying. and still engaged in shameful acts. then they're not really praying.

## Section 5754

Intro

What is love? - benefit. from Hubb. seed

---

Let me explain gratitude to you. In classical arabic. the word for gratitude is شکر. Even in Urdu you say. شکریہ. in arabic you say. شُکراً. So the tri-literal root for these words is شکر. And you can see that the three letters are connected. There is no gap in between any of these. The first letter sheen. represents the gratitude of the heart or the mind. which is the recognition of the benefit. the second letter represents the tongue praising. or eulogizing the benefactor. and the third letter is fulfilling the purpose of the benefit. So gratitude. or شکر. involves the heart. the tongue and the limbs. When the heart recognizes the benefit. the tongue praises the benefactor. and the limbs get busy with acquiring the benefit as intended by the benefactor.

You insert yourself into the benefit. you start using it for your own benefit. in ways not intended for us. you get شرک. same letters. different sequence.  SubhanAllah! 

that start using the benefit what what's NOT intended. For example. Allah gave me a tongue. to articulate my emotions. and ultimately praise him. But instead I use it to hurt people. I use it to sing stupid songs. I use it to gossip. to backbite. to slander. In other words I corrupt it's purpose. and now what happens. it's no longer gratitude. it's ingratitude. That's why when I change the sequence of the letters in شکر. what do I get?. I get شرک.

And shukar is based on 5 foundations.

1. humility towards the benefactor

2. love for him

3. acknowledgment of the benefit

4. praising the benefactor

5. not using the gift in a manner which the benefactor dislikes.

And what that does is. کَشْرٌ. Same 3 letters?. which means the act of uncovering. or exposing to view. that which was hidden. which is the blessings of Allah. resulting from Shukr.

شَکَر. is when a camels udder fills up with milk to the point that it looks like its going to burst. that's شَکَر. And when the baby camel sucks out the milk from such a full udder. that process is called. شَکِرَۃ. to benefit completely from abundant blessings of Allah. What happens when then the baby sucks drinks the milk?. becomes strong?.

The word begins with the letter. sheen. which is for شئی. And I just told you that. شئی. is the manifestation of the will. شئی. is from مشیئا. OK?. So in this example. Khala's مشیئا. her will was love. and what came out of it. the شئی.  is the meal. which is a manifestation of her love. makes sense?. That's sheen. How many letters after that?. Kaaf and Ra. I won't go into the linguistics of it, because it'll get too complicated and overwhelming. and I'll lose the focus of todays session.

concept of saying "Thank you". of verbalizing the words. "Thank you". it falls under the category of praise. NOT gratitude.

---

### Grammatical Analysis

Today we're going to do a linguistic analysis of the words.  الحمد للہ. And there is a two fold purpose to that. The first is that by this analysis we will get to understand the true meaning of Hamd from the Quranic perspective. Because gratitude is a very subjective word. We all can have our own definitions of the word Hamd in our heads. What does Alhamdulilla mean?. Praise belongs to Allah. Gratitude belongs to Allah. Thank you Allah. You're awesome Allah. So there are various mental images of ⟪ar:الحمد للہ⟫. And so it becomes that we understand the only definition that actually counts. The only definition that matters. which is what the Quran consideres Hamd. The second purpose is that I want to show you the prefection. in the usage of this word. الحمد للہ. and I want us all to understand. why NO other words could have been used in its place.

As I said earlier. in Arabic. the word Hamd is a composite of two words. The first is ⟪ar:المدح⟫which mean praise. And the second is ⟪ar:الشکر⟫which means thanks or gratitude. So then why did Allah not say. ⟪ar:المدح و الشکر للہ رب العلمین⟫. Praise and gratitude belongs to Allah.

Lets begin by understanding the difference between the two words.

You're walking down the street and you see a beautiful car. What you do?. Do you thank it? Or do you praise it?. Hopefully you don't thank it! Hopefully you don't walk up to the car patt it on the hood and say thank you so much BMW. The normal thing to do. would be to praise it . It's a beautiful car! You praise it!. If you go to somebody's house who just had a baby. Do you thank the baby?. Or do you praise the baby?. You praise it!. Oh  what a cute baby! Such a beautiful baby. You don't thank a baby!.

Thanks is something entirely different. Thanks is only done when someone does something for you. If somebody lends you money. you say shukran. If somebody gives you something. if somebody donates to your cause. When somebody helps you with your effort. shows you a kindness. In other words DOES something FOR you. You say thank you. And if you don't say it. you show the person thanks. Because shukar can also be shown. It does not always have to be verbal. And that's why Allah says.
⟪ar-quote:ٱعْمَلُوٓا۟ آلَ دَاوُۥدَ شُكْرًۭا⟫

Show me through your actions that you are grateful. So Shukr or gratitude has to be in return for something nice. something beneficial done for you. Whereas when you see something impressive. When you see something beautiful . When you see something that intrigues you and interests you. you will praise it!

Also understand this distinction. that someone you thank. is not necessarily someone you priase. Now generally in coversation. these two ARE used together. I can say. Thank you so much for doing this for me. you're SO amazing!. In this case I thanked and praised together. But then it is also possible that I can thank someone. but not priase them. Let's think about that for a second. How do you thank someone without actually praising them. Let's look at an example or two from the Quran. You know Moosa AS was raised in a pretty interesting home. Where was he raised?. What was his address?. You know he had a pretty famous address. He is adopted and raised by Firon. Now years later when Moosa AS returns to him and delivers the message of Allah to him. Firon basically says. how dare you? How dare you talk to me this way?
⟪ar-quote:قَالَ أَلَمْ نُرَبِّكَ فِينَا وَلِيدًۭا . وَلَبِثْتَ فِينَا مِنْ عُمُرِكَ سِنِينَ⟫

Did we not raise you as a newborn in this house? Did you not spend many years of your life here? How dare you talk to me like that?. In other words what is Firon saying?. Aren't you what?. Aren't you grateful?. And then Moosa responds.
⟪ar-quote:وَتِلْكَ نِعْمَةٌۭ تَمُنُّهَا عَلَىَّ⟫

That is the favor. you did in fact do for me. Thanks!. That is Moosa AS's way of expressing gratitude. So even though Firon is a guy who will NEVER be praised. The guy will never be praised. especially not by a prophet. But when he does a favor, he will still be what?.  Thanked! Thanks can exist without praise.

Quran  talks about the rights of parents. And Allah says about parents.

أَنِ ٱشْكُرْ لِى وَلِوَلِدَيْكَ إِلَىَّ ٱلْمَصِيرُ

Be grateful to me and both of your parents!

وَإِن جَهَدَاكَ عَلَىٰٓ أَن تُشْرِكَ بِى مَا لَيْسَ لَكَ بِهِۦ عِلْمٌۭ

If your parents are struggling against you. If they are the ones telling you to disbelieve. to commit shirk. Don't obey them. But you still have to be what?. the verse began by saying . but you still have to be grateful to them. In other words if your parents are doing shirk.  Will you praise them? No! You will not praise them. But you still have to be what? You still have to be grateful to them!
Think about Abraham AS. He does not praise what his father does. But he is still thankful to him isn't he?

So the first thing I want you to understand. is that words. ⟪ar:الشکر و المدح⟫. praise and gratitude. are two different things. and they are mututally exclusive. Sometimes you can have praise without thanks. And then there are times where you can be grateful to someone. but not praise them. But the word ⟪ar:حمد⟫necessarily means both things together!. When Allah says. الحمد للہ. He is saying praise is for Allah. And he is ALSO saying gratitude is for Allah. And he is not just saying one or the other. He is saying that they BOTH exist together.

### مدح

Now what if the ayah read. ⟪ar:المدح للہ رب العالمین⟫ . All praise is for Allah. What would be the problem with that?. The problem with that is. that ⟪ar:المدح⟫ is praise. that is not always genuine. Praise can be insincere. Let's say you come home with a really bad report card. You walk home and as soon as you enter the house you say.  Mom! OMG. Your cooking smells so delicious.   And she hasn't even started cooking yet. So you're praising her but it's not genuine. You get it?. Praise could be fake. There is fake praise done for kings. for bosses. for judges.  It is done all the time!. People praise physical appearances. You look so beautiful!. That's a false praise. Because you are not worthy of that praise. because YOU did not make you look beautiful. ALLAH made you look beautiful by giving you these features. That's why in Arabic when you praise someone's look. you don't say Hamida. You would say. Madaha. Because it's a false praise. Even though. the time and energy some some women put into makeup. There is this lady in my office. she puts on SO MUCH makeup. So much powder. I always imagine that if I went over and slapped her. there would be like a cloud of powder all around her. LOL

So Madah can be false praise. it can be insincere praise. But Hamd cannot be a false praise. it cannot be insincere. why?. Because Hamd. generates in the heart. by the awareness of the magnificence.  and the glory of the one being praised.  I'll say that again. Hamd. the praise element of hamd. it occurs when the heart becomes aware of the magnificence. and the glory of the one being praised. It is done because of the the knowledge one acquires. about the glory. the brilliance. the greatness of the one that is being praised. It can therefore never be false. Once I gain the knowledge of gravity and exeperience it. I then can never lie about gravity. because I have now witnessed it as a fact. and therefore I do not have a choice but to declare it. Its the realization that if I say gravity does not exist. it does not affect the law of gravity in any way shape or form. gravity will still exist. Only I will get hurt by ignoring and rejecting the principles of gravity. Therefore my statement about gravity can now never be false.

It's the same with Hamd for Allah. He is worthy of praise by the knowledge of who he is through his 99 attributes. Not because you and I are praising him. He is worth of praise. even if there is absolutely no one praising him. He is not dependent on our praise. We are dependent on praising him. He does not need our praise. He does not need our hamd. it is our need that we praise him. the more knowledge we gain about him. about his being. about his 99 attributes. we are forced to turn to him with Hamd. He does not need our hamd at all.

. When you praise somebody and you do not really mean it for example you are praising in order to get something in return that is Madah. Hamd means that O Allah you are worthy of every single ultimate praise because of who you are. Not because of what you have given me. Even if you had not given me anything. Even if I did not exist you would be worthy of being praised . You would be worthy of my Hamd. Not because of what you have done for me but because of who you are.

Or sometimes praise is done just to impress somebody. but you don't necessarily mean it. For example when I go to a job interview and it goes terrible. It was the worst interview I ever had. I absolutely hated the guys that interviewed me. But even then when I am leaving. I say. It was nice meething you. It was not nice meeting him. but I still say that. It's fake praise you understand? So when the word ⟪ar:مدح⟫is used. it could be fake. it has the possiblity to be insincere. and that word in itself makes it appropriate for Allah. But HAMD. hamd cannot be insincere. Linquistically the word Hamd can only be used for genuine praise.

Now let's think about ⟪ar:شکر⟫. If Allah said ⟪ar:الشکر للہ رب العلمین⟫. Which means thanks or gratitude is for Allah. What's the problem with that?. Thanks is ONLY done when you are acknowledging a favor. Something was done for you. and you realize and appreciate that something was done for you. and then you finally thank the one who did the favor for you. You had a flat tire. Somebody came and helped you out. You say thank you! Thanks can only happen when you have a REASON to thank. In other words gratitude is a reaction. Is that clear to everybody?. Thank you is ALWAYS a reaction. Thank you is not something you start with. Ever! . You don't meet somebody just passing by and you say. hey you! thanks!! . You never do that.

When Allah uses the word Hamd. linguistically. this word combines both praise and thanks with certain rules. And the rules are. that praise HAS to be genuine. it can NEVER be fake. it cannot be manufactured. And secondly. gratitude is not reactionary. Therefore linquistically. saying ⟪ar:الحمد للہ⟫. is more powerful than saying ⟪ar:المدح للہ⟫ and it is more powerful than saying ⟪ar:الشکر للہ⟫. It is more comprehensive than both of them. Allah chose something to say. that is better than both of them combined. subhanAllah

Now here's another thing. . In English so far how many words did I have to use to replace the word Hamd. I had to use two words. I had to use gratitude and I had  to use praise . But how many words did Allah use? One! So here we are learning about a complication that occurs when we start translating the Quran. Allah uses one word, but to get the idea across we need to use a couple of words . But what if Allah himself used both words . What if Allah said  المدح و الشکر للہ رب العلمین . Praise and gratitude belongs to Allah . If Allah had done that would it have been the same? Actually NO! It would not have been the same because of a beautiful principle of the Arabic language . And it is actually a principle of all languages . They say in Arabic:

خیر الکلام ما قل و دل

which means.  the best kinds of speech is that . which uses very few words, but still gets the point across completely . When you use fewer words and get your point across .  that is eloquence . Now some of us MashaAllah have friends that talk to us for 30 minutes . But they still haven't made a point yet .  They say a lot . But they don't actually say anything . And you're hoping they still get to the point. hopefully before Christmas . Some people use too many words to even describe the simplest of things . The best kind of speech.  is one that is brief . that's easier on the tongue . that gets the point across . So alhamd, from an eloquence standpoint, is better than saying المدح و الشکر للہ

Another reason for not saying.⟪ar:المدح و الشکر للہ رب العلمین⟫ . is that in classical Arabic. when you put the word AND  in between two things. which is the letter ⟪ar:و⟫. it separates both words even in meaning. When I say  ⟪ar:المدح و الشکر للہ⟫. linguistically what I'm saying. is that praise belongs to Allah for some things. and gratitude belongs to Allah for other things. They're not always combined. Because the words aren't combined. This is a cool feature of Arabic language. You don't say what you don't mean. So if we use the two words gratitude and praise and combined them with an AND. in classical Arabic that means. that sometimes I am in the mood to praise him. but not thank them . And then there are other times when I'm in the mood to thank him. but not praise him. But when Allah says AlHamdulillah. that means for every act he does. for every blessing he gives. genuine praise. and unconditional gratitude is for Allah. BOTH at the same time. You don't get to pick and choose which one.

So now if you own a nice car. and you say AlHamdulillah. What have you just done?.  You genuinely praised Allah for giving human beings the ability to create cars. to design cars. manufacture it. AND you thank Allah for letting you own one. So you are praising and thanking Allah both at the same time. Thats all captured in this beautiful word. HAMD.  And this is why. AlHamdulillah  is the attitude of a true Muslim. Because AlHamdulillah is optimistic in nature.  You know sometimes you're going through a difficult time. and somebody comes and asks you. How are you doing and you just say. Oh you know. life sucks. but Alhamdulillah. You're not really praising him or thanking him when you say it that way. AlHamdulillah  is not something we just say. or throw around. It's a reminder for an attitude!. Allah is not interested in what comes out of our tongues. He's more interested in what comes out of our tongues.  that is also connected to our hearts. So we have to mean what we say. when we say AlHamdulillah.

If I'm going through a difficult time. someone asks me. How is it going?. AlHamdulillah!!. I'm grateful to Allah because whatever I'm going through. because it could always have been worse. Someone right now in the world is going through a much harsher version of what I'm going through. I'm grateful to Allah that he is linient with me. and AlHamdulillah. I praise him. because it is only He who can and will get me out of my situation. So a sincere AlHamdulillah. is an optimistic attitude towards Allah. This may seem a bit contradictory right now. but InshaAllah it will become a lot more clear when we talk about trials and tribulations. whether they are a curse or a blessing.

---

Now let's look at this phrase. ⟪ar:الحمد للہ⟫. grammatically. In the arabic language you can use nouns and you can use verbs. Between nouns and verbs. which has tenses? You know present tense, future tense, past tense?. Verbs have a tense. Nouns do not have a tense. There's no past tense noun or present tense noun or future tense noun. right?. Now when I say. I praise Allah. Did I use a noun or a verb?. I used a verb. What tenses is it?.  It's the present tense. 

But when I say praise belongs to Allah. Is the word praise a noun or a verb?.  It is now a noun. Allah could have used a verb. He could've said.  ⟪ar:احمدُ اللہ⟫. I praise Allah. He could've said ⟪ar:نحمد اللہ⟫ .  WE praise Allah. But Allah did not use a verb. He used a noun. Why?. Now here is what makes this so beautiful. When I use a verb. obviously there is going to be a tense associated with it. and when I use a present tense to say. I praise Allah. then I am only talking about the present. I said nothing about the past. and I said nothing about the future. If I use the past tense. then I am not guaranteeing anything about the future or the present. Because a tense has to be one or the other. A verb is limited. It is temporary. But Allah used a noun. And nouns are what?.  They are permanent. Allah's genuine praise and unconditional gratitude. is described with permanence. You know what that means?. It means I may be praising Allah now. but the praise of Allah has always been there. And I am not going to be here in this world forever. but the praise and gratitude of Allah will always be there forever. His praise and gratitude are not dependent on me. A huge reality within Alhamdulillah. is that the praise and gratitude of Allah is permanent. and it is not dependent on me. it's not because of me!.

See when we use the verb. somebody needs to DO the verb. It's called the subject. or the ⟪ar:فاعل⟫in Arabic. There has to be a doer. You cant just go into a conversation and say. Failed the test!. Who failed the test?. You cant just say. Disappeared!. What disappeared?.  Oh my book disappeared. You see?. When you use a verb you need somebody to do it. You need a subject. You cannot just have a verb all by itself. It doesn't make sense. It creates confusion. But a noun doesn't need someone to do it. A noun does not need a subject. A noun is independent by itself. An apple is an apple. it can exist all by itself. independent of any doer. So when Allah used the word AlHamd. He made it a noun. he made it independent. He doesn't need anyone to do the actual praise. and he doesn't need anyone to be grateful. Had he used a verb. that would have meant. that he needed someone to praise him. and he needed someone to be grateful to him.

Even if Allah said everything and everyone praises and is grateful to Allah. that too would have been limited. Why?. Because everything and everyone implies everyone and everything that exists NOW. in the present. It excludes everything and everyone in the past or the future. And that is why Allah used a noun for his praise and gratitude. He used the word Hamd as a noun. so that it is not confined in time and space. Because Allah does not need his creation to praise him and be grateful to Him. Even if there was not a single creation in this world. the Hamd of Allah would always still be there. his praise and gratitude does not require a doer. SubhanAllah!. All of this captured in just one word.

Now what if Allah said. ⟪ar:أِحمد اللہ رب العلمین⟫. What if he used a command. Praise Allah! The master of Alameen. Wouldn't that have been better?. I mean after all he is master. so a command could make sense. So why didn't he make it a command. I'll give you an example to help you understand. I tell my daughter Erum to bring me a glass of water. I say. Hey Erum! bring me a glass of water!.  I'm giving her a command. Once she hears me. she has two possible choices. She can either bring me the glass of water. OR. she can bring me the glass of water. Hahaha. Those are the only two clear choices as far as she's concerned.

Now if Allah said to praise him as a command. What are the two things that could happen?.  Some would praise him. Some would obey his command. And then there would be others who would disobey him. When you tell someone to do something. the ball is in their court . It depends on them . Maybe they'll choose to do it . Maybe they won't. Allah did not talk about praise and gratitude in a way that depends on us. He did not put the ball in our court. He said whether you do it or not. Whether you are grateful to me or not. Whether you praise me are not . My praise and gratitude is always still there. My Hamd is still there. It has been there forever. and it WILL be there forever. Human beings will come and go. nations will come and go. Generations will come and go. THIS WORLD will come and go. But the Hamd of Allah will always be there. It is a matter of fact . SubhanAllah!

Now what if Allah said. ⟪ar:انَّا الحمد للہ رب العلمین⟫. ⟪ar:C⟫ertainly. For sure. No doubt about it. ABSOLUTELY. Hamd is for Allah. Now what sounds more powerful?. Is All praise and gratitude belongs to Allah more powerful. Or is it saying. Definitely. Certainly. Absolutely Hamd is for Allah. Obviously the latter one?. So how come Allah didn't say.⟪ar:انَّا الحمد للہ رب العلمین⟫. A Khateeb uses it all the time. I say it in the beginning of sessions all the time to glorify Allah.

انا الحمد للہ نحمدہ و نستعینہ و نستغفر بہ ن. . So how come Allah didn't say it?

If you remember our sessions on the miracle of Quran. on the topic of conversation. I told you there are two kinds of communications. A communication can either be informative or it can emotional. ⟪ar:جملۃ انشائیۃ  and جملۃ خبریۃ⟫ . Either you have speech that is expressing your feelings and emotions. or you have speech that is communicating information. These are the two kinds of speech that human beings are capable of. That's it. Let's look at an example. Right now. when I'm teaching you about Hamd. am I delivering information. or am I expressing my emotions?. I am giving you information. This is informative speech. But when I'm talking to my friend. And I'm telling my friend how I feel about someone or something. what kind of communication is that?. That is an emotional conversation. So those are the only two types of speech we as human beings are capable of.

The thing is. that in Arabic linguistics. when you use Inna. the statement can ONLY be informative. It can only be factual. It can NEVER be emotional.

But if you don't use Inna. the communication can now be informative and it can also be emotional. By not using Inna. Allah made his Hamd. a statement such that we can use to talk about Allah's praise and gratitude with others. to give them information about it. But he also made it a statement to express our own emotion. SubhanAllah!.  The beauty of it is that it can now be used to communicate the emotions of our heart. as well as a message that we want to give to somebody else. Right now by saying. ⟪ar:الحمد للہ رب العلمین.⟫I'm giving you information about Allah's hamd. A few hours later. when I use the same word.⟪ar:الحمد للہ رب العلمین.⟫ I will be expressing my gratitude and my praise to Allah.

. We can now do both . If Innal Hamda was used . technically it could not have been used to express emotion . It would only have been meant to talk to somebody else . It would only remain for the intellect . And not for the heart . So Allah said Alhamdulilallhi rab Alameen. So that it could be used for the heart as well as for the intellect! SubhanAllah

And the same phrase could be used for both emotional as well as informational conversations .  For example right now I am telling you about AlHamdulillah. And this conversation is informational . Now as I'm speaking. I get thirsty. I take a sip of water . And then I say AlHamdulillah!. What was it this time? It was emotional. I actually expressed gratitude and praised Allah. It's the exact same phrase. AlHamdulillah . But when I'm telling you about it, it is informational. but when I'm expressing it for myself. It is emotional .  So the same phrase AlHamdulilah can be used as information . And it can also be used as emotion .

I'll say two sentences. you tell me which one sounds normal. 

I ate lunch. Lunch I ate. which one sounds normal to you?

they went to school. to school they went. which one sounds normal? But if I say to school they went. do you still understand me? OK so one is normal. and one is strange. but they're both understandable.  I'm not telling you this to explain how YODA speaks in star wars. Strong the force is! or whatever.

In the arabic language sometimes the sequence of a sentence is changed. and it is made strange.

No we find in the Quran . a different variation. Allah says.

فَلِلَّهِ ٱلْحَمْدُ رَبِّ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَرَبِّ ٱلْأَرْضِ رَبِّ ٱلْعَلَمِينَ ‎

He starts the ayah with وللہ الحمد . but fateha begins. الحمد للہ . They are the same words. but they have been put in a different order. So now whats the difference between the two? Because Allah could have said.

فَلِلَّهِ ٱلْحَمْدُ رَبِّ رب العلمین

For Allah belongs all priase who is the master of the worlds. what's the difference?

You know in Arabic. when you mess up the sequence. You know what that mean? So instead of saying "I ate lunch" .  If I said.  "Lunch I ate". what I'm actually saying is that I did not eat anything else. I only ate lunch. but ancient arabs did not have to use the word ONLY. they would just change the sequence of words. .and the exclusivity clause would automatically apply. it would automatically communicate the word ONLy. If I say. they went to school. it's normal. but if I say. to school they went. in the arabic sense.  that means they ONLY went to school and no where else. they did not go to the movie theatre. they did not go shopping. they did not go to work. they ONLY went to school. no place else. You understand? So it adds the word ONLY to the meaning. when you change the sequence of words.

Imagine you're teaching a class. and two students are talking in the back. zainab and fatima. and i can tell you one thing about girls. cause I have one of those. BOY They can talk!! So the teacher is teaching and these girls are yapping in the back. and the teach goes. Zainab!!! and she syas. I wasn't the ONLY one. now when she says. I wasn't the only one. what is she actually saying? If I am going to the principals office. Faitma better come with me! But she didn't have to use the other sentence. she just used one word strategically. ONLY! so if you use the word only strategiclaly. then you can actually be saying 2 things by saying just 1 thing. thats the cool thing about saying the word only.

So if I say. you are not the ONLY people I am teaching. I dind't say more. but you get the message. there must be others I am teaching as well.

Now allah says sometime.s.

فَلِلَّهِ ٱلْحَمْدُ

Hamd ONLY belongs to Allah. fill in the rest. what is implied? Hamd only belongs to Allah. no one else! It doesn't belong to anyone else. full stop. when you are saying ONLY you are saying Hamd ONLY belongs to Allah and nobody else.

 In Surah AlJasiay. in the second last ayah. Allah says

فَلِلَّهِ ٱلْحَمْدُ رَبِّ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَرَبِّ ٱلْأَرْضِ رَبِّ ٱلْعَلَمِينَ ‎

And in this entire surah. Allah is talking to mushrikeen. the people who commit shirk. who praise and are grateful to other than Allah. so Allah reverses the sequence of words and say. Hey! Hamd ONLY belongs to Allah and nobody else!.

But when you and I speak. we don't say. وللہ الحمد. we just say الحمد للہ . because we don't have that confusion! we don't have that confusion.we don't talk to a Muslim and say. Hey! Hamd only belongs to Allah!!!! NO. we just say AlHamdulillah. because the guy knows that Hamd ONLY belongs to Allah. so there is no need for a debate. no need to use that tone.

40:50

للہ الحمد  is the tone of a debate. it is tone of an agrument. it is a tone of anger.

When Allah introduced himself to us with Surah AlFateha. he did not want to make it a debate. he didn't want to make it an argument. he didn't want to yell at us. he spoke to us in a tone that indicates. that AlHamdulillah. All praise belongs to Allah. is not a debate. it is not an argument. it is something you already know in your hearts. so there is no reason for me to say. lillahil Hamd. . So allah said what instead?  AlHamdulillah. You know what that is teaching us? AlHamdulillah is already in my heart. The disbeliever lost it. the polythiest lost it. he had to be given it again. He had to be argued with. he had to be debated with. he had to be convinced of this. thats why he had to be told.  فَلِلَّهِ ٱلْحَمْدُ

So you see . Every phrase in the Quran. Starting with AlHamdulillah . is so perfect in the way Allah says it . That no matter what variation you try to come up with . You try to use a verb . You use Inna. You try to change it into a command . you use alternate words like Shukar and Madah . You don't get what Allah actually communicated . You don't get what Allah himself said . And the perfection of what He said is lost . SubhanAllah!

Allah has atleast 99 names. Allah did not say. الحمد للمالک، الحمد للقھار، الحمد للوھاب، الحمد للغفور. all of those would have been correct. all of those are correct. none of them are wrong. Fateha is Allah. introducing himself to us. when you introduce someone you use your name.

الحمد لی رب العلمین

Hamd belongs to Rabb Alalameen. could it be possible that they have a different concept of Rabb Alalmeen. Praise the lord. to a christian could mean something else. it could mean something else to a jew. but Praise Allah. the lord of alameen. leaves no room for confusion.  This actually happened.

Which prophet was supposed to face off against magicians? Moosa AS! Moosa AS faces off against magicians. they throw their ropes and their rods . he throws his staff . it swallows everything they coame up with . what happens to the magicians?what do they do?  they fell into sajda. Firon is standing on stage. and the magicians are in sajda. and he's confused. what's going on? Are you guys getting ready for round 2?? Or is this part of the act? what's going on?

so the magicians stand up from sajda and they say.

قَالُوٓا۟ آمَنَّا بِرَبِّ ٱلْعَلَمِينَ

We believe in the master of the worlds.  Firon is still confused. why? Why is he confused? Because what had Firon declared? أنا ربکم الاعلی . I am your greatest master. He had declared himself as Rabb. and the magicians are saying.  قَالُوٓا۟ آمَنَّا بِرَبِّ ٱلْعَلَمِينَ .We believe in the maser of the worlds.

So Firon is confused. because he believes he is the Rabb they are prostrating to.  He's like . AAAANNNNDDDD?? GOOO ONNNN???  And they say. No you idiot!

رَبِّ مُوسَىٰ وَهَرُونَ

the rabb of Moosa and Haroon. the master of moosa and haroon. they had to clarify. because if they had just said rabb alameen. they would have had no problems with that. you understand?. So the word Allah is critical.

But there is something else too. which is so beautiful. when I look at a painting and I say that is beautiful. what am I praising them for? their art! I am praising his one particular skill.  When I thank a teacher . what do I thank him for? for teaching me something. Thanks is specific. it is for a particular favor that was done for me. Praise is also specific. you praise the beauty of a flower. because its beautiful. you praise the freshness of the air because of how you feel.

So if we said. الحمد للخالق . Hamd belongs to the creator. then the only thing we are thanking allah for is. creating. if we say الحمد للحکیم . praise and thanks belongs to the wise. then the only thing we are appreciating about Allah is what? His wisdom. How do I appreciate EVERY SINGLE thing about ALlah. without missing anything? The things I can think of. and the things I can't even think of. how do I include everything in one concise statement . so that I truly get to thank Allah in the way he truly deserves to be thanked. when praising Allah?

What did we study about the name Allah. when we say Allah. it combines what? It combines ALL of his attributres.  So when I say الحمد للہ . I am praising and I am grateful to him for EVERY single attribute that he possess . That is ONLY possible through the use of the word Allah.

Now this exercise I did with you guys. this exhaustive exercise. of just kind of exploring what AlHamdulillah is. and what are the alternatives? and how come the alternatives are not good enough? can you imagine? This exercise exists for the entire quran. word by word by word. And it gives you an apprecateion of the power of the Quran like nothing else. Understanding the Fateha. opens the doors to the rest of the Quran. why? Because that is what fateha means. an opening. when we under estimate the power of AlFateha. we are naturally going to underestimate the power of the rest of the Quran. When we begin to appreciate the beauty and the depth of the fatiha. it will MAKE us want to explore the rest of the Quran. That's why fateha means the "opening" or the "opener". because the more you reflect on it. the more it opens the rest of the doors. and if you don't reflect on it. the door remains closed. that's what we're trying to do today. that's why the fateha.

<!-- section 11 (id=5695, raw_sort=11): الحمد للہ رب العلمین -->

## Section 5695

### Hamd from Tafseer of Dr.

we have reached the verse الحمد للہ رب العٰلمین . This is one of the most profound and succinct verses in the entire Koran. The more you think about it, the more you will realize that they could not have been a better way to begin the word of Allah. In order to fully appreciate the meaning of this verse, we need to first understand what the word AlHamd means. All Hamd belongs to Allah the Rab Alalameen. What exactly does Hamd mean?  And in order to fully understand the word H, we need to compare the word H with other similar words.

Shukr (gratitude) is for Allah
لَىِٕن شَكَرْتُمْ لَأَزِيدَنَّكُمْ ۖ وَلَىِٕن كَفَرْتُمْ إِنَّ عَذَابِى لَشَدِيدٌۭ

A Shukr is ONLY done in response to a favor done unto you. 

Whereas Hamd is not in return for anything!

Now what is the difference between Hamd and Madah. Madah in Arabic also means praise. But Madah could be a false praise. But Hamd is never a false praise. And Madah could be a praise that is something beyond your control.

And the AL signifies that every single type of Hamd belongs to you. ALHAMDU not Hamdan lillahi . To to Allah belongs praise. NO! To Allah belongs ALL praise!! Which means every Hamd imaginable is for Allah. And the LAAM in Li-Allah means that all Hamd ONLY belongs to Allah and nobody else in the entire universe.

Nobody else in this world deserves Hamd unless Allah allows it for him them. All Hamd exclusively belongs to Allah and no one else other than Allah . This is why H amd is more specific than Shukr  . It is more precise and concise and narrow then Shukr . Because Hamd  can only be done by the tongue .  buut you cannot show Hamd through our actions . But we can show Shukr . And Hamd is not done in exchange for a favor . But Shukr is always done in exchange for a favor . Even in Urdu we have Shukriya. But when do you see Shukriay. Only when something is done for you . You do not just walk up to a person and for no reason tell them Shukriya. Because it is always in response to something good that was done for you . Or in response to something that was given to you . Whereas Hamd is not something you say because something was given to you . But because of the recognition of the perfection of the being or the entity that you are praising .

---

Rasul Allah SAS said. when something pleased him he would say

⟪ar-quote:الحمد للہ الذی بِنعمتِہِ تَتِمُّ الصّٰلحات⟫

Rasul Allah SAS said. when something pleased him he would say

⟪ar-quote:الحمد للہ علی کل حال⟫

All praise is due to Allah  no matter what the situation is.

What is the common phrase in both? AlHamdulillah. We do not praise AllahJust when Allah shows us something good. NO! Allah is worthy of HAMD  regardless of the situations of our life. Wallahi if we did not exist, Allah would be worthy of praise! Had he not even created us. Had he not created this magnificent universe, he would still be worthy of Hamd.

So no matter what situation we are in, no matter what conditions we are in, no matter what emotional states we are in, whether we are happy or we are sad or we are anxious or we are depressed. Allah is worthy of Hamd. That's what our prophet SAS demonstrated. When something good happens.

⟪ar-quote:الحمد للہ الذی بِنعمتِہِ تَتِمُّ الصّٰلحات⟫

When something bad happens.

⟪ar-quote:الحمد للہ علی کل حال⟫

In every situation, in every circumstance, a law is worthy of praise. There is never a opportunity in which we do not praise Allah. And how can that not be the case, when Allah himself says to him belongs Hamd from the very beginning till the very end, and to him belongs Hamd in the heavens and the earth. and The Angels praise him as the circle around his throne. And the people of Jannah. Are finishing every single conversation with Hamd. and our father Adam began his existence with Hamd. And the scales are filled with the Hamd of Allah SWT. on the day of judgment. So then how would it be possible to start this magnificent book of Allah with any other word other than Hamd.

Why did Allah choose the word Hamdulillah. Why did Allah begin in the third person?

If Allah had commanded us to praise him. A command is not as eloquent as a statement of fact. A command can be obeyed. but a command can also be disobeyed. Whereas a statement of fact applies at all times. Whether you choose to obey. or you choose to disobey . it does not change the fact that Allah is worthy of praise. A rule is a rule whether you follow it or not. And Allah AWJ is saying AlHamdulilAllah as a rule, without any exceptions.

Now if Allah had changed this to a verb. Nahmadulllah. We are praising Allah. That would still not have been eloquent. why? Because verb is always taking place at a specific time. When we say that we praise right now! That means we were not praising him a second ago. It means that we many necessarily be praising him after this moment. So using it as a verb. Nahmaullah . would have limited the praise of Allah in time. But the phrase AlHamdulillah means that whether you are praising are not, Hamd belongs to Allah. So if Allah  had used it as a verb , it would have been finite, it would have been temporary.  Secondly, we would be praising Allah according to our quality of praise. Whereas Allah's praise is higher than our quality and our capacity.

So a verb would limit Allah's praise to a particular time. we are praising you now. meaning we were not praising you a second ago. and secondly . we would be linking the praise to our quality. and our quality will always be what? Inferior. limited. deficient

So by saying AlHamdulillah we remove the limitations of time and quality. So AlHamd Is a statement of fact

The AL means ⟪ar:استغراق الجنس⟫ . EVERY SINGLE kind of sincere praise belongs to Allah. There is no praise, except that it belongs to Allah. Which means that nobody else is independently worthy of praise. Think about it! When somebody is praising you, he is not praising you except for a blessing that Allah has given you! He says Mashallah your face is so beautiful. Who gave you this face? Who gave you this beauty? Who gave you these features? It was Allah! Therefore even though you are being praised for something, that praise actually belongs to Allah . because he was the one who gave it to you in the first place!

If someone says you are so intelligent! Who gave you that intelligence? Allah gave you that intelligence! Therefore that praise too belongs to Allah! For every single thing that you and I believe, that we are worthy of praise for it, it is in fact Allah that gave us that quality, that feature, that capability, that capacity for which we are being praised. therefore it is Allah who is in reality worthy of the praise that is being given to me. That is why when somebody praises me I must say AlHamdulillah. I must turn the praise towards its rightful owner. That Oh ALlah All this praise belongs to you alone! And it is a reminder to the one praising me. that it is Allah that gave me what you are praising. I cannot accept it. I am not truly worthy of it. It is my master who is worthy of this blessing that you are seeing and acknowledging! So when somebody comes and praises you or they praise me. they are in reality indirectly praising Allah . because it is Allah who gave you and I this blessing.

Therefore when I say AlHamdulillah. I am acknowledging that nobody,  including myself,  is worthy of praise, except Allah. This is an unconditional statement of praise. . Every other praise in this world is a conditional praise. That is Allah has given you something that people are praising you for. This is what the two letters AL represent!

⟪ar-quote:وَإِن تَعُدُّوا۟ نِعْمَتَ ٱللَّهِ لَا تُحْصُوهَآ⟫

If you attempted to count the blessings of Allah. you would not be able to count them. Numbers would deceive you. they would abandon you. there is not a number that could encompass the blessings that Allah has bestowed upon you.

Imaging starting the day as a rock. and then after you say AlHamduillah for each item it activates.

Laam in the Li-Allah Indicates that this Hamd has exclusive rights reserved for Allah. No one other than the Allah worthy of praise. To Allah alone belongs every Hamd. AlHamdulillah. To Allah belongs every Hamd. And if we go back to what we discussed about the meaning of the name Allah. He is the one that is worthy of worship! So we can therefore translate Alhamdulillah as every single ultimate praise unconditionally belongs to the one being, the only entity that is worthy of being worshiped. That is actually the literal translation of the prhase AlHamdulillah. Every single, ultimate, and unconditional praise. It is exclusively owned by, it is exclusively attributed to the one entity that is worthy of being worshiped.AlHamdulillah.

**Rabb Alalameen.7:50**

Why should all praise be due to Allah? Why is it that Allah alone should be praised? It is because he is the master of the world's. because he is Rabb Alalameen. So out of all his 99 names, allah chose the name Rabb . Because Rabb - master is the most significant relationship between us and our Creator.

What does Rabb mean? It means the ultimate owner. The maalik. The one who controls.  this implies that he is the one who brought us into existence. Because ultimate ownership always belongs to the creator. I repeat. The ultimate ownership always belongs to the creator. If you think about it. You do not own anything completely. What ever you own today, was handed to you. And it will be handed to someone else after you. You have to buy your car. You have to purchase your house. Even if you meet something with your own hands, you needed to first purchase the raw materials to make it. You could not bring anything into existence by yourself. When we say Allah is the Rabb. And there is no one competing with the Rabb this means that Allah's ownership is unique and complete. He did not have to first get spare material to create anything. No ownership was transferred to him. Ownership always belongs to him. Has always belong to him. Will always belong to him. Which implies what? That he created from nothing! So when we use the word Rabb. We automatically imply that Allah is the creator who created from nothing. Because ultimate ownership, necessitates creation. Is that clear?

When we say Allah is the Rabb. When we say Allah is the ultimate owner, then this means that Allah AWJ created because ultimate ownership cannot be transferred. As opposed to our ownership that is always transferred. Anything that we do ownership is first transferred. Even if you discover something, for example if you discover a well. You cannot say I made this well. You have to discover it. Because you discovered it within something that Allah had created. He created the earth, he ran water beneath it. All you did was dig a hole to extract that water. You did not create the earth. You did not run the water beneath it. It was Allah who did all of that. Therefore even if you discover a well, the ultimate ownership still belongs with Allah.

Even if you go into a showroom and buy a car it is simply a transfer of titleship. Every ownership that we have is conditional. Only Allah's ownership is unconditional. And if Allah's ownership is unconditional, then this implies, this necessitates that Allah must have created from nothing and therefore he is the Rabb

The second meaning of Rabb, is the one who is obeyed. Rabb means the one that is obeyed. In Surah Yusuf when the prisoners are released, Yusuf says to the prisoners

⟪ar-quote:ٱذْكُرْنِى عِندَ رَبِّكَ⟫

Mention me to the God that you obey . the king. He called the king Rabb here because The meaning of the word Rabb is the one who is obeyed. So when we say Allah is Rabb Alamaeen. It implies that Allah is obeyed. Everything in the universe, everything in the universe is, in the multi-versus obey Allah's command

And the third meaning of the word Rabb  is the one who takes care of , the one who nourishes, the one who sustain. and from this meaning of the word Rabb we get the word Tarbiyah . What does Tarbiyah mean? To take care of! To noursih.

So when we say Allah is Rabb Alameen we are implying 3 things.

1. Allah is the unconditional owner

2. Allah is the one that is obeyed. Nothing happens in this world except through his command.

3. Allah is the one who is taking care of all his creation. And from that we get the word Tarbiyah. In other words, my existence cannot be sustained until my Rabb takes care of me. Without my Rabb. Without my master, I cannot exist. My Rabb has to give me tarbiyah . My physical spiritual and emotional Tarbiyah comes from my master.

Why is Allah worthy of praise? Because he is Rabb Alalameen. He is the one that is the owner, the one that is obeyed and the one who sustains and takes care of.

---

---

Our problem today is not that we are unappreciative or ungrateful people. The problem is that we are not acquiring this knowledge of the Quran. We are so busy acquiring the knowledge demanded by our academic or professional lives. that we've thrown the knowledge of Quran behind our backs. That's why we are unable to appreciate the blessings of Allah. Islam is a blessing. Emaan is a blessing. Quran is a blessing. the messenger of Allah  and Maulana Ali are blessings. Taharat. Salaah. Zakaat. Saum. Hajj. these are all blessings. but what's missing. is our knowledge. Our knowledge about these blessings is missing. And you also have to understand. that we will NEVER EVER be able to acquire complete knowledge. We will NEVER EVER be able to FULLY appreciate and be grateful for Allah's blessings. We will NEVER be able to do justice to Allah. it is simply not possible.

Rasul Allah (SAS) would wake up in the middle of the night. perform wudu.  pray 2 rakaat namaaz.  and then fall in Sajdah.  in prostration he would say.

سبحنک اللہ

how exalted you are o Allah

لا احصی ثَناءً علیک.  أنتَ کما أثنَیتَ علی نَفسِک

I cannot do justice in praising you!. Now just imagine this for a second. Who is saying this?. The best creation. among all of creations. EVER created!!!!.  The most noble. the most pious. the most knowledgeable creation of Allah.  And he is saying this. in his masjid. which is the second most holiest place on this earth. When? In the middle of the night. which is the best time of the night for worship. when nobody else is looking at him!.  I just want you to really visualize this. The one who worships Allah, with the perfection that is not possible by anyone else in the world. The BEST of the BEST of creations. in the best possible posture of worship. sajda. In the best masjid. during the BEST time of the night. What does he say?

لا احصی ثَناءً علیک! أنتَ کما أثنَیتَ علی نَفسِک

Oh Allah! I cannot praise you as you deserve to be praised!!!! . Even Rasul Allah SAS says. you are too great for me to praise.

أنتَ کما أثنَیتَ علی نَفسِک

Only you can praise yourself.  as you deserve to be praised

So we praise Allah. recognizing. that our praise falls short of what Allah deserves. We praise Allah realizing.  that only Allah can praise himself in a way that is suitable for him. With the majesty that Allah deserves. So the point is Allah is not asking us to appreciate him. and be grateful to him. at HIS level. He is asking us to appreciate him. and be grateful to him at our own levels.  SubhanAllah! What an amazing master. Take any other master of this world. is the work required to be at the level of the master?. or the level of the slave?. The level of the master. Slaves are whipped and tortured if they don't meet the standards of the master. But look at our master!. He demands nothing more than what WE are capable of. And he accepts our weak efforts with open arms.

One Moosa AS passed by a shepherd. sitting under the tree with his sheep. He was combing the fur of the sheep and he was saying. Ya Allah. Why don't you come to me too. I will comb your hair. I'll remove the lice from your hair. I'll feed you the finest grass of the land to eat. I'll give you the best milk to drink. right?. When Moosa AS hears this. he gets furious. He goes and stands before this shepherd and yells at him. What nonsense and rubbish are you speaking about Allah?. You think Allah is like your sheep?. How dare you even think about Allah that way. And the shepherd he asks Moosa. So is Allah not like my sheep?. Moosa AS gets even more angry. You compare Allah(Azza Wa Jal) to you sheep. If I ever hear you speak this way again. I will punish you severly. And the shepherd hearing this starts weeping.

That evening when Moosa AS climbs the mountain of Toor to meet Allah. Allah says to him. Moosa! What have you done!. You turned my beloved away from me!. No matter what he was saying. in whichever way he was remembering me. at least he was remembering me. at least he was appreciating me. Why did you turn him away from me Moosa. And then he commands Moosa to leave. and not return until that shepherd is happy with Allah again.  SubhanAllah!. What an amazing master!

My point is. we must try to excel. we must try to acquired more and more knowledge about our beautiful religion. About this amazing master. so that we can increase in our appreciation and gratitude towards him. We must increase in our salaah. in our fasts. in our Ibaadah. but don't underestimate the value of whatever you're doing right now. Don't ever think its not good enough. But we must strive for more. Look at what people will do for worldly rewards. That show. Who's going to be a millionaire. or any of these games shows that have money involved. People will go to all sorts of extremes to win. And in these game shows. you may. or may not win. These are designed for you to lose. Then how about a game which is designed for you to win. and where you have the CERTAINTY to win!.

But because of the recognition of the perfection of the being or the entity that you are praising .

Rasul Allah said.

الحمد للہ تملأُ المیزان

Saying AlHamdulillah fills the entire scale. on the day of judgment.  Simply saying AlHamdulillah fills the entire scale on the day of judgment . And our master has used this word Hamd so many times in the Koran . He used this word when he talked about creating the creation .

ٱلْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ ٱلَّذِى خَلَقَ ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضَ وَجَعَلَ ٱلظُّلُمَتِ وَٱلنُّورَ

All Hamd belongs to Allah who created the heavens and the earth . So Allah is praised at all times .

وَهُوَ ٱللَّهُ لَآ إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ۖ لَهُ ٱلْحَمْدُ فِى ٱلْأُولَىٰ وَٱلْآخِرَةِ

to Allah belongs Hamd from the very beginning of time. and to Allah belongs Hamd till the very end of time.

To Allah belongs praise wherever you and whenever you are

وَلَهُ ٱلْحَمْدُ فِى ٱلسَّمَوَتِ وَٱلْأَرْضِ وَعَشِيًّۭا وَحِينَ تُظْهِرُونَ

To him belongs constant Hamd. Those in the heavens praise Him. and those on the earth praise him. So wherever you are, when ever you are Hamd always belongs to Allah alone.

How do you and I begin our day? How often do we truly praise allah.

Baddoo ka salaam

قال اميرالمؤمنين عليه السلام. إنّ‌قوماً عبدوا الله رغبةً فتلك عبادة التّجار . وإنّ قوماً عبدوا الله رهْبةً فتلك عبادة العبيد . وإنّ قوْماً عبدوا الله شُكراً فتلك عبادة الأحرار

Imam Ali --peace be upon him-- has stated: [Among those who worship Allah] one group worships Allah in hope [of profit], such is the worship of traders; and another group worships Allah out of fear [from His Wrath], such is the worship of slaves; and yet another group of people worships Allah out of gratitude, such is the worship of free noble men. [Nahj al-Balaghah, short saying #237]

According to a hadith, Allah said He was a hidden treasure and He wanted to be known. As a result, He created the universe.

The final servant created in the creation stage of the universe was man. As a matter of fact, creation of man was the purpose of creation of the universe. This is because man was the only servant that was capable of being His khalifa. According to another hadith, this khalifa was created in His form. Thus represented His authority over all things. There had been no creature before him that was capable of knowing all known Divine Names on its own.

Allah wants us to get closer to Him and know Himself better. As long as we lack knowledge (regarding the manifestation of His names), we won't accomplish this and stay as animal-humans. This is why Sufis add nafilahs to the obligatory religious practices. And most importantly, they aim to learn more and more of Him everyday.

Sufis realized we are not only created to serve Him, but all our actions serve Him on its own. That means we are servants not because Allah wanted us to be, but we are servants because indeed we are. The universe as we call it is where His names manifest themselves and all consciousness is synced to Him. And thus as the hadith says: "He who knows himself, knows His Lord."

Now let's return to the example of khala's cooking. Let's say instead of appreciating her food. instead of showing gratitude. I take a bite from that raan. and I spit it out. I say. who cares if you cooked this raan for me. You didn't do me any favor. You were going to cook dinner anyway. I didn't ask you to do all this for me. Don't think you're going to get any praise or gratitude out of me. How do I know you did this for me?. What if you did it for someone else.that guy didn't show up and you're just trying to get credit for it. Now how do you think khala will feel?. Does she have a right to be angry with me at this point?. Does she have a right to take away the food from in front of me?. Does she have a right to make me starve now?. ABSOLUTELY. Why?. Because I don't deserve it. You don't give gifts and blessings to people that don't deserve. Who are going to waste it. isn't that true?.

What is praise?. and when do we praise something?. Lets take the example of cars. Who are cars designed for?. Who benefits from cars. People. the consumers benefit from cars, right?. Sure the company makes money too. so in the financial sense they benefit too. But then they deserve that money. for the efforts they've made, right?. Nothing wrong with company getting what they deserve. But from a benefit standpoint. cars are designed to benefit people. The effort that is put into the design. into the construction of a car. is for people. Let's say I go to the BMW headoffice. and I meet the designer of the latest BMW model. that is about to be released. He takes me on a tour and show me this beautiful piece of machinery. and I say. WOW. THIS is freaking awesome!. What a look. what an amazing design. Such a beautiful interior. It looks so comfortable. This car is CRAZY AWESOME!!!.

Now the question is. Did the designer of the car NEED my praise?. Had I not said any of that. would that put a dent in his day?. Would he go back to his wife and cry on her shoulder. He didn't praise my car. NO!. Of course not!. He wouldn't care. His design is AWESOME whether I appreciate it or not. right?. But when I praised his work. do you think it made him happy?. Do you think he appreciated my praise?. He ABSOLUTELY did!. Why is that?. Let's think about why you and I feel happy when someome praises us.

And what did we just learn?. When are we compelled to praise??. When we gain knowledge about the one we are praising. In Jannah we will constantly be gain knowledge about Allah's loftiness. about his mercy. about his grace. about his 99 attributes. and with every bit and piece of knowlege we acquire. with every bit of awareness we gather. We will be compelled to praise him. We will be forced by our immense gratitude for the gift of His awareness. that we will have not choice but to praise him. willingly. out of our love for him.  and out of our awe of his glory and loftiness.

The blessings of allah are readily available. when it comes time to respond with gratitude. we delay our salaah

a dog leaves a bone and answers its masters call

Society is designed such that we want things instantly.

Recap

Hadees: Praise you as you have praised yourself

What is knowledge

Tie it with heart tongue and limbs

Salaah is knowledge in action

Now because salaah is an instrument. it too has operational knowledge. structural knowledge. and essential knowledge. But where do we have to begin?. We have to begin with operational knowledge. That's the first thing to learn. How does this THING work?. What are the prerequisites?. What are the Dos and Donts.

Which is not to say that you should not WANT to understand the structure. and the intent. YOU ABSOLUTELY should WANT TO. Because at the end of the day. salaah is just another instrument. And the BETTER you understand the internal structure and the INTENT in the design of that instrument. the BETTER you will be able to use it. So to be VERY clear. I am NOT saying that you should not want to study its structure and understand its intent. In fact you should absolutely WANT to. What I'm saying though is. it is not a requirement. for its operation. There is a difference. And I hope you understand that difference. This whole idea that I need to understand every single meaning behind every single action of salaah . only then I can do it. that is ABSOLUTELY not true. The only motivation you need for salaah. is HAMD. That's it. That's the reason why Rasul Allah prayed. That's the reason why Maulana Ali prayed. that's the reason why an Imam prays. why a Dai prays. why a mansoob prays. why the most ordinary believer like myself prays. HAMD. We're all unified in that purpose. From the higest rank to the lowest rank. We are all unified in our HAMD. The Imam with ALL of his TREMENDOUS knowledge. he prays the same number of rakaats. the same surah Fateha. the same tasbeeh in each action. the same tashhahud. as you and I do. We're all unified in action. we're all unif
